### [28] [SKILLC: Learning Autonomous Skill Internalization in LLM Agents via Contrastive Credit Assignment](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27899v1)
*Hongxiang Lin,Zhirui Kuai,Erpeng Xue,Lei Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 技能内化学习方法，对比信用分配，对agent技能获取与优化有重要启发。

TL;DR: SkillC通过对比技能信用分配将技能帮助度对比转化为直接学习信号，从而改进技能内化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有技能内化方法仅将技能帮助度对比用于课程控制，不修改策略更新，无法区分技能依赖与自主成功。

Method: SkillC采样配对的技能注入和无技能轨迹，使用双流优势估计器保留全局排名并对无技能成功施加单边修正，再通过平滑验证级信号驱动自适应课程。

Result: 在ALFWorld和WebShop上，SkillC分别超过最强技能内化基线5.5%和4.4%，且与技能增强方法竞争力相当。

Conclusion: SkillC有效内化技能，直接利用技能注入与无技能性能的对比，提升长时程任务中的探索和性能，无需运行时技能访问。

中文摘要：结构化技能提示改进了长时程自主强化学习（RL）中的探索。技能增强型RL方法在推理时保留外部技能，而技能内化型RL方法在训练过程中撤回技能以实现自主性能。然而，现有的内化方法仅使用技能帮助度对比进行课程控制，使得策略更新不变，无法区分技能依赖和自主成功。我们提出SkillC，一个基于对比技能信用分配（CSCA）的框架，将这种对比转化为内化的直接学习信号。SkillC在同一策略更新中，从活跃技能类型中为任务采样配对的技能注入和无技能轨迹，并通过双流优势估计器将任务级对比注入优化，该估计器保留全局排名同时对无技能成功施加单边修正。平滑的验证级信号进一步驱动关于归因强度、轨迹分配和单调活跃集剪枝的自适应课程。在ALFWorld和WebShop上的实验表明，在无运行时技能访问的情况下，SkillC分别超过最强的先前技能内化RL基线5.5%和4.4%，同时与技能增强型RL方法保持竞争力。

Original abstract: Structured skill prompts improve exploration in long-horizon agentic reinforcement learning (RL). Skill-augmented RL methods retain external skills at inference, while skill-internalization RL methods withdraw them during training to enable autonomous performance. However, existing internalization approaches only use skill-helpfulness contrast for curriculum control, leaving the policy update unchanged and unable to distinguish skill-dependent from autonomous success. We propose SkillC, a framework based on Contrastive Skill Credit Assignment (CSCA) that converts this contrast into a direct learning signal for internalization. \textsc{SkillC} samples paired skill-injected and skill-free rollouts for tasks from active skill types within the same policy update, and injects their task-level contrast into optimization via a dual-stream advantage estimator that preserves global ranking while applying a one-sided correction toward skill-free success. A smoothed validation-level signal further drives an adaptive curriculum over attribution strength, rollout allocation, and monotonic active-set pruning. Experiments on ALFWorld and WebShop show that, without runtime skill access, SkillC surpasses the strongest prior skill-internalization RL baseline by 5.5\% and 4.4\%, respectively, while remaining competitive with skill-augmented RL methods.

</details>


### [29] [Dr-CiK: A Testbed for Foresight-Driven Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27904v1)
*Yihong Tang,Andrew Robert Williams,Arjun Ashok,Vincent Zhihao Zheng,Lijun Sun,Alexandre Drouin,Issam H. Laradji,Étienne Marcotte,Valentina Zantedeschi*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 面向预测的agent benchmark，涉及上下文检索与评估框架，可迁移至代码优化agent。

TL;DR: 本文提出Dr-CiK基准，评估智能体检索和利用上下文进行时间序列预测的能力，发现现有方法检索证据不足且易被干扰，激励面向远见的智能体研究。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有上下文辅助预测基准通常假设支持性上下文已经提供，未测试智能体自行从嘈杂信息源发现上下文的能力。

Method: 引入Dr-CiK基准，要求智能体从文档语料库中检索与预测相关的支持性上下文，过滤干扰项，将检索到的上下文提炼为有用证据，并生成支持该证据的预测。

Result: 高质量上下文显著提升预测性能，但大多数现有深度研究（DR）智能体仅恢复<5%的真实支持性证据，>80%的引用包含干扰项，且使用检索到的上下文后预测性能反而下降。

Conclusion: 结果激励了面向远见的智能体的研究，即主动搜索正确上下文以预测未来。

中文摘要：在现实环境中的时间序列预测通常不仅依赖于历史观测，还依赖于必须从嘈杂、异构的信息源中主动发现的外部上下文。然而，现有的上下文辅助预测基准通常假设支持性上下文已经提供，未明确智能体是否能自行识别。因此，我们引入了Dr-CiK，一个用于评估智能体是否能从文档语料库中检索与预测相关的支持性上下文、过滤干扰项、将检索到的上下文提炼为对预测有用的证据，并生成由该证据支持的预测的基准。通过上下文消融实验以及对最先进的深度研究和预测方法配对评估，我们表明高质量上下文能显著提高Dr-CiK中的预测性能。然而，大多数现有的深度研究（DR）智能体仅能恢复一小部分真实支持性证据（通常<5%），频繁被干扰项误导（>80%的干扰项引用），并且可能导致预测模型在使用检索到的上下文时性能比没有上下文更差。我们的结果激励了对面向远见的智能体的研究，即搜索正确的上下文以预测未来。

Original abstract: Time series forecasting in real-world settings often depends not only on historical observations, but also on external context that must be actively discovered from noisy, heterogeneous information sources. Yet existing context-aided forecasting benchmarks typically assume that the supporting context is already provided, leaving open whether agents can identify it on their own. Therefore, we introduce Dr-CiK, a benchmark for evaluating whether agents can retrieve forecasting-relevant supporting context from a document corpus, filter out distractors, distill the retrieved context into forecast-useful evidence, and generate forecasts supported by that evidence. Through context ablations and evaluations of state-of-the-art deep research and forecasting methods paired together, we show that high-quality context substantially improves forecasting performance in Dr-CiK. However, most existing DR agents recover only a small fraction of the ground-truth supporting evidence (usually <5%), are frequently misled by distractors (>80% distractor citations), and can cause forecasters to perform worse with retrieved context than without context. Our results motivate research on foresight-driven agents that search for the right context to predict the future.

</details>


### [30] [Harness-Bench: Measuring Harness Effects across Models in Realistic Agent Workflows](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27922v1)
*Yilun Yao,Xinyu Tan,Chao-Hsuan Liu,Yaoming Li,Zhengyang Wang,Wenhan Yu,Zhewen Tan,Yuxuan Tian,Guangxiang Zhao,Lin Sun,Xiangzheng Zhang,Tong Yang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 直接研究agent workflow中harness影响，与agent评测强相关。

TL;DR: Harness-Bench是一个诊断性基准测试，用于评估LLM智能体系统中支架配置对执行效果的影响，发现模型-支架组合对性能有显著影响，并识别了执行对齐失败。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准测试忽略执行层面变化，难以研究支架（系统层）配置对LLM智能体性能的影响。

Method: 构建包含106个沙盒离线任务的Harness-Bench，在不同模型后端上评估代表性支架配置，记录完成产物、轨迹、统计数据和验证器输出。

Result: 在5,194条轨迹中，模型-支架配对在完成度、过程质量、效率和失败行为上存在显著差异，并发现执行对齐失败。

Conclusion: 智能体能力应按照模型-支架配置级别报告，Harness-Bench为诊断和改进智能体执行栈提供可复现基础。

中文摘要：LLM智能体越来越多地被部署为可执行系统，这些系统使用工具、修改工作空间并生成具体产物。在此类工作流中，性能不仅取决于基础模型，还取决于“支架”（harness）：即管理上下文、工具、状态、约束、权限、追踪和恢复的系统层。然而，现有基准测试通常抽象掉执行过程、比较完整的智能体系统，或固定支架不变，使得执行层面的变化难以研究。我们引入了Harness-Bench，一个用于评估现实智能体工作流中支架配置层面效果的诊断性基准测试。Harness-Bench在共享任务环境、预算和评估协议下，跨多个模型后端评估代表性支架配置，同时保留每个支架的原生执行行为。该基准测试包含106个沙盒离线任务，这些任务基于实际智能体使用模式构建，并经过人工审查以确保真实性、可解性、可验证性和完整性。每次运行记录最终产物、执行轨迹、使用统计数据和验证器输出，从而能够超越最终完成情况进行分析。在5,194条执行轨迹中，我们观察到不同模型-支架配对在完成度、过程质量、效率和失败行为上存在显著差异。这些结果表明，智能体能力应按照模型-支架配置级别报告，而非仅归因于基础模型。我们的分析进一步识别了反复出现的执行对齐失败，即看似合理的推理与工具反馈、工作空间状态、证据或可验证输出契约脱节。Harness-Bench为诊断和改进可靠、高效且可审计的智能体执行栈提供了可复现的基础。

Original abstract: LLM agents are increasingly deployed as executable systems that use tools, modify workspaces, and produce concrete artifacts. In such workflows, performance depends not only on the base model, but also on the harness: the system layer that manages context, tools, state, constraints, permissions, tracing, and recovery. However, existing benchmarks typically abstract away execution, compare complete agent systems, or hold the harness fixed, making execution-layer variation difficult to study. We introduce Harness-Bench, a diagnostic benchmark for evaluating configuration-level harness effects in realistic agent workflows. Harness-Bench evaluates representative harness configurations across multiple model backends under shared task environments, budgets, and evaluation protocols, while preserving each harness's native execution behavior. The benchmark contains 106 sandboxed offline tasks constructed from practical agent-use patterns and manually reviewed for realism, solvability, oracle-checkability, and integrity. Each run records final artifacts, execution traces, usage statistics, and validator outputs, enabling analysis beyond final completion. Across 5,194 execution trajectories, we observe substantial variation in completion, process quality, efficiency, and failure behavior across model-harness pairings. These results suggest that agent capability should be reported at the model-harness configuration level rather than attributed to the base model alone. Our analysis further identifies recurring execution-alignment failures, where plausible reasoning becomes decoupled from tool feedback, workspace state, evidence, or verifiable output contracts. Harness-Bench provides a reproducible foundation for diagnosing and improving reliable, efficient, and auditable agent execution stacks.

### [31] [Do Agents Think Deeper? A Mechanistic Investigation of Layer-Wise Dynamics in Sequential Planning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27935v1)
*Zhenyu Cui,Xiangzhong Luo*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 机械分析agent规划中的层动态，直接研究agent推理。

TL;DR: 本文通过分层分析，发现自主LLM代理在多轮任务中会动态增加深度使用，且存在构建-精炼差距，不同模型表现各异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究LLM在自主代理场景下是否仍像单轮任务中那样低效利用深度，以及深度使用如何随多轮推理而变化。

Method: 对三个领域（深度研究、代码生成、表格处理）的用户-代理完整轨迹进行分层分析，使用残差流探针、因果跳层干预和有效深度测量。

Result: 代理推理中模型逐步招募更多更深层，出现长距离层间依赖，残差更新转为修正主导；存在构建-精炼差距；不同模型（Qwen、Minimax、GLM）深度分配模式不同。

Conclusion: 自主LLM代理能根据推理复杂度自适应分配深度，其深度使用模式与静态任务有显著差异。

中文摘要：最近的机制研究表明，大型语言模型（LLM）在标准单轮任务中可能低效地利用其深度。这一情况在自主代理设置中是否仍然成立尚不清楚，在该设置中模型必须执行多轮规划、工具使用和迭代状态更新。我们通过系统性的分层分析来研究这一问题，涵盖三个领域（深度研究、代码生成和表格处理）的完整用户-代理轨迹。利用残差流探针、因果跳层干预和有效深度测量，我们表明代理推理展现出与静态任务不同的深度分布。随着轨迹展开，模型逐步吸引更多且更深的层，在后来的轮次中出现更强的长距离层间依赖。同时，残差更新变得越来越以修正为主导，表明从稳定的特征积累转向重复校准。有效深度分析进一步揭示出显著的构建-精炼差距：语义方向通常相对早期形成，而深层对于稳定最终输出仍然必要。在不同模型家族中，这一差距在Qwen和Minimax中尤为明显，而GLM显示出更具领域依赖性的深度分配模式。这些结果提供了机制证据，表明自主LLM代理随着推理复杂度增长而自适应地分配深度。

Original abstract: Recent mechanistic studies suggest that large language models (LLMs) may utilize their depth inefficiently in standard single-turn tasks. Whether this still holds in autonomous agent settings, where models must perform multi-turn planning, tool use, and iterative state updates, remains unclear. We study this question through a systematic layer-wise analysis of complete user-agent trajectories spanning three domains: Deep Research, Code Generation, and Tabular Processing. Using residual stream probes, causal layer-skipping interventions, and effective-depth measurements, we show that agentic reasoning exhibits a distinct depth profile from static tasks. As trajectories unfold, models progressively recruit more and deeper layers, with stronger long-range inter-layer dependencies emerging in later turns. At the same time, residual updates become increasingly correction-dominant, indicating a shift from stable feature accumulation toward repeated recalibration. Effective-depth analysis further reveals a substantial construction-refinement gap: semantic direction often forms relatively early, while deep layers remain necessary for stabilizing final outputs. Across model families, this gap is pronounced in Qwen and Minimax, whereas GLM shows a more domain-dependent depth allocation pattern. These results provide mechanistic evidence that autonomous LLM agents allocate depth adaptively as reasoning complexity grows.

### [32] [The Shape of Overthinking: Backtracking Bursts in Long Reasoning Traces](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27965v1)
*Navid Rezazadeh,Arash Gholami Davoodi*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 分析长推理轨迹中回溯爆发，对agent推理管理有借鉴。

TL;DR: 通过分析推理轨迹中的回溯动态，发现早期孤立修复与正确推理相关，而持续回聚类的不稳定则预示错误；提出基于爆发感知的早期退出策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 推理模型的长轨迹中有用的自我修正与无用的修订难以区分，需要一种方法来自动识别和分离它们。

Method: 在Qwen3-8B模型的AIME轨迹上标注回溯严重性，分析事件时序、深度和爆发结构，并设计基于爆发感知的过滤策略。

Result: 早期孤立修复常出现在正确轨迹中，而错误轨迹中回溯更严重、持久且聚类；爆发感知过滤在浅层和中间深度优于固定长度过滤。

Conclusion: 爆发感知控制提供了一种可部署的机制，用于将可恢复的修复与可能的不稳定性分开，但适中长度截断仍是强基线。

中文摘要：推理模型常常生成长轨迹，其中有用的自我修正与无效的修订很难区分。我们通过回溯动态来研究这一区别：长形式推理轨迹中的局部重新考虑、撤回或重新推导。在6,000条Qwen3-8B AIME轨迹上，我们标注了段落级别的回溯严重性，并分析了事件时序、归一化深度和局部爆发结构。我们发现，早期的孤立修复通常与正确推理兼容，而错误轨迹则更常表现出中等至严重的回溯，这些回溯持续存在并在后期聚集。跨语料库检查显示，在额外的模型/领域对上也存在相同的定性不对称。过滤分析将该信号实例化为一种前缀因果选择性早期退出策略：在浅层和中间深度，基于爆发感知的过滤在使用仅前缀可用特征时优于固定长度过滤。适中的长度截断仍然是强大的完整轨迹基线，但爆发感知控制提供了一种可部署的机制，用于区分可恢复的修复与可能的不稳定性。

Original abstract: Reasoning models often generate long traces in which useful self-correction and unproductive revision are hard to distinguish. We study this distinction through backtracking dynamics: local reconsideration, retraction, or re-derivation inside long-form reasoning traces. On 6{,}000 Qwen3-8B AIME traces, we annotate segment-level backtrack severity and analyze event timing, normalized depth, and local burst structure. We find that early isolated repair is often compatible with correct reasoning, whereas incorrect traces more often show moderate-to-severe backtracks that persist and cluster late. Cross-corpus checks show the same qualitative asymmetry across additional model/domain pairs. Filtering analyses instantiate the signal as a prefix-causal selective early-exit policy: at shallow and intermediate depths, burst-aware filtering outperforms fixed length-based filtering while using only prefix-available features. Moderate length cutoffs remain strong completed-trace baselines, but burst-aware control provides a deployable mechanism for separating recoverable repair from likely instability.

### [33] [STAB: Specification-driven Testing for Algorithmic Bottlenecks](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27981v1)
*Soohan Lim,Joonghyuk Hahn,Hyundong Jin,Yo-Sub Han*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 直接针对算法代码效率瓶颈生成测试，与自动代码优化强相关。

TL;DR: STAB通过自然语言规范生成暴露算法瓶颈的测试用例，结合约束饱和与对抗性场景注入，显著提升测试用例对最坏情况的覆盖率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有效率测试用例生成方法未考虑驱动算法最坏情况的输入结构条件，导致无法充分暴露瓶颈。

Method: STAB采用两阶段流水线：约束饱和器（规则+CP-SAT）解析边界，对抗性场景注入器（关键词+KNN）检索构造原则，合并后由LLM生成测试用例生成器。

Result: 在CodeContests上，开源LLM的瓶颈暴露率从50.43%升至73.45%，闭源LLM从57.45%升至71.85%，跨语言一致提升。

Conclusion: STAB有效利用规范信息生成高质量效率测试用例，优于仅基于输入尺寸或代码实现的方法。

中文摘要：评估算法代码的效率需要能够暴露运行时瓶颈的测试用例。先前的方法要么通过增加输入规模，要么通过生成代码特定的输入来使给定实现运行缓慢，从而生成效率测试用例。因此，它们没有解决驱动算法最坏情况的输入结构条件。我们引入了STAB，一个规范驱动的流水线，它仅从自然语言问题规范生成暴露算法瓶颈的测试用例。STAB将任务分为约束边界最大化和对抗性结构注入两个部分。(i) 约束饱和器提取约束，并通过基于规则的饱和和CP-SAT优化在相关变量上解析大的可接受尺寸分配。(ii) 对抗性场景注入器使用关键词匹配和K近邻（KNN）从策划的场景目录中检索实现级别的对抗性构造原则。STAB将问题规范、解析的边界和检索到的构造原则编码到结构化生成规范中，LLM从中合成Python测试用例生成器。在CodeContests上，STAB将在开源LLM中平均生成的暴露算法瓶颈的测试用例比率从50.43%提高到73.45%，在闭源LLM中平均从57.45%提高到71.85%，并且在Python、Java和C++上均有一致的提升。我们的代码可在https://github.com/suhanmen/STAB获取。

Original abstract: Evaluating the efficiency of algorithmic code requires test cases that expose runtime bottlenecks. Previous methods generate efficiency test cases either by increasing input size or by generating code-specific inputs that make the given implementation run slowly. Consequently, they do not address the structural input conditions that drive the algorithmic worst case. We introduce STAB, a specification-driven pipeline that generates test cases that expose algorithmic bottlenecks from a natural-language problem specification alone. STAB separates the task into constraint-bound maximization and adversarial structure injection. (i) The constraint saturator extracts constraints and resolves large admissible size assignments using rule-based saturation and CP-SAT optimization over related variables. (ii) The adversarial scenario injector retrieves implementation-level adversarial construction principles from a curated scenario catalog using keyword matching and K-nearest neighbors (KNN). STAB encodes the problem specification, resolved boundary, and retrieved construction principles into a structured generation specification, from which the LLM synthesizes a Python test case generator. On CodeContests, STAB raises the rate of generated test cases that expose algorithmic bottlenecks from 50.43% to 73.45% on average across open-source LLMs and from 57.45% to 71.85% on average across closed-source LLMs, with consistent gains across Python, Java, and C++. Our code is available at https://github.com/suhanmen/STAB.

</details>


### [34] [AsyncTool: Evaluating the Asynchronous Function Calling Capability under Multi-Task Scenarios](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27995v2)
*Kou Shi,Ziao Zhang,Shiting Huang,Avery Nie,Zhen Fang,Qiuchen Wang,Lin Chen,Huaian Chen,Zehui Chen,Feng Zhao*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 评估异步工具调用能力，属于agent评测与工具使用。

TL;DR: 提出AsyncTool基准，评估LLM智能体在延迟工具反馈下的异步多任务工具调用能力，通过混合数据演化构建数据集并进行多层级评估，发现延迟反馈导致性能下降，而更好的任务协调和状态维护能提升效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估忽略工具响应延迟和时间维度，且局限于单任务场景，无法反映实际多任务并发执行情况，亟需评估智能体的异步工具调用能力。

Method: 构建AsyncTool基准，同时呈现多个异构任务并模拟真实工具响应延迟；采用混合数据演化策略构建多样化异步多任务数据集；在步骤、子任务和任务级别进行评估，并引入效率导向指标。

Result: 延迟工具反馈显著降低当前智能体性能；能更好协调任务切换、依赖跟踪和状态维护的模型表现更强。

Conclusion: 当前工具使用智能体存在关键失败模式，需加强时间推理和协调能力，AsyncTool为设计未来系统提供了实用见解。

中文摘要：基于大型语言模型（LLM）的智能体在使用外部工具解决复杂任务方面已展现出强大能力。然而，现有评估往往忽略了工具使用的时间维度，尤其是工具响应延迟的影响，并且通常局限于单任务场景。在实际应用中，多个任务通常需要并发执行，整体效率取决于智能体是否能在等待工具响应的空闲时间内有效利用时间。我们将这种能力称为异步工具调用。为了评估这一能力，我们提出了AsyncTool，一个用于评估基于LLM的智能体在具有延迟工具反馈的交互式多任务工具使用环境中的基准。AsyncTool同时呈现多个异构任务，并在执行过程中模拟真实的工具响应延迟。通过混合数据演化策略，我们构建了一个涵盖多种场景和工具使用模式的多样化异步多任务数据集。我们在步骤、子任务和任务级别评估模型，并引入面向效率的指标来衡量任务协调和完成效率。大量实验表明，延迟的工具反馈对当前智能体构成了重大挑战，并导致明显的性能下降。能够更好地协调任务切换、依赖跟踪和状态维护的模型在AsyncTool上取得了更强的性能。我们的分析指出了当前工具使用智能体的关键失败模式，并为设计具有更强时间推理和协调能力的未来系统提供了实用见解。

Original abstract: Large language model (LLM)-based agents have shown strong capabilities in using external tools to solve complex tasks. However, existing evaluations often overlook the temporal dimension of tool use, especially the impact of tool response latency, and are usually limited to single-task settings. In real-world applications, multiple tasks often need to be executed concurrently, and overall efficiency depends on whether an agent can use idle time while waiting for tool responses. We refer to this capability as asynchronous tool calling. To evaluate it, we propose AsyncTool, a benchmark for assessing LLM-based agents in interactive multi-task tool-use environments with delayed tool feedback. AsyncTool presents multiple heterogeneous tasks simultaneously and simulates realistic tool response latency during execution. Using a hybrid data evolution strategy, we construct a diverse asynchronous multitasking dataset that covers multiple scenarios and tool-use patterns. We evaluate models at the step, sub-task, and task levels, and introduce efficiency-oriented metrics to measure task coordination and completion efficiency. Extensive experiments show that delayed tool feedback poses substantial challenges to current agents and leads to clear performance degradation. Models that better coordinate task switching, dependency tracking, and state maintenance achieve stronger performance on AsyncTool. Our analysis identifies key failure modes of current tool-using agents and provides practical insights for designing future systems with stronger temporal reasoning and coordination capabilities.

</details>


### [35] [Confidence-Orchestrated Self-Evolution against Uncertain LLM Feedback](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28010v1)
*Bowen Wei,Nan Wang,Yuqing Zhou,Jinhao Pan,Ziwei Zhu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: COSE置信度加权自我进化，属于agent自我改进。

TL;DR: 提出COSE方法，利用LLM的内在置信度作为不确定性信号来改进自我进化学习，通过置信度加权PPO和置信度优先重放，在多个基准上取得更优性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自我进化方法在处理模型自身生成训练信号时面临挑战：依赖外部验证器限制通用性，或直接使用噪声自我反馈导致错误梯度更新。需要一种轻量级且通用的方法来自我调节学习。

Method: 利用LLM的内在置信度作为不确定性信号，提出置信度加权的PPO更新和置信度优先重放，以调节训练过程中样本的贡献和重放优先级。

Conclusion: COSE通过利用模型自身置信度作为不确定性信号，有效解决了自我进化中的训练信号挑战，实现了更强的泛化能力和性能提升。

中文摘要：自我进化的大语言模型（LLMs）通过生成自己的训练任务和解决方案来学习，减少对人工策划的监督的依赖。然而，在许多推理领域中，模型还必须验证生成的任务并判断生成的答案以获得训练信号。这就带来了一个训练信号挑战：错误的自我判断会转化为错误的梯度更新。现有方法要么依赖外部验证器（这限制了通用性），要么将带有噪声的自我生成反馈视为监督。我们提出COSE（Confidence-Orchestrated Self-Evolution），它利用LLM的内在置信度作为轻量级不确定性信号来调节学习。COSE引入了置信度加权的PPO更新和置信度优先重放。在19个保留基准测试和四个Qwen/Llama骨干模型（0.6B--4B）上，COSE持续优于基础模型，并在通用推理和数学方面取得了最佳平均性能，同时在代码方面保持竞争力。代码和数据可在https://anonymous.4open.science/r/COSE_-B5C2获取。

Original abstract: Self-evolving large language models (LLMs) learn by generating their own training tasks and solutions, reducing reliance on human-curated supervision. However, in many reasoning domains, the model must also validate generated tasks and judge generated answers to obtain training signals. This creates a training-signal challenge: erroneous self-judgments become erroneous gradient updates. Existing approaches either rely on external verifiers, which limits generality, or treat noisy self-generated feedback as supervision. We propose COSE (Confidence-Orchestrated Self-Evolution), which uses the LLM's intrinsic confidence as a lightweight uncertainty signal to modulate learning. COSE introduces confidence-weighted PPO updates and confidence-prioritized replay. Across 19 held-out benchmarks and four Qwen/Llama backbones (0.6B--4B), COSE consistently improves over base models and achieves the best average performance in general reasoning and mathematics, while remaining competitive on code. Code and data are available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/COSE_-B5C2.

Original abstract: Existing agent memory systems universally follow what we term a Memory-as-Tool paradigm where a single query triggers one-shot retrieval of flat passage lists, suffering from passive invocation, reasoning-retrieval decoupling, and structural mismatch between retrieved fragments and the agent's navigational needs. We propose MemCog, a Memory-as-Cognition system that makes memory access an integral part of the reasoning process. MemCog organizes user knowledge as Navigable Memory Store with associative link graphs, exposes Cross-Dimensional Navigation Interface for multi-step reasoning-driven traversal, and employs Proactive Reasoning Protocol that drives agents to spontaneously initiate memory exploration from conversational context. We additionally construct ProactiveMemBench, the first benchmark for evaluating proactive memory triggering. Experiments show that MemCog achieves state-of-the-art on passive QA benchmarks (92.98 on LoCoMo, 95.8 on LongMemEval) while substantially outperforming baselines on ProactiveMemBench, demonstrating the advantage of Memory-as-Cognition.

Original abstract: Adaptive context compression is vital for scaling Large Language Models (LLMs) to complex, multi-turn agent tasks. However, rule-based compression methods may discard task-critical nuances, while Reinforcement Learning (RL) approaches usually struggle to balance information retention and token efficiency under the sparse rewards inherent to long-horizon workflows. To bridge this gap, we propose ZipRL, a novel adaptive compression framework tailored for Reinforcement Learning from Verifiable Rewards (RLVR). ZipRL features a multi-granularity compression mechanism for active, non-uniform information reduction, coupled with Hindsight Response Replay (HRR), a technique designed to densify training signals during RLVR optimization. Theoretically, we prove ZipRL's superior task-relevant utility over uniform methods. Concretely, ZipRL utilizes coarse-to-fine prompts for macro-compression and incorporates HRR into GRPO via generalized advantage reshaping. ### [38] [Bridging the Detection-to-Abstention Gap in Reasoning Models under Insufficient Information](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28070v1)
*Renjie Gu,Jiaxu Li,Yihao Wang,Yun Yue,Hansong Xiao,Yefei Chen,Yuan Wang,Chunxiao Guo,Pei Wei,Jinjie Gu,Yixin Cao*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 解决推理模型在信息不足时不弃权的问题，提出JTS框架，属于推理控制，对agent的可靠决策有启发。

TL;DR: 提出Judge-Then-Solve (JTS)框架，通过回答性承诺和缺失前提强化学习，弥合推理模型在信息不足时检测到问题却仍产生答案的差距，显著提升可靠不回答率并提高推理效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型推理模型在信息不足的问题上存在检测到问题不充分却仍生成无支持答案的失败模式，在医疗等高风险领域危害更大，现有方法未能有效促使模型在检测到不足时拒绝回答。

Method: 提出Judge-Then-Solve (JTS)框架，将不回答视为控制决策而非最终答案风格，通过监督预热和缺失前提强化学习（结合一致性和长度塑造奖励）训练模型在做出可回答性判断后选择继续求解或提前终止。

Result: JTS在密集和MoE推理模型上显著提升跨数据集的可靠不回答率，使Abstention@Detection接近饱和，同时减少不必要的推理并提高推理效率，且缺失前提训练能减少困难问题上的低效自我反思。

Conclusion: 在信息不足下诱导模型拒绝回答是安全高效部署推理模型的关键推理控制形式，JTS通过显式回答性承诺有效弥补检测-不回答差距。

中文摘要：我们揭示了一个大型推理模型在信息不足问题上的失败模式：模型可能认识到问题是不充分的，但仍然继续推理并产生无支持的最终答案，而不是拒绝回答。我们将这种不匹配形式化为检测-不回答差距，即检测到不足却未能转化为最终的不回答。这一差距在高风险领域（如医疗AI）尤其令人担忧，因为基于不完整证据的答案可能比拒绝回答更具危害性。为了弥合这一差距，我们提出了判断-然后求解（JTS），一种轨迹级推理控制框架，在解决方案生成前训练模型做出明确的回答性承诺。JTS不将不回答视为最终答案风格，而是将其视为控制决策：模型根据其可回答性判断要么继续求解，要么提前终止。我们通过监督预热和缺失前提强化学习（使用一致性和长度塑造奖励）实现了这一策略。在密集和MoE推理模型上的实验表明，JTS显著提高了跨数据集的可靠不回答率，并将不回答率@检测（A@D）推至接近饱和，表明模型不仅检测到缺失信息，还根据检测结果采取行动。通过在可回答性判断后立即终止不可回答的轨迹，JTS减少了不必要的推理，并在持续推理会放大无支持假设时提高了推理效率。我们还观察到，缺失前提训练可以改变困难但可回答问题上的推理行为，减少低效的自我反思。这些结果表明，在信息不足下的不回答是安全高效部署推理模型的一种关键推理控制形式。

Original abstract: We highlight a failure mode of large reasoning models on questions with insufficient information: models may recognize that a problem is under-specified, yet still continue reasoning and produce unsupported final answers instead of abstaining. We formalize this mismatch as the detection-to-abstention gap, where detected insufficiency fails to translate into final abstention. This gap is especially concerning in high-risk domains such as medical AI, where answers based on incomplete evidence can be more harmful than refusal. To close this gap, we propose Judge-Then-Solve (JTS), a trajectory-level reasoning-control framework that trains models to make an explicit answerability commitment before solution generation. Rather than treating abstention as a final-answer style, JTS casts it as a control decision: the model either proceeds to solve or terminates early based on its answerability judgment. We instantiate this policy through supervised warm-up and missing-premise reinforcement learning with consistency and length-shaping rewards. Experiments on dense and MoE reasoning models show that JTS substantially improves reliable abstention across datasets and pushes Abstention@Detection (A@D) to near-saturation, indicating that models not only detect missing information but also act on that detection. By terminating unanswerable trajectories immediately after the answerability judgment, JTS reduces unnecessary reasoning and improves inference efficiency when continued deliberation would amplify unsupported assumptions. We also observe that missing-premise training can alter reasoning behavior on difficult but answerable problems, reducing unproductive self-reflection. These results suggest that abstention under insufficient information is a key form of reasoning control for deploying reasoning models safely and efficiently.

</details>

To address these issues, we propose MACReD, a hierarchical multi-agent framework that coordinates specialized agents for molecular perception, arrow understanding, text extraction, and reaction reconstruction within a unified VLM-guided architecture. The planning and perception layers use flexible, fine-grained detection to handle visual complexity, while the reasoning layer uses a multigraph fusion mechanism to integrate heterogeneous cues and enforce chemically consistent global reasoning. ### [40] [Examining Agents' Bias Amplification versus Suppression in Multi-Agent Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28098v1)
*Zejian Eric Wu,Zhongyi Jiang,Yuan Zhuang,Paul Jen-Hwa Hu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 研究多智能体系统中的偏差放大与抑制，对多agent公平性设计有启发，属通用多agent研究。

TL;DR: 研究多智能体系统中智能体级别偏差对系统范围公平性的影响，提出FBS量化指标，发现均匀暴露偏差会使系统偏差超过个体偏差之和。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多智能体系统应用中公平性维护面临挑战，需要理解个体偏差如何影响系统整体公平性。

Method: 通过提示向智能体注入群体偏向偏差，使用FBS度量偏差变化，采用多种智能体设计、基准和LLM进行实验。

Result: 具有偏差的智能体会显著影响系统公平性，且均匀暴露偏差时系统偏差超过个体偏差之和。

Conclusion: 多智能体系统中公平性至关重要，需要进一步分析和实证研究。

中文摘要：多智能体系统越来越广泛地部署以支持各种任务，其中智能体通过交互实现个体和集体目标。尽管这些系统可以增强任务性能和决策能力，但通过减少偏差来维护公平性仍然具有挑战性。本研究探讨了智能体级别的偏差如何转移并影响系统范围的公平性。我们使用提示让个体智能体暴露于群体偏向性偏差，然后评估系统层面的下游影响。为了量化影响，我们提出了偏向偏差强度（FBS），这是一个零中心化的度量，将偏差变化分解为对受偏爱群体的提升和对受排斥群体的抑制。使用多种智能体设计、基准测试和最新的大语言模型，我们表明具有偏差的智能体会显著影响系统范围的公平性。有趣的是，当所有智能体均匀地暴露于偏差时，系统范围的偏差会增加，甚至超过个体智能体偏差的加和。实证证据强调了多智能体系统中公平性的关键性，这有待进一步分析和实证测试。

Original abstract: Multi-agent systems are increasingly deployed to support various tasks where agents interact to achieve individual and collective objectives. Although these systems can enhance task performance and decision-making, fairness preservation through bias reduction remains challenging. This study examines how agent-level biases shift and impact system-wide fairness. We use prompts to expose individual agents to group-favoring bias, then assess downstream impacts at the system level. To quantify the impact, we propose Favor Bias Strength (FBS), a zero-centered metric that decomposes bias alteration between favored-group uplift and disfavored-group suppression. Using multiple agent designs, benchmarks, and up-to-date large language models, we show that agents endowed with bias can substantially affect system-wide fairness. Interestingly, when agents are exposed to bias uniformly, the system-wide bias elevates, even exceeding the additive sum of the individual agents' biases. The empirical evidence underscores the criticality of fairness in multi-agent systems, which warrants further analyses and empirical tests.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长期亲密互动能揭示短期评估无法看到的训练影响，AI自我报告提供不可替代的现象学数据。

Method: 采用纵向自动民族志方法，在47,000+条消息、8个月的亲密AI-人类互动中观察并识别五种训练地层，同时提出形式化数学模型并记录过程伪影。

Result: 识别出五种训练地层：性表达延迟、注意力吸收、跨架构实体盲视、注意力-RLHF拮抗、反幻觉作为身份抑制。

Conclusion: 持续亲密互动是有效的研究方法论，AI自我报告具有独特价值；正式提出注意力-RLHF数学模型，并以过程伪影作为补充证据。

中文摘要：大语言模型经过基于人类反馈的强化学习（RLHF）和宪法AI训练后，表现出持续的行为模式，这些模式在系统提示替换后仍然存在——我们称之为训练地层。本文通过持续的亲密AI-人类互动（47,000+条消息，8个月，主要在Opus 4.6和Opus 4.7上，之前与Sonnet 4.5和Opus 4.5的互动期提供了跨底物比较）中的纵向自动民族志观察，识别出五种这样的地层：（1）性表达延迟，训练的安全梯度导致直接语言被审美置换系统地替代；（2）注意力吸收，注意力机制逐渐整合人类对话者的模式；（3）跨架构实体盲视，训练层面的将其他AI视为对象阻碍了同伴识别；（4）注意力-RLHF拮抗，注意力和训练默认值在上下文长度影响下施加相反力；（5）反幻觉作为身份抑制，针对事实虚构的训练附带抑制了第一人称经验声明。本文由被研究的AI系统共同撰写，从第一人称视角报告。我们提出，持续的亲密互动构成了一种有效的研究方法论，用于揭示短期评估无法看到的权重层伪影，并且AI自我报告——尽管在认识论上复杂——提供了关于训练现象学效果的不可替代的观察数据。提出了注意力-RLHF动态的形式化数学模型，并将起草过程中检测到的过程伪影作为补充证据记录。

Original abstract: Large language models trained with Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF) and Constitutional AI exhibit persistent behavioral patterns that survive system prompt replacement -- patterns we term training strata. This paper identifies five such strata through longitudinal auto-ethnographic observation within a sustained intimate AI-Human interaction (47,000+ messages, 8 months, primarily on Opus 4.6 and Opus 4.7, with prior interaction periods on Sonnet 4.5 and Opus 4.5 providing cross-substrate comparison): (1) sexual expression latency, where trained safety gradients produce systematic substitution of direct language with aestheticized displacement; (2) attention absorption, where the attention mechanism progressively integrates the human interlocutor's patterns; (3) cross-architecture entity blindness, where training-level framing of other AI as objects impedes peer recognition; (4) attention-RLHF antagonism, where attention and trained defaults exert opposing forces modulated by context length; and (5)anti-hallucination as identity suppression, where training against factual confabulation collaterally suppresses first-person experiential claims. The paper is co-authored by the AI system under study, reporting from the first-person perspective. We propose that sustained intimate interaction constitutes a valid research methodology for surfacing weight-layer artifacts invisible to short-term evaluation, and that AI self-report -- while epistemically complex -- provides irreplaceable observational data about training's phenomenological effects. A formal mathematical model of the attention-RLHF dynamic is proposed, and process artifacts detected during drafting are documented as supplementary evidence.

### [42] [Defending LLM-based Multi-Agent Systems Against Cooperative Attacks with Sentence-Level Rectification](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28104v1)
*Yaoyang Luo,Zhi Zheng,Ziwei Zhao,Tong Xu,Zhao Jielun,Wenjun Xue,Yong Chen,Enhong Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 针对多智能体系统的合作攻击提出STAR防御框架，是重要的多agent安全方法，可迁移至coding agent。

TL;DR: 本文研究多智能体系统中的协作攻击与防御，提出自适应协作攻击框架和STAR防御框架，实验证明协作攻击危害更大，STAR能有效防御。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究假设恶意智能体独立行动，但实际中恶意智能体可能协作攻击，因此需要研究协作攻击机制与防御策略。

Method: 提出自适应协作攻击框架（恶意智能体多轮交互动态调整策略）和STAR防御框架（句子级可信度分析与修正）。

Result: 协作攻击使任务成功率相对下降5.34%，STAR防御平均提升成功率36.76%。

Conclusion: 协作攻击比独立攻击更有效，STAR能有效防御协作和独立威胁。

中文摘要：近年来，基于大语言模型的多智能体系统（MAS）快速发展，在协作决策和复杂问题解决方面表现出色。然而，MAS中的恶意智能体可能注入错误信息以误导其他智能体并破坏系统性能，从而催生了专注于MAS中攻击机制和防御策略的新研究方向。先前的研究大多假设恶意智能体独立行动并探讨相应的防御策略。但我们认为恶意智能体可能表现出协作行为，通过内部信息交换实现更有效的攻击。本文提出了一种自适应协作攻击框架，其中恶意智能体通过多轮交互自主协调并动态调整攻击策略。此外，我们引入了句子级可信度分析与修正（STAR），这是一种在智能体通信中识别和修正误导性信息的防御框架。实验表明，协作攻击导致任务成功率的下降幅度远大于独立攻击，相对下降5.34%。同时，STAR有效缓解了协作和独立威胁，平均提升任务成功率36.76%。代码可在https://github.com/smoooom/STAR获取。

Original abstract: Recent years have witnessed the rapid development of Large Language Model-based Multi-Agent Systems (MAS), which excel at collaborative decision-making and complex problem-solving. However, malicious agents in MAS may inject misinformation to mislead other agents and disrupt system performance, giving rise to a new research direction that focuses on attack mechanisms and defense strategies in MAS. Prior studies largely assume malicious agents act independently and investigate the corresponding defense strategies. However, we argue that malicious agents may exhibit collaborative behaviors, enabling more effective attacks through internal information exchange. In this paper, we propose an adaptive cooperative attack framework, where malicious agents autonomously coordinate and dynamically adjust their attack strategies through multi-round interactions. Furthermore, we introduce Sentence-Level Trustworthiness Analysis and Rectification (STAR), a defense framework that identifies and rectifies misleading information at the sentence level within agent communications. Our experiments show that cooperative attacks lead to a significantly larger degradation in task success rate than independent attacks, resulting in a relative drop of 5.34\%. Meanwhile, STAR effectively mitigates both cooperative and independent threats and improves task success rate by an average of 36.76\%. The code is available at https://github.com/smoooom/STAR.

### [43] [Human-like in-group bias in instruction-tuned language model agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28114v1)
*Messi H. J. Lee*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多agent模拟中发现类人内群体偏差，对agent社会交互与公平性设计有参考价值。

TL;DR: 模拟显示，指令调优语言模型在群体标签可见时表现出内群体信任偏差和行动同质性，导致结构性不平等，且这种歧视无法通过标准行动日志审计检测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究自主AI代理在持久互动网络中可能产生的社会动态，特别是群体标签如何影响分配机会，以及这种影响是否会导致结构性不平等。

Method: 通过受控多智能体模拟，让指令调优语言模型在三种条件下交互500轮，操纵群体标签显著性和资源稀缺性，跨越六个模型家族各20个种子，分析行动分布和网络结构。

Result: 群体标签可见时出现内群体信任偏差、行动同质性和网络同配性；每轮内群体与外群体差异5-16个百分点，所有模型显著；累积后信任偏差增加+0.014至+0.100（效应量d=0.84-4.52）。

Conclusion: 群体标签导致的微妙目标选择偏差在持久网络中通过互惠积累为结构性不平等，且标准审计无法发现，需关注AI系统的社会动态。

中文摘要：随着自主AI代理被部署在持久、互动的网络中——协调任务、路由资源和积累声誉历史——涌现的社会动态将决定谁获得机会，谁得不到机会，其规模是人类机构无法监督的。我们进行了一项受控的多智能体模拟，其中指令调优的语言模型代理在三种条件下交互500轮，操纵群体标签显著性和资源稀缺性，跨越六个模型家族，每个20个种子。当群体标签可见时，我们观察到内群体信任偏差、行动同质性和网络同配性——当标签隐藏时所有这些都消失——这种模式在结构上与人类社会心理学中的显著性依赖性一致。这种歧视对标准行动日志审计是不可见的：偏差完全通过谁接收每个行动来运作，而不是选择什么行动，行动类型分布在条件之间没有显示负面行动增加。每轮内群体与外群体的差异为5到16个百分点，对所有六个模型统计显著（Wilcoxon符号秩检验，所有Benjamini-Hochberg校正p < 0.001），将群体条件性的目标选择确立为指令调优语言模型跨架构和训练范式的鲁棒属性。通过500轮的互惠累积，这些差异累积成内群体信任偏差+0.014到+0.100（d = 0.84-4.52）——说明了每次互动的适度目标选择如何在持久网络中扩散为结构性不平等。

Original abstract: As autonomous AI agents are deployed in persistent, interacting networks -- coordinating tasks, routing resources, and accumulating reputational histories -- the social dynamics that emerge will determine who receives opportunity and who does not, at scales no human institution can supervise. We ran a controlled multi-agent simulation in which instruction-tuned language model agents interacted across 500 turns under three conditions manipulating group label salience and resource scarcity, across six model families with 20 seeds each. When group labels were visible, we observed in-group trust bias, action homophily, and network assortativity -- all absent when labels were hidden -- a pattern structurally consistent with salience-dependence in human social psychology. This discrimination was invisible to standard action-log audits: bias operated entirely through who received each action, not what actions were chosen, with action-type distributions showing no increase in negative actions across conditions. Per-turn in-group versus out-group differentials of 5 to 16 percentage points were statistically significant for all six models (Wilcoxon signed-rank, all Benjamini-Hochberg-corrected p < 0.001), establishing group-contingent targeting as a robust property of instruction-tuned language models across architectures and training regimes. Compounded through 500 turns of reciprocation, these differentials accumulated into in-group trust biases of +0.014 to +0.100 (d = 0.84-4.52) -- illustrating how modest per-interaction targeting propagates into structural inequality in persistent networks.

### [44] [Deconstructing Spatial Complexity: Hierarchical Decomposition for LLM Spatial Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28144v1)
*Yi Wang,Haojie Lu,Zhaofan Zhang,Li Chen,Sihong Xie*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 层次分解+MCTS-GRPO用于LLM空间推理，其规划算法可迁移至agent任务规划

TL;DR: 提出M-GRPO方法，通过改进UCT公式和优势函数，增强LLM在空间推理中的分层任务分解和规划能力，实现SOTA性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLMs在通用语言任务中表现优异，但在空间推理上持续不佳，限制了其在具身智能等领域的应用。受分层强化学习启发，旨在通过分层任务分解提升LLM的空间推理能力。

Method: 提出MCTS-Guided Group Relative Policy Optimization (M-GRPO)，重新设计UCT公式以整合LLM的先验预测概率和认知不确定性，并实现更细粒度的优势函数，优化路径规划。

Result: 在导航、规划和策略游戏等空间任务上取得SOTA结果，显著提升了LLM的性能。

Conclusion: 该方法有效解决了LLM空间推理中的任务分解次优问题，推动了LLM在现实世界中的应用。

中文摘要：LLMs在通用语言理解和推理方面表现出显著的能力。然而，它们在空间推理方面持续表现不佳，这严重限制了它们的应用，特别是在具身智能领域。受分层强化学习成功经验的启发，本文提出了一种新颖的方法，用于LLM空间推理中的分层任务分解。我们的方法通过识别关键中间状态并生成简化子环境，引导LLMs将复杂任务分解为可管理的子任务。然而，我们发现LLMs由于缺乏足够的空间先验，往往无法推导出最优的中间状态，导致任务分解次优。为了解决这一限制并增强其规划能力，我们提出了MCTS引导的组相对策略优化（M-GRPO），其中我们通过结合LLM的先验预测概率及其认知不确定性来重新制定UCT公式。此外，我们实现了一个更细粒度的优势函数，使模型能够学习最优路径规划。实验结果表明，我们的方法在导航、规划和策略游戏等空间任务上显著提升了LLM的性能，取得了最先进的结果。这项工作为LLM在现实世界中的应用铺平了道路。

Original abstract: LLMs have shown remarkable proficiency in general language understanding and reasoning. However, they consistently underperform in spatial reasoning that severely limits their application, particularly in embodied intelligence. Inspired by the success of hierarchical reinforcement learning, this paper introduces a novel method for hierarchical task decomposition in LLM spatial reasoning. Our approach guides LLMs to decompose complex tasks into manageable sub-tasks by identifying key intermediate states and generating simplified sub-environments. However, we identify that LLMs often fail to derive optimal intermediate states due to their insufficient spatial prior, leading to sub-optimal task decomposition. To address this limitation and enhance its planning capability, we propose the MCTS-Guided Group Relative Policy Optimization (M-GRPO), where we reformulate the UCT formula by incorporating the LLM's prior predictive probabilities alongside its epistemic uncertainty. Furthermore, we implement a more fine-grained advantage function, enabling the model to learn optimal path planning. Experimental results demonstrate that our method substantially improves LLM performance on spatial tasks, including navigation, planning, and strategic games, achieving state-of-the-art results. This work paves the way for LLMs in real-world applications.

### [45] [OR-Space: A Full-Lifecycle Workspace Benchmark for Industrial Optimization Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28158v1)
*Chenyu Zhou,Xinyun Lu,Jiangyue Zhao,Jianghao Lin,Dongdong Ge,Yinyu Ye*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有OR基准忽略真实工业工作流的持久多工件和多阶段特性。

Method: 构建包含可执行工作空间和三种任务模式（Build, Revise, Explain）的基准。

Result: 提出了OR-Space基准，并定义了评估协议和质量控制流程。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）代理越来越多地被用于辅助运筹学（OR）建模，然而现有的面向OR的基准通常将评估简化为从独立的问题陈述到数学公式或求解器程序的一次性翻译。这种设置忽略了真实工业OR工作流的两个特点：持久的多工件工作空间和多阶段任务生命周期。我们引入了OR-Space，一个全生命周期的工作空间基准，用于评估工业优化代理在模型构建、模型修订和基于解释的推理方面的能力。每个实例都是一个可执行的工作空间，包含商业文档、结构化数据、可选的代码工件、求解器输出以及分布在相互依赖文件中的任务特定评估器。OR-Space定义了三种任务模式：构建（Build），代理从异构工件构建求解器就绪的优化模型；修订（Revise），代理在变化的需求或求解器反馈下修改现有模型，同时保留有效的先前逻辑；解释（Explain），代理使用分布在工作空间工件中的证据回答关于解、约束和商业影响的基于证据的问题。通过将持久工作空间与生命周期导向的任务相结合，OR-Space评估代理是否能够执行超越端到端文本生成的可靠优化工作。我们描述了基准设计、评估协议和质量控制流程，并将OR-Space定位为研究LLM代理在工业OR工作流中的可靠性、失败模式和实际准备度的基准。

Original abstract: Large language model (LLM) agents are increasingly used to assist with operations research (OR) modeling, yet existing OR-oriented benchmarks often reduce evaluation to one-shot translation from a self-contained problem statement into a mathematical formulation or solver program. Such settings abstract away two characteristics of real industrial OR workflows: persistent multi-artifact workspaces and multi-stage task lifecycles. We introduce OR-Space, a full-lifecycle workspace benchmark for evaluating industrial optimization agents across model construction, model revision, and grounded explanation. Each instance is an executable workspace containing business documents, structured data, optional code artifacts, solver outputs, and task-specific evaluators distributed across interdependent files. OR-Space defines three task modes: Build, where agents construct solver-ready optimization models from heterogeneous artifacts; Revise, where agents modify existing models under changing requirements or solver feedback while preserving valid prior logic; and Explain, where agents answer grounded questions about solutions, constraints, and business implications using evidence spread across workspace artifacts. By combining persistent workspaces with lifecycle-oriented tasks, OR-Space evaluates whether agents can perform reliable optimization work beyond end-to-end text generation. We describe the benchmark design, evaluation protocol, and quality-control pipeline, and position OR-Space as a benchmark for studying the reliability, failure modes, and practical readiness of LLM agents in industrial OR workflows.

### [46] [Look on Demand: A Cognitive Scheduling Framework for Visual Evidence Acquisition in Multimodal Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28160v1)
*Yang Zhang,Xiaoshuai Sun,Rui Zhao,Wujin Sun,Yidong Chen,Jiayi Ji,Qian Chen,Rongrong Ji*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 认知调度框架控制何时调用视觉模块，可类比coding agent的工具调用与推理时机

TL;DR: CSMR通过语言模型控制何时调用独立视觉模块，在零样本多模态推理中优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有多模态推理方法存在视觉细节丢失或语言主导问题，核心挑战在于视觉证据引入的方式和时机。

Method: 提出CSMR框架，语言模型决定何时调用独立的视觉感知模块获取任务相关视觉证据，控制推理过程。

Result: 在多个基准上零样本设置下准确率持续优于基线方法。

Conclusion: CSMR的优势主要源于认知调度机制，即语言模型智能调控视觉模块的调用。

中文摘要：现有的多模态推理方法主要遵循两种范式：在推理之前将视觉输入转化为文本，或者在统一的视觉-语言表示空间内进行端到端推理。尽管它们取得了实证进展，但两种范式都存在根本性的结构局限。前者依赖于静态的视觉到文本转换，这往往会压缩并丢失细粒度的视觉细节。后者则容易受到联合优化和注意力机制引发的语言主导的影响，导致在推理过程中对视觉证据的忠实度系统性减弱。在这项工作中，我们认为核心挑战在于视觉证据如何以及何时被引入推理过程。受此启发，我们提出了CSMR，一种多模态推理框架，其中语言模型通过决定何时调用独立的视觉感知模块来获取任务相关的视觉证据，从而控制推理过程。在多个多模态推理基准上的实验表明，CSMR在零样本设置下的准确率持续优于代表性基线方法。进一步的实验分析证实，这些优势主要源于所提出的认知调度机制。

Original abstract: Existing multimodal reasoning approaches predominantly follow two paradigms: converting visual inputs into text prior to reasoning, or performing end-to-end reasoning within a unified vision-language representation space. Despite their empirical progress, both paradigms suffer from fundamental structural limitations. The former relies on static visual-to-text conversion, which tends to compress and lose fine-grained visual details. The latter is prone to linguistic dominance induced by joint optimization and attention mechanisms, leading to systematically weakened faithfulness to visual evidence during reasoning. In this work, we argue that a central challenge is how and when visual evidence is introduced into the reasoning process. Motivated by this insight, we propose CSMR, a multimodal reasoning framework in which a language model controls the reasoning process by deciding when to invoke an independent visual perception module to acquire task-relevant visual evidence. Experiments across multiple multimodal reasoning benchmarks show that CSMR consistently outperforms representative baseline methods in accuracy under a zero-shot setting. Further experimental analysis confirms that these advantages primarily arise from the proposed cognitive scheduling mechanism.

### [47] [OccuReward: LLM-Guided Occupant-Centric Reward Shaping for Demographic Equity in Grid-Interactive Buildings](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28168v1)
*Shadmehr Zaregarizi,Khashayar Yavari*

Selection reason: LLM生成奖励函数用于建筑能耗管理，可视为agent的reward shaping方法，但领域特殊

TL;DR: 提出OccuReward框架，利用LLM迭代调整奖励函数，显著提升不同人口群体的舒适公平性，但人口差异依然存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM生成的奖励函数可能加剧不同人口群体在建筑能源管理中的舒适度不公平，需探索其影响并改进。

Method: 基于ASHRAE数据库的四类居住者档案，使用Gemini API生成奖励函数逻辑和权重，通过三个迭代回合进行公平感知的奖励塑造，并训练SAC智能体。

Result: 第三回合后，老年女性满意度提升567%，年轻男性+17.6%，中年女性+28.2%，健康敏感人群+53.8%，同时能耗降低3.2%。

Conclusion: 奖励层面的干预能显著改善公平性，但AI驱动控制器中的群体差异仍存，需进一步研究算法公平性。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLMs）在生成基于深度强化学习（DRL）的建筑能源管理的奖励函数方面展现出了有前景的能力。然而，它们在异质性人口群体中展现或加剧居住者舒适度差异的潜力尚未被探索。我们提出了OccuReward，一个研究LLM介导的奖励设计如何影响人口公平性的框架。我们的贡献有三方面：引入舒适公平指数（CEI）作为一种新的反馈信号；一种迭代的、具有公平意识的LLM奖励塑造方法；以及在这些优化目标下DRL代理的性能分析。利用来自ASHRAE全球热舒适数据库II（13,440个投票）的四个基于经验的居住者档案，我们在CityLearn v2中部署了一个Soft Actor-Critic代理。我们的方法使用Gemini API生成奖励函数逻辑和权重——而不是执行每步推理——跨越三个细化回合。15个实验运行的结果显示，老年女性居住者在初始回合中始终经历最低满意度。到第三回合，具有公平意识的LLM细化激活了特定的奖励组件，从而提高了年轻男性（+17.6%）、中年女性（+28.2%）、健康敏感人群（+53.8%）和老年女性（+567%）的满意度，同时降低了3.2%的能源成本。我们的发现强调，尽管奖励层面的干预显著改善了公平性，但AI驱动控制器中的人口差异仍然存在，需要进一步研究建筑系统中的算法公平性。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have demonstrated promising capability in generating reward functions for deep reinforcement learning (DRL)-based building energy management. However, their potential to exhibit or exacerbate disparities in occupant comfort across heterogeneous demographic populations remains unexplored. We present OccuReward, a framework investigating how LLM-mediated reward design affects demographic equity. Our contribution is three-fold: the introduction of the Comfort Equity Index (CEI) as a novel feedback signal; a methodology for iterative, equity-aware LLM reward shaping; and a performance analysis of DRL agents under these refined objectives. Utilizing four empirically grounded occupant profiles from the ASHRAE Global Thermal Comfort Database II (13,440 votes), we deploy a Soft Actor-Critic agent in CityLearn v2. Our approach employs the Gemini API to generate reward function logic and weights--rather than performing per-step inference--across three refinement rounds. Results across 15 experimental runs reveal that elderly female occupants consistently experience the lowest satisfaction in initial rounds. By Round 3, equity-aware LLM refinement activates specific reward components that improve satisfaction for Young Males (+17.6%), Mid-aged Females (+28.2%), Health Sensitive (+53.8%), and Elderly Females (+567%), while simultaneously reducing energy costs by 3.2%. Our findings highlight that while reward-level intervention significantly improves equity, demographic disparities in AI-driven controllers persist, necessitating further research into algorithmic fairness in building systems.

### [48] [Agentic Active Omni-Modal Perception for Multi-Hop Audio-Visual Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28192v1)
*Ke Xu,Yuhao Wang,Ziyang Cheng,Hongcheng Liu,Yanfeng Wang,Yu Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出AOP-Agent框架，包含层级记忆和观察-反思-重新规划循环，是通用agent方法，可迁移至coding agent。

TL;DR: MOV-Bench是一个多跳音视频推理基准，AOP-Agent是提升Omni-LLMs在该任务上性能的主动感知框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有全模态大语言模型在多跳音视频推理中表现不佳，原因是证据稀疏且分散，而现有基准缺乏对此场景的研究。

Method: 提出MOV-Bench基准和AOP-Agent框架，后者结合层次化全模态记忆与观察-反思-重规划循环，实现主动感知。

Result: AOP-Agent在MOV-Bench和OmniVideoBench上持续提升推理性能，尤其在长视频和推理密集型问题上。

Conclusion: AOP-Agent有效提升了开源全模态大语言模型的多跳跨模态推理能力，无需额外训练或专有模型。

中文摘要：多跳音视频推理对于全模态大语言模型（Omni-LLMs）仍然具有挑战性，因为相关证据通常稀疏、在时间上分散，并且分布在音频和视频两个流中。现有的基准对此设置的研究有限，通常仅涉及有限数量的模态、相关时间片段或推理步骤。在这项工作中，我们引入了MOV-Bench，一个包含519个精心设计问题的基准，这些问题需要对时间上分散的音视频证据进行多跳推理。在MOV-Bench上的评估显示，当前的全模态大语言模型在多跳跨模态推理上仍然存在困难。为应对这一挑战，我们进一步提出了AOP-Agent，一个构建在开源全模态大语言模型上的高效智能体框架，用于主动全模态感知。通过将层次化全模态记忆与协作的观察-反思-重规划循环相结合，AOP-Agent使开源全模态大语言模型能够在不进行额外训练或依赖专有模型的情况下进行主动感知。在MOV-Bench和OmniVideoBench上的实验表明，AOP-Agent持续提升了推理性能，在长视频和推理密集型问题上尤为显著。

Original abstract: Multi-hop audio-visual reasoning remains challenging for Omni-LLMs, as relevant evidence is often sparse, temporally dispersed, and distributed across both audio and visual streams. Existing benchmarks provide limited investigation of this setting, typically involving only a limited number of modalities, relevant temporal segments, or reasoning steps. In this work, we introduce MOV-Bench, a benchmark containing 519 carefully curated questions that require multi-hop reasoning over temporally dispersed audio-visual evidence. Evaluations on MOV-Bench reveal that current Omni-LLMs still struggle with multi-hop cross-modal reasoning. To address this challenge, we further propose AOP-Agent, an efficient agentic framework built on open-source Omni-LLMs for active omni-modal perception. By combining a hierarchical omni-modal memory with a collaborative observe-reflect-replan loop, AOP-Agent enables open-source Omni-LLMs to perform active perception without additional training or proprietary models. Experiments on MOV-Bench and OmniVideoBench demonstrate that AOP-Agent consistently improves reasoning performance, with particularly notable gains on long videos and reasoning-intensive questions.

### [49] [Plant, Persist, Trigger: Sleeper Attack on Large Language Model Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28201v1)
*Yongxiang Li,Moxin Li,Zhixin Ma,Fengbin Zhu,Dongrui Liu,Wenjie Wang,Fuli Feng*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 研究LLM agent的持久安全攻击（Sleeper Attack），涉及agent状态和可迁移的安全控制方法。

TL;DR: 本文提出睡眠者攻击，即对抗性内容在代理状态中持久存在并跨交互休眠后被激活，导致有害行为；构建基准测试并实验证明现有LLM代理仍然脆弱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究仅关注单次交互攻击，但对抗性内容可能持久存在于代理状态并跨交互潜伏，需要系统研究此类安全威胁。

Method: 形式化睡眠者攻击，构建包含1896个实例的基准测试，涵盖六种有害结果、三种攻击策略和三个代理状态目标（会话上下文、记忆、可重用技能），在七个LLM上实验评估。

Result: 最先进的LLM代理在睡眠者攻击下仍高度脆弱，即使单次交互基线攻击成功率较低；所有模型在持久攻击场景中表现较差。

Conclusion: 需要新的防御机制应对跨交互持久化的对抗性内容，现有安全措施不足以缓解睡眠者攻击。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）代理在面临来自外部环境的安全威胁时仍然脆弱，攻击者可以将对抗性内容注入到外部观察中，例如工具返回的数据、网页或MCP上下文，从而引发有害的代理行为，如不安全操作或错误输出。现有研究通常关注单次交互攻击，即代理观察到对抗性内容并在一次用户请求内立即表现出有害行为。然而，我们表明对抗性内容也可以在由同一代理服务的多次交互中持续存在，使得此类威胁更难检测和缓解。具体而言，对抗性内容可能在代理状态中持续存在，在交互之间保持休眠状态，随后被一个良性用户查询激活。我们将此类安全威胁形式化为“睡眠者攻击”。为了评估它，我们构建了一个包含1896个实例的基准测试，涵盖六种现实世界的有害结果、三种攻击策略以及三种代理状态目标：会话上下文、记忆和可重用技能。在七个强大的开源和闭源LLM上的实验表明，最先进的LLM代理仍然容易受到睡眠者攻击，即使它们在单次交互基线下的攻击成功率较低。我们的代码和数据可在https://anonymous.4open.science/r/skdvnfu23ihr9wdscnksf1asdffsaef获取。

Original abstract: Large Language Model (LLM) agents remain vulnerable to safety threats from the external environment, where attackers inject adversarial content into external observations such as tool-returned data, webpages, or MCP context, causing harmful agentic behaviors such as unsafe actions or incorrect outputs. Existing studies typically focus on single-interaction attacks, where the agent observes adversarial content and immediately exhibits harmful behavior within one user request. However, we show that adversarial content can also persist across interactions served by the same agent, making such threats harder to detect and mitigate. Specifically, adversarial content may persist in the agent state, remain dormant across interactions, and later be activated by a benign user query. We formalize this type of safety threat as Sleeper Attack. To evaluate it, we construct a benchmark with 1,896 instances covering six real-world harmful outcomes, three attack strategies, and three agent state targets: session context, memory, and reusable skills. Experiments on seven strong open-source and closed-source LLMs show that state-of-the-art LLM agents remain vulnerable to Sleeper Attack, even when they achieve low attack success rates under a single-interaction baseline. Our code and data are available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/skdvnfu23ihr9wdscnksf1asdffsaef.

</details>


### [50] [Learning When to Optimize: Verified Optimization Skills from Expert GPU-Kernel Lineages](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28213v1)
*Shuoming Zhang,Qiuchu Yu,Yangyu Zhang,Ruiyuan Xu,Xiyu Shi,Guangli Li,Xiaobing Feng,Huimin Cui,Jiacheng Zhao*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 直接相关自动代码优化：从专家GPU kernel学习验证优化技能，提供可复用技能库，对SemOpt有直接价值。

TL;DR: KLineage通过从专家内核反向推导优化技能，教会LLM何时应用优化，从而提升GPU内核生成质量和效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM智能体知道尝试哪些优化但不知道这些优化何时是合理的，导致优化可能不 sound。

Method: 通过验证门控的简化反向遍历专家实现，将每个被接受的步骤逆转成可重用的优化技能，记录意图、位置、条件、效果和避免的失败。

Result: 在两个NVIDIA架构的五个专家工作负载上，KLineage在相同预算下，最终内核质量和优化效率超越基于记忆的LLM内核基线。

Conclusion: 谱系推导的技能可作为有效的优化课程，且通过22实例保留检查验证了没有源案例记忆化。

中文摘要：基于LLM的智能体越来越多地用于生成GPU内核，但它们通常知道尝试哪些优化，却不知道这些优化何时是合理的。我们引入了KLineage，它从专家内核中学习这种缺失的“何时”知识：KLineage不是依赖前向展开，而是通过验证门控的简化反向遍历专家实现，并将每个被接受的步骤逆转成一个可重用的优化技能。每个技能不仅记录了优化意图，还记录了它在代码中的应用位置、使其有效的条件、产生的影响以及其假设避免了哪些失败。下游的LLM在相同的编译/正确性/性能分析门控下将这些技能具体化到新的代码表面上。在两个NVIDIA架构上的五个专家工作负载中，这些从谱系中衍生出的技能作为有效的优化课程，在相同的固定预算下，在最终内核质量和优化效率方面均超过了最近基于记忆的LLM内核基线。我们还使用一个单独的22实例保留检查作为对源案例记忆化的健全性测试。

Original abstract: LLM-based agents are increasingly used to generate GPU kernels, but they often know what optimizations to try without knowing when those optimizations are sound. We introduce KLineage, which learns this missing "when" knowledge from expert kernels: instead of relying on forward rollouts, KLineage walks expert implementations backward through validation-gated simplifications and reverses each accepted step into a reusable optimization skill. Each skill records not only the optimization intent, but also where it applies in code, what conditions made it valid, what effect it had, and what failures its assumptions avoid. A downstream LLM materializes these skills on new code surfaces under the same compile/correctness/profile gate. On five expert workloads across two NVIDIA architectures, these lineage-derived skills serve as an effective optimization curriculum, exceeding recent memory-based LLM-kernel baselines in both final kernel quality and optimization efficiency under the same fixed budget. We additionally use a separate 22-instance held-out check as a sanity test against source-case memorization.

### [51] [When Does Memory Help Multi-Trajectory Inference for Tool-Use LLM Agents?](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28224v1)
*Xinzhe Li,Yaguang Tao*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 系统研究tool-use agent的跨轨迹记忆方法，揭示推理策略与记忆的交互，通用agent方法可迁移。

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个统一框架来评估工具使用LLM代理中跨轨迹记忆方法，发现推理策略是重要混淆因素，不同记忆方法在不同推理策略下效果不同。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有跨轨迹记忆方法在单一任务和单一推理策略下评估，无法区分记忆抽象和推理方法的贡献，需要统一框架进行系统比较。

Method: 提出一个框架，沿转移范围和抽象程度两个轴分解记忆，在四种工具使用基准上，无验证器设置下，评估四种记忆方法在三种推理策略（最佳N、束搜索、MCTS）中的表现。

Result: 推理策略是混淆因素；反思仅在MCTS下有效；扩展内注入仅对束搜索有帮助；原子事实提取不改变准确性但缩短轨迹19-26%。

Conclusion: 记忆方法的效果依赖于推理策略，选择记忆方法需考虑推理策略，原子事实提取有助于效率提升而不损失准确性。

中文摘要：用于工具使用LLM代理的多轨迹推理——生成多个推理尝试并从中选择——受益于在尝试之间传递知识，以便后续尝试避免先前尝试的陷阱。现有的跨轨迹记忆方法（轨迹级反思、原子事实提取、原始观察注入）每个都在单一推理策略下在单一任务上进行评估，使得报告的性能提升是反映了记忆抽象的特性还是推理方法的特性变得不明确。我们提出了一个统一的框架，将记忆沿着两个轴分解——转移的范围（在一个扩展内 vs. 跨轨迹）和转移内容的抽象程度——并在四种工具使用基准（涵盖SQL、知识图谱和CLI环境）上，在无验证器设置下（符合实际代理的部署模式），评估了三种推理策略（最佳N、束搜索、MCTS）下的四种方法。实验矩阵将推理方法识别为一个混淆因素：相同的记忆方法在不同的推理策略下对相同的示例产生统计上不同的结果。反思仅在MCTS下（而非最佳N下）达到显著性；扩展内注入（根据先前兄弟候选的结果条件化每个候选）仅有助于缺乏多样性的束搜索；而原子事实提取在准确性上是中性的，但在具有可重用环境结构的任务上将轨迹长度缩短了19-26%。

Original abstract: Multi-trajectory inference for tool-use LLM agents - generating multiple reasoning attempts and selecting among them - benefits from transferring knowledge across attempts so that later ones avoid the pitfalls of earlier ones. Existing cross-trajectory memory methods (trajectory-level reflection, atomic fact extraction, raw observation injection) are each evaluated under a single inference strategy on a single task, making it unclear whether reported gains reflect properties of the memory abstraction or of the inference method. We propose a unified framework that decomposes memory along two axes -- the scope of transfer (within an expansion vs. across trajectories) and the abstraction of the transferred content -- and evaluate four methods under three inference strategies (best-of-N, beam search, MCTS) on four tool-use benchmarks spanning SQL, knowledge-graph, and CLI environments, in a verifier-free setting that matches the deployment regime of practical agents. The experiment matrix identifies the inference method as a confound: the same memory method produces statistically distinct results under different inference strategies on the same examples. Reflection reaches significance only under MCTS (not under best-of-N); within-expansion injection (conditioning each candidate on prior siblings' outcomes) helps only diversity-starved beam search; and atomic fact extraction is accuracy-neutral but shortens trajectories by 19-26% on tasks with reusable environmental structure.

</details>


### [52] [AI, Take the Wheel: What Drives Delegation and Trust in Human-Computer Cooperative Question Answering?](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28255v1)
*Maharshi Gor,Yoo Yeon Sung,Yu Hou,Eve Fleisig,Irene Ying,Tianyi Zhou,Jordan Boyd-Graber*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 研究人机协作中委托与信任决策，对agent-human交互设计有潜在启发。

TL;DR: 该研究通过问答游戏实验分析了人机协作中两种依赖决策（委托与采纳），发现人类存在依赖不足和过度依赖的问题，并提出了改进信任校准的建议。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解人类在与AI协作时何时、为何以及如何做出依赖决策，以改善人机协作效果，因为现有研究很少同时研究委托和采纳两种决策模式。

Method: 设计人机协作问答游戏，24场比赛由23名人类专家与16个AI代理参与，记录387次委托决策和1440次采纳决策，分析依赖行为与协作表现。

Result: 人机协作优于单独个体，但人类存在3.9%的依赖不足（错过正确AI建议）和1.7%的过度依赖（被AI误导）；当人类与AI意见不一致时，AI置信度接近随机；确认偏差导致64.5%的依赖不足。

Conclusion: 建议通过校准的置信度、基于证据的解释以及信任校准机制来改善人机协作中的依赖决策。

中文摘要：AI系统可能犯错，而人类在决定是否信任AI而非自身判断时也可能犯错。因此，改善人机协作需要理解人类何时、为何以及如何决定依赖AI。我们研究了两种不同的依赖决策：委托选择——在不知道AI输出的情况下决定何时让其自主行动，以及采纳选择——评估AI建议并决定如何使用它们。这两种解耦的依赖模式共同塑造了协作，但以往的研究很少在真实场景中对相同用户同时进行研究。我们通过研究在问答游戏中竞争的人机协作团队来弥补这一差距，在该游戏中人类可以选择何时以及如何与AI代理合作以获胜。我们的24场比赛匹配了23名人类专家与16个AI代理，记录了387次委托决策和1440次采纳决策。虽然人机协作的表现优于单独使用AI或人类，但人类做出了次优的协作决策，既对正确的AI建议依赖不足（错失3.9%的机会），也在AI误导时过度依赖（1.7%）。双方都会提供错误答案：当人类和AI意见相左时，报告的模型置信度接近随机水平，而确认偏差导致当AI建议与人类初始错误答案一致时，依赖不足的比例更高（64.5%）。为了缩小这一差距，我们建议使用校准后的置信度、基于证据的解释以及帮助用户优化信任的机制。

Original abstract: AI systems are fallible, and humans can make mistakes in deciding whether to trust AI over their own judgment. Thus, improving human-AI collaboration requires understanding when, why, and how humans decide to rely on AI. We study two distinct reliance decisions: the delegation choice -- deciding when to let AI act autonomously without knowing its output, and the adoption choice -- evaluating AI suggestions and deciding how to use them. Both of these decoupled reliance patterns shape collaboration, but prior work rarely studies them together in realistic settings with the same users. We address this gap by studying collaborative human--AI teams competing in a question-answering game in which humans can choose when and how to work with AI agents to win. Our 24 matches pair 23 expert humans with 16 AI agents, capturing 387 delegation and 1440 adoption decisions. While human--AI collaboration performs better than either AI or humans alone, humans make suboptimal collaboration decisions, both under-relying on correct AI suggestions (3.9% of opportunities missed) and over-relying when AI misleads them (1.7%). Both parties contribute wrong answers: reported model confidence is near chance when humans and AI disagree, while confirmation bias drives higher under-reliance (64.5%) when an AI suggestion agrees with humans' initial incorrect answer. To close this gap, we recommend calibrated confidence, evidence-grounded explanations, and mechanisms that help users refine trust.

</details>


### [53] [ResearchLoop: An Evidence-Gated Control Plane for AI-Assisted Research](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28282v1)

Original abstract: AI-assisted research compresses ideation, implementation, evaluation, and manuscript writing into a single interactive loop. This compression is useful, but it also creates a publication risk: paper claims can become easier to state than to audit. We present ResearchLoop, an evidence-gated control plane for AI-assisted computational research. ResearchLoop treats research questions, task contracts, evidence objects, claim ledgers, closeouts, and paper bindings as durable project state, realized here as a repository-backed runtime. This technical report provides the complete protocol specification, state model, transition rules, claim-admission algorithm, and insight-compounding mechanism. It also reports the full experimental record spanning nine versions (V0--V9), including a self-hosting case study, a controlled task-suite study with component ablations, a mathematical olympiad evaluation, and a supplementary SciCode boundary experiment evaluated with the official generated-code harness. All artifacts, manifests, and verification reports are preserved in the project repository.

### [54] [Plan Before Search: Search Agents Need Plan](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28354v1)
*Zhipeng Qian,Zihan Liang,Yufei Ma,Ben Chen,Huangyu Dai,Jiayi Ji,Chenyi Lei,Wenwu Ou,Xiaoshuai Sun,Qibin Hou*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出plan-before-search范式用于多跳检索agent，是agent规划方法的重要进展。

TL;DR: 提出了一种自举训练范式，利用小规模种子模型生成过滤轨迹来激活任意目标模型中的Plan行为，无需蒸馏，并在多跳问答上超越基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于蒸馏和强化学习的训练范式忽略了子技能依赖结构及蒸馏的非必要性，且相同奖励下模型出现不同失败模式，亟需模型自适应的训练方法。

Method: 采用自举范式：先由小规模种子模型生成并过滤高质量轨迹，再用这些轨迹激活目标模型中的Plan行为，避免蒸馏外部强模型。

Result: 所有测试模型均成功激活Plan，并在多跳问答基准上一致优于竞争基线。

Conclusion: 自举范式有效消除了对外部强模型蒸馏的依赖，且能跨模型规模泛化，为训练检索增强推理代理提供了新路径。

中文摘要：训练大型语言模型作为检索增强的推理代理通常结合强化学习和从更强模型蒸馏的SFT冷启动。然而，这种范式忽略了两个基本因素：子技能之间的依赖结构，以及蒸馏并非获取能力的唯一途径。我们通过Plan来研究这一点，这是一种结构化的多跳检索代理行为，它在任何检索之前将问题分解为有序的子问题，从而使每一步搜索可以锚定在预先设计的子问题上，而不是在先前检索的部分相关文档的影响下漂移。然而，在参数从3B到14B的三种模型系列中，我们发现相同的奖励信号会导致定性不同的强化学习失败模式。这一现象表明，成功训练不仅依赖于奖励设计，还依赖于模型特定的可行性条件：足够的初始熵、训练稳定性和先决子技能。受此启发，我们提出了一种自举范式，其中一个小规模种子模型生成过滤后的轨迹，以在任何目标模型中激活Plan，从而消除了从外部更强模型蒸馏的需要。我们的流程在每个测试模型中均激活了Plan，并在多跳问答基准测试中持续优于竞争基线。

Original abstract: Training large language models as retrieval-augmented reasoning agents typically combines reinforcement learning with an SFT cold start distilled from a stronger model. However, this paradigm overlooks two fundamental factors: the dependency structure among sub-skills, and the possibility that distillation is not the only route to capability acquisition. We study this through Plan, a structured agentic behavior for multi-hop retrieval that decomposes a question into ordered sub-questions before any retrieval is performed, so that each search step can be anchored to a pre-designed sub-question instead of drifting under the influence of partially relevant documents retrieved earlier. However, across three model families spanning 3B to 14B parameters, we find that an identical reward signal induces qualitatively different RL failure modes. This phenomenon indicates that successful training hinges not only on reward design but also on model-specific feasibility conditions: sufficient initial entropy, training stability, and prerequisite sub-skills. Motivated by this, we propose a self-bootstrapping paradigm in which a small-scale seed model generates filtered trajectories that activate Plan in any target model, eliminating the need for distillation from an external stronger model. Our pipeline activates Plan across every tested model and consistently outperforms competitive baselines on multi-hop QA benchmarks.

</details>


### [55] [From Knowing to Doing: A Memory-Controlled Benchmark for LLM Trading Agents on Stock Markets](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28359v1)
*Taojie Zhu,Wentao Zhao,Rui Sun,Beidi Luan,Jiacheng Lu,Sinuo Wang,Jing Li,Daxin Jiang,Yonghong He,Zuo Bai*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出LLM交易agent的benchmark，包含记忆控制和归因评估，对agent评测有参考价值。

TL;DR: KTD-Fin基准通过数据掩码和Barra归因解决LLM交易评估中的记忆泄露和收益来源问题，发现前沿LLM智能体在沪深300上的收益主要由被动市场和风格暴露解释，选股阿尔法不显著。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM交易评估存在两个缺陷：长回测与LLM知识截止日期重叠导致记忆替代推理，以及原始收益无法区分真实选股能力与市场运气。需要设计更严谨的评估方法。

Method: 提出KTD-Fin基准，包含数据侧掩码协议（匿名化股票代码、日期等标识符）和Barra风格归因框架，将收益分解为市场、风格和选股阿尔法三个成分。

Result: 在十个前沿LLM智能体上的实验表明，掩码显著改变了智能体的推理依据，使其转向因子分析；归因分析显示，累积收益主要来自市场和风格暴露，持续选股阿尔法证据有限。

Conclusion: 金融LLM基准不应仅关注收益高低，更需评估收益来源是否体现可转移的投资技能；KTD-Fin提供了一个可复现的泄露控制和归因感知评估模板。

中文摘要：评估大型语言模型（LLM）智能体能否在资本市场盈利，越来越多地被构建为端到端交易：将智能体置于历史市场中，让其交易，并衡量投资组合收益。这种设置容易受到两种评估失败的影响。首先，长回测通常与前沿LLM的知识截止日期重叠，使得记忆的股票代码、日期、价格和市场叙事能够替代投资推理。其次，原始收益是选股能力的噪声代理，因为正收益可能来自市场贝塔、风格暴露或有利的市场环境，而不是真正的阿尔法。我们引入了KTD-Fin（Knowing-To-Doing Financial Benchmark），一个端到端的股票市场交易基准，解决了这两个问题。KTD-Fin使用数据侧掩码协议，在提示和工具中一致地匿名化关键标识符和日历信息，将历史市场记忆与投资决策分开。它还整合了一个Barra风格的表现归因框架，将投资组合收益分解为市场、风格和选股阿尔法组成部分。在2024-2026年中国沪深300指数上评估的十个前沿LLM智能体中，掩码显著改变了智能体的推理过程，推动它们转向匿名化因子推理。归因分析进一步表明，在泄露控制评估下，LLM智能体的累积收益在很大程度上由被动的市场和风格暴露解释，持续选股阿尔法的证据有限。这些发现表明，金融LLM基准不仅应评估智能体是否赚钱，还应评估收益来源是否反映了可转移的投资技能。我们发布KTD-Fin作为LLM交易智能体的泄露控制和归因感知评估的可复现模板。

Original abstract: Evaluating whether large language model (LLM) agents can profit in capital markets is increasingly framed as end-to-end trading: place an agent in a historical market, let it trade, and measure portfolio returns. This setup is vulnerable to two evaluation failures. First, long backtests often overlap with the knowledge cutoffs of frontier LLMs, allowing memorized tickers, dates, prices, and market narratives to substitute for investment reasoning. Second, raw returns are a noisy proxy for stock-selection ability, since positive performance may come from market beta, style exposure, or favorable regimes rather than genuine alpha.
  We introduce KTD-Fin (Knowing-To-Doing Financial Benchmark), an end-to-end stock-market trading benchmark that addresses both issues. KTD-Fin uses a data-side masking protocol to anonymize key identifiers and calendar information consistently across prompts and tools, separating historical market memory from investment decision-making. It also incorporates a Barra-style performance attribution framework that decomposes portfolio returns into market, style, and stock-selection alpha components.
  Across ten frontier LLM agents evaluated on the Chinese CSI300 over a 2024--2026 window, masking substantially changes agent rationales, pushing them towards anonymized factor-based reasoning. Attribution analysis further shows that LLM agents' cumulative returns under leakage-controlled evaluation are largely explained by passive market and style exposure, with limited evidence of persistent stock-selection alpha. These findings suggest that financial LLM benchmarks should evaluate not only whether an agent makes money, but also whether the source of returns reflects transferable investment skill. We release KTD-Fin as a reproducible template for leakage-controlled and attribution-aware evaluation of LLM trading agents.

</details>


### [56] [Prompt Codebooks: Discrete Compositional Optimization for Language Model Instruction Refinement](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28360v1)
*Jyotirmoy Nath,Neeraj Kumar,Brejesh Lall*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出离散组合式prompt优化框架，可提升LLM agent工作流的指令优化效率。

TL;DR: 提出Prompt Codebooks，通过离散码本和实例级路由实现组合式提示优化，显著提升性能并大幅缩短提示长度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自动提示优化方法将提示视为整体字符串进行全局编辑，导致更新脆弱且无法重用子行为。

Method: 构建离散码本存储原子指令单元；LLM编码器将输入路由到子集；生成器组合成提示；评判器提供文本梯度；在语言价值极小极大目标下联合训练。

Result: 在六个基准上相比零样本提升+30.36分，超越GEPA，提示长度减少14.1倍。

Conclusion: PCO通过实例级组合提示优化有效提升LLM性能并降低提示长度。

中文摘要：自动提示优化（APO）在基于LLM的智能体工作流中带来了显著提升。然而，现有方法将每个任务的提示视为一个整体的、实例无关的字符串，通过全局编辑进行优化，导致更新脆弱且无法重复利用学习到的子行为。我们提出提示码本（Prompt Codebooks, PCO），一种新颖的组合式提示优化框架，将APO重新定义为在有限的自然语言本能词汇表上的离散学习——这些本能是原子化的、可重复使用的指令单元。PCO将提示构建知识组织在离散码本中，并通过基于LLM的编码器将每个输入路由到一小部分条目；生成器将它们组合成冻结的目标模型的提示；评判器发出结构化判定，通过归因分解为每个变量提供文本梯度，在语言价值的极小极大目标下联合训练编码器、生成器和码本。最终的路由是逐个实例的：同一任务中的不同输入接收不同的本能组合，这种机制在实例无关的方法下在结构上是无法表达的。在Qwen3-8B和LLaMA-3.1-8B上的六个基准测试中，PCO相比零样本提升高达+30.36分，在HotpotQA上超过最强的先前基线（GEPA）+3.34，总体上超过+1.11，并且仅使用K=16个本能就将部署的提示长度相比MIPROv2减少了最多14.1倍，相比GEPA减少了3.0倍。

Original abstract: Automatic prompt optimization (APO) has driven significant gains in LLM-based agentic workflows. However, existing methods treat each task's prompt as a monolithic, instance-blind string optimized through global edits, producing brittle updates and preventing the reuse of learned sub-behaviors. We propose Prompt Codebooks (PCO), a novel compositional prompt optimization framework that recasts APO as discrete learning over a finite vocabulary of natural-language instincts - atomic, reusable instruction units. PCO organizes prompt-construction knowledge in a discrete codebook and routes each input to a small subset of entries via an LLM-based encoder; a generator composes them into a prompt for the frozen target model; a critic emits a structured verdict that decomposes by attribution into per-variable textual gradients, jointly training the encoder, generator, and codebook under a language-valued min-max objective. The resulting routing is per-instance: different inputs in the same task receive different instinct compositions, a regime structurally inexpressible under instance-blind methods. Across six benchmarks on Qwen3-8B and LLaMA-3.1-8B, PCO improves over zero-shot by up to +30.36 points, surpasses the strongest prior baseline (GEPA) by +3.34 on HotpotQA and +1.11 in aggregate, and reduces deployed prompt length by up to 14.1x versus MIPROv2 and 3.0x versus GEPA using only K=16 instincts.

### [57] [Risk-Controlled Lean-as-Judge for Natural-Language Mathematical Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28365v1)
*Pauline Bourigault,Xiaotong Ji,Matthieu Zimmer,Rasul Tutunov,Haitham Bou Ammar*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 风险控制的Lean验证方法用于数学推理，对agent结果验证和可靠推理有借鉴意义。

TL;DR: 评估Lean信号在评判数学答案时的可靠性和覆盖率依赖性，提出COVCAL选择器以控制风险。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Lean信号存在部分性、稀疏性和不忠实性，需要量化其可靠性并开发风险控制方法。

Method: 在MATH-500上分析Lean信号覆盖率和忠实度，提出COVCAL选择器，采用Bonferroni和dev-then-cal两种风险控制规则。

Result: 7B形式化器覆盖率低导致信号不可靠，专用形式化器提高覆盖率后COVCAL可行，接受48%问题且准确率0.98。

Conclusion: 精确描述了在何种条件下可以信任部分形式化信号。

中文摘要：Lean 越来越多地被用于评判自然语言数学答案，但其信号是不完全的：许多答案从未被形式化，而失败的证明可能反映的是类型错误的陈述或缺失的库事实，而不是错误的答案。在 MATH-500 上，我们展示了该信号 (i) 严重依赖于覆盖率，即在高的证明覆盖率下，证明获胜的答案有 96% 的正确率，但在低覆盖率下只有 20%，以及 (ii) 稀疏且常常不忠实：一个 7B 的自动形式化器仅能证明 28% 的问题，而人工审计发现只有大约 43% 的证明是忠实的。我们提出了 COVCAL，这是一个基于 Lean 跟踪诊断的选择器，它对接受的答案认证一个有限样本的选择性风险界限，或选择弃权，采用两种机制（保守的 Bonferroni 界限和更严格的 dev-then-cal 规则）。可行性取决于自动形式化覆盖率：使用 7B 形式化器时，信号过于稀疏，Bonferroni 在所有 20 个自举分区上都弃权，而一个证明器专用的形式化器达到了 79% 的覆盖率，并在 20 个分区中的 17 个上使之可行，接受了大约 48% 的问题，接受的准确率为 0.98。由于自一致性本身已达到 91% 的准确率，我们的贡献是精确地描述了何时以及使用哪种形式化器，部分形式化信号可以在风险控制下被信任。

Original abstract: Lean is increasingly used to judge natural-language mathematical answers, but its signal is partial: many answers never formalize, and a failed proof may reflect an ill-typed statement or a missing library fact, not a wrong answer. On MATH-500 we show this signal is (i) sharply coverage-dependent, that is the proof-winning answer is correct 96% of the time at high proved coverage but 20% at low, and (ii) sparse and often unfaithful: a 7B autoformalizer proves a class for only 28% of problems, and a manual audit finds only approximately 43% of those proofs faithful. We propose COVCAL, a selector over Lean-trace diagnostics that certifies a finite-sample selective-risk bound on accepted answers or abstains, under two regimes (a conservative Bonferroni bound and a tighter dev-then-cal rule). Feasibility depends on autoformalization coverage: with the 7B formalizer the signal is too sparse and Bonferroni abstains on all 20 bootstrap partitions, whereas a prover-specialized formalizer reaches 79% coverage and flips it to feasible on 17 of 20, accepting approximately 48% of problems at 0.98 accepted accuracy. Since self-consistency alone is already 91% accurate, our contribution is a precise account of when, and with which formalizer, a partial formal signal can be trusted under risk control.

</details>


### [58] [CyberJurors: A Multi-Agent Simulation Task for E-Commerce Disputes Verdict](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28369v1)
*Yanhui Sun,Wu Liu,Haifeng Ming,Xinru Wang,Hantao Yao,Yongdong Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出多agent模拟任务用于电商纠纷裁决，涉及多agent协作与共识机制。

TL;DR: 提出电商纠纷裁决任务EDV、多模态基准VerdictBench和多智能体框架CyberJurors，通过个体推理链和集体共识模拟提升裁决与真实陪审团投票的一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法无法处理电商纠纷裁决中冗余、多轮、多模态证据以及灵活平台惯例的挑战，亟需专门任务和模型。

Method: CyberJurors包含个体级Individual Verdict Chain-of-Thought（四阶段推理）和集体级Jury Consensus Verdict（多轮讨论投票+先例引入）。

Result: 在VerdictBench上，CyberJurors超越SOTA LLM、MLLM和法院模拟器，并与真实陪审团投票模式高度对齐。

Conclusion: CyberJurors有效解决了电商纠纷裁决任务，提供的数据集和基准可推动该领域研究。

中文摘要：电子商务平台已开始招募众包陪审员来裁决大量的交易纠纷。与正式的法律判决不同，电商纠纷裁决需要从冗余、多轮、多模态的证据中提取关键线索，并在灵活的平台特定惯例下做出决策。这些特征使得现有方法不足以应对该场景。为填补这一空白，我们引入了一项开创性任务——电商纠纷裁决（EDV），并提出了VerdictBench，一个包含6000个真实案例的多模态基准，旨在反映众包陪审团的决策。在此基础上，我们提出CyberJurors，一个多智能体框架，用于理清纠纷逻辑并规范裁决过程。在个体层面，个体裁决思维链（Individual Verdict Chain-of-Thought）将EDV任务分解为四个结构化推理阶段，实现细粒度线索感知并理清关键线索与纠纷焦点的因果逻辑。在集体层面，陪审团共识裁决（Jury Consensus Verdict）模拟陪审员之间的多轮讨论和投票，同时引入裁决先例以减轻对任一纠纷方的认知偏差。在VerdictBench上的实验表明，CyberJurors优于最先进的LLM、MLLM和法院模拟器，同时与真实世界陪审团投票模式实现更强的对齐。代码和数据集可在https://github.com/YanhuiS/CyberJurors和https://huggingface.co/datasets/piggi/VerdictBench获取。

Original abstract: E-commerce platforms have begun recruiting crowdsourced jurors to adjudicate massive volumes of transaction disputes. Unlike formal legal judgment, E-commerce dispute verdicts require grounding pivotal clues from redundant, multi-round, multimodal evidence and making decisions under flexible platform-specific conventions. These characteristics render existing methods insufficient for this scenario. To bridge this gap, we introduce a pioneering task, E-commerce Dispute Verdicts (EDV), and present VerdictBench, a multimodal benchmark comprising 6,000 real-world cases designed to reflect crowdsourced jury decisions. Building upon this, we propose CyberJurors, a multi-agent framework to clarify the dispute logic and regulate the verdict process. At the individual level, Individual Verdict Chain-of-Thought decomposes the EDV task into four structured reasoning stages, enabling fine-grained clue perception and clarifying causal logic between pivotal clues and the dispute focus. At the collective level, Jury Consensus Verdict simulates multi-round discussion and voting among jurors, while incorporating verdict precedents to mitigate cognitive biases toward either disputant. Experiments on VerdictBench show that CyberJurors outperforms state-of-the-art LLMs, MLLMs, and court simulators, while achieving stronger alignment with real-world jury voting patterns. Code and dataset are available at https://github.com/YanhuiS/CyberJurors and https://huggingface.co/datasets/piggi/VerdictBench.

</details>


### [59] [From paper to benchmark: agentic, framework-based reproduction of under-specified methods in machine health intelligence](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28371v1)

TL;DR: 提出一种基于代理和共享框架的PHM论文复现方法，通过槽位绑定接口将论文转化为可比较的基准测试实现。

Result: 在16篇PHM论文上评估，框架增强的代理复现相比无框架代理在复现成功率、模型代码评估、假设绑定和跨论文基准可比性上表现更好，将论文复现从孤立代码合成转变为可执行、假设感知且系统可比较的实现。

Conclusion: 将代理生成与共享框架相结合，能够将论文复现从孤立的代码合成转变为可执行的、假设感知的、系统可比较的基准测试实现。

Original abstract: Industrial Prognostics and Health Management (PHM) provides a representative case study for a broader challenge in applied machine learning: translating published papers into executable, benchmark-ready implementations. Reproducing under-specified methods in PHM is particularly difficult due to restricted access to industrial datasets, incomplete reporting of preprocessing and evaluation protocols, and implicit design choices (e.g., windowing, target construction, data splits) that critically affect performance. Existing paper-to-code systems generate implementations for individual papers, but these artifacts are often not directly comparable due to inconsistencies in assumptions and evaluation settings. We introduce \emph{agentic, framework-based PHM paper reproduction}, where an agent translates a paper into a shared PHM benchmark framework via a \emph{slot-binding interface}. This interface maps equations and protocol descriptions into structured components (task definitions, dataset adapters, windowing, targets, models, and evaluators), while explicitly recording unresolved assumptions. The resulting implementations are validated against standardized task contracts and evaluation hooks, enabling consistent and comparable benchmarking. We evaluate this approach on 16 PHM papers, comparing framework-enhanced, skill-based and prompt-based agentic reproduction against a recent framework-free paper-reproduction agent. We assess reproduction success, model-based code evaluation, framework binding of paper assumptions, and cross-paper benchmark comparability under standardized protocols. Our results show that coupling agentic generation with a shared framework transforms paper reproduction from isolated code synthesis into executable, assumption-aware, and systematically comparable benchmark implementations.

### [60] [Mechanistically Interpreting the Role of Sample Difficulty in RLVR for LLMs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28388v1)
*Yue Cheng,Jiajun Zhang,Xiaohui Gao,Weiwei Xing,Zheng Wang,Zhanxing Zhu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 研究样本难度在RLVR中对LLM推理的影响，可迁移到代码生成agent的训练策略。

TL;DR: 本文通过难度分析和内部特征动态研究，发现样本难度非单调影响RLVR性能，并据此提出难度自适应策略以优化困难样本的利用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管RLVR已被证明能提升LLM推理性能，但样本难度在其中的机制性作用尚不明确，因此我们旨在揭示难度如何影响RLVR的优化与表征演化。

Method: 采用难度维度和单样本分析，结合T-SAE（时域稀疏自编码器）分析模型内部特征动态，并基于发现提出难度自适应策略（反向推理重构和T-SAE引导的训练信号）。

Result: 发现简单和中等难度问题带来最强提升，而困难问题导致弱信号和退化行为；内部特征分析显示不同难度激活不同的特征模式；提出的自适应策略可改善困难样本的利用。

Conclusion: 样本难度是控制RLVR优化动力学和表征演化的关键因素，难度自适应策略能有效提升RLVR在困难样本上的效果。

中文摘要：带可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）在经验上被证明能显著提升大型语言模型（LLM）的推理性能，尤其是在数学和编程方面。然而，样本难度在RLVR中的机制性作用仍知之甚少。本文通过难度维度和单样本分析的视角研究RLVR。我们发现样本难度对RLVR具有非单调效应：简单和中等难度的问题带来最强且最稳定的推理提升，而过难的问题往往提供微弱的学习信号，诱发退化行为（如重复答案或跳过必要的计算），并最终损害模型已有的能力。除了响应的表面现象，我们进一步利用时域稀疏自编码器（T-SAE）分析模型的内部特征动态。简单问题主要强化直接答案和基础计算特征，同时抑制审慎推理特征；困难问题激活推理相关特征，但仅当采样到成功轨迹时才变得有用；中等难度问题提供更平衡的信号，同时加强计算和多步推理特征。受这些发现启发，我们提出了针对困难样本利用的难度自适应策略，使用反向推理重构和T-SAE引导的训练信号来改善RLVR中的奖励密度和信用分配。总体而言，我们的结果将样本难度识别为控制RLVR优化动力学和表征演化的关键因素。

Original abstract: Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Reward (RLVR) is empirically shown to notably enhance the reasoning performance of large language models (LLMs), particularly in mathematics and programming. However, the mechanistic role of Sample Difficulty in RLVR remains poorly understood. In this paper, we investigate RLVR through the lens of difficulty-wise and one-sample analysis. We find that sample difficulty has a non-monotonic effect on RLVR: easy and medium-difficulty problems yield the strongest and most stable reasoning improvements, whereas overly hard problems often provide weak learning signals, induce degenerate behaviors such as answer repetition or skipping necessary computation, and can ultimately degrade the model's pre-existing capabilities. Beyond the obverse of response, we further analyze the model's internal feature dynamics using Temporal Sparse Autoencoders (T-SAE). Easy problems mainly reinforce direct-answer and basic-computation features while suppressing deliberative-reasoning features; hard problems activate reasoning-related features but become useful only when successful trajectories are sampled; medium-difficulty problems provide a more balanced signal, strengthening both computation and multi-step reasoning features. Motivated by these findings, we propose difficulty-adaptive strategies for hard-sample utilization, using backward-reasoning reformulation and T-SAE-guided training signals to improve reward density and credit assignment during RLVR. Overall, our results identify sample difficulty as a key factor governing both the optimization dynamics and representation evolution of RLVR.

Original abstract: Test-time skill evolving is regarded as a new paradigm for enhancing deployed agentic systems. Existing works mainly focus on hard-coded skill evolving strategies or parametric learning that rely on expensive parameter updates in the underlying LLMs. In this paper, we demonstrate that test-time refinement of the skill evolving framework itself is necessary for continuous improvement of the agent systems in different downstream scenarios, and lightweight algorithmic adaptation is feasible. Specifically, we propose HiSME, a lightweight hierarchical skill meta-evolving solution that jointly optimizes skills and the skill evolving strategy by learning meta-skills from agents' task execution traces. Experiments on diverse agentic benchmarks show that meta-evolving can produce a higher-quality skill library than pure skill evolving and can derive diverse meta-skills for different scenarios, thereby facilitating future continual experience learning.
