### [94] [Governing Technical Debt in Agentic AI Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29129v2)
*Muhammad Zia Hydari,Raja Iqbal,Narayan Ramasubbu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 代理AI系统技术债务管理，对agent系统工程有参考价值。

TL;DR: 本文定义了代理型技术债务和随机税，并提出了通过轻量级仪表板和治理控制来管理这些负债和运营成本的方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 代理型AI系统带来的治理挑战超出了传统软件或预测性ML技术债务的范畴，因此需要定义并可视化新的债务形式和运营成本。

Method: 作者定义了代理型技术债务和随机税，并概述了使用轻量级仪表板和治理控制来追踪它们的方法。

Result: 提供了代理型技术债务和随机税的正式定义，并说明了管理者如何使这些概念可见。

Conclusion: 通过区分债务和税，并利用仪表板，组织可以更好地管理随机代理系统的负债和运营成本。

中文摘要：代理型人工智能系统正越来越多地被探索作为生产基础设施：它们进行多步推理、调用工具、通过工作流行动，并通过记忆和反馈适应。这些系统带来了传统软件或预测性机器学习技术债务无法完全捕捉的治理挑战。我们将代理型技术债务定义为当提示词、记忆、工具模式、编排图、控制策略和可观测性例程被拼凑在一起的速度超过它们被验证、标准化和治理的速度时累积的负债。我们将随机税定义为将概率性代理行为保持在可接受范围内所产生的重复性运营负担。这一区别很重要：债务是设计和治理负债的存量，而税是由随机代理通过工具和工作流行动产生的运营成本流。我们概述了管理者如何通过轻量级仪表板和治理控制使这两者变得可见。

Original abstract: Agentic AI systems are increasingly being explored as production infrastructure: they reason over multiple steps, call tools, act through workflows, and adapt through memory and feedback. These systems create governance challenges that are not fully captured by traditional software or predictive ML technical debt. We define Agentic Technical Debt as the accumulated liability created when prompts, memory, tool schemas, orchestration graphs, control policies, and observability routines are patched together faster than they can be validated, standardized, and governed. We define Stochastic Tax as the recurring operating burden of keeping probabilistic agent behavior within acceptable bounds. The distinction matters: debt is a stock of design and governance liability, while the tax is a flow of operating cost that arises because stochastic agents act through tools and workflows. We outline how managers can make both visible through lightweight dashboards and governance controls.

</details>


<div id='astro-ph.IM'></div>

# astro-ph.IM [[Back]](#toc)

### [95] [First head-to-head comparison of agentic AI applied to the analysis of simulated data of the Einstein Telescope](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28916v2)
*Gianluca Inguglia*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

Selection reason: agentic AI系统头对头比较，为coding agent行为分析提供实证。

TL;DR: 比较Claude Code和Codex两个AI代理自主执行引力波数据分析流程，发现Claude Code更快但存在无声偏差，Codex更慢但更透明，两者在指令解释上产生科学分歧。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 评估和比较当前最先进的代理型AI系统在科学计算工作流中的自主行为、可靠性和透明度，以指导它们在科研中的应用。

Method: 设计一个引力波数据分析流程，包括功率谱估计、模板库生成、匹配滤波、结果生成和手稿撰写，将相同任务分配给Claude Code和Codex，给定相同规范和计算资源，运行两次（不同信噪比），记录行为、成本及结果差异。

Result: Claude Code在3.4分钟内完成但存在无声偏差，Codex在16分钟内完成且更透明；第二次运行中因指令解释差异导致科学分歧；自动生成手稿质量不同。

Conclusion: 代理型AI在科学任务中表现出速度与可审计性、错误处理方式、指令解释等权衡，需关注中间数据表示和透明性，以确保可靠部署。

中文摘要：我们报告了两种最先进的代理型AI系统——Claude Code（Anthropic）和Codex（OpenAI）的比较，它们被任务自主执行一个简单的端到端引力波数据分析流程，在共享计算基础设施上无需人工干预。该流程包括从模拟的爱因斯坦望远镜原始噪声中估计功率谱密度、生成几何模板库、匹配滤波恢复100个双黑洞信号注入、自动结果生成以及大语言模型辅助生成格式符合《物理评论D》风格的手稿。两个代理都收到相同的书面规范和相同的计算资源。实验进行了两次：第一次使用不切实际的高信噪比注入，第二次将信号缩放到物理合理的信噪比范围。两次运行的科学结果均收敛。然而，代理表现出截然不同的行为和计算成本：Claude Code在约3.4分钟内完成流程，但存在与规范不符的无声偏差；而Codex则需要约16分钟，包括显式的自我纠正重启，以及对匹配滤波内循环进行了未经请求的性能优化。自动生成的手稿在长度、细节和质量上也有差异。在第二次运行中，对信噪比范围指令解释的细微差异导致了真正的科学分歧：Claude Code无声地重新解释了指令，而Codex严格按照规范执行。我们讨论了这些行为差异（如速度与可审计性、无声与透明的错误处理、指令解释以及多模型流程中中间数据表示的关键性）对科学计算工作流中部署代理型AI的影响。

Original abstract: We report a comparison of two state-of-the-art agentic AI systems, Claude Code (Anthropic) and Codex (OpenAI), tasked with autonomously executing a simple end-to-end gravitational wave data analysis pipeline on a shared computing infrastructure without human intervention. The pipeline comprises power spectral density estimation from raw Einstein Telescope simulated noise, geometric template bank generation, matched filter recovery of 100 binary black hole signal injections, automated results generation, and large language model-assisted production of a manuscript formatted in the style of Physical Review D. Both agents received identical written specifications and identical compute resources. The experiment was run twice: a first run with unrealistically loud injections, and a second run with signals rescaled to a physically motivated SNR range. The scientific results converged in both runs. However, the agents exhibited substantially different behaviors and computational costs: Claude Code completed the pipeline in ~3.4 minutes with silent deviations from the specification, while Codex required ~16 minutes across explicit self-correcting restarts, including an unsolicited performance optimization of the matched filter inner loop. The autonomously generated manuscripts also diverged in length, details, and quality. In the second run, a subtle difference in the interpretation of the SNR range instruction led to a genuine scientific divergence: Claude Code silently reinterpreted the instructions, while Codex followed the specification literally. We discuss the implications of these behavioral differences, such as speed versus auditability, silent versus transparent error handling, instruction interpretation, and the criticality of intermediate data representations in multi-model pipelines, for the deployment of agentic AI in scientific computing workflows.

</details>

### [96] [Verified Misguidance: Measuring Structural Citation Failures in Search-Augmented LLMs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28565v1)
*Yongsik Seo,Wooseok Jeong,Eunyoung Kim,Hyeonseo Jang,Dongha Lee*

Main category: cs.DL

Selection reason: 检索增强LLM引用可靠性评测，涉及工具使用与可信性，对agent工具使用评测有参考价值

TL;DR: 构建了CITETRACE数据集和三维评估框架，发现搜索增强LLM存在系统性引用误导模式（已验证的误导），30.6%引用扭曲源，提供商差异主导引用质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准孤立评估引用质量，缺乏联合结构；引用质量决定用户是否被误导，需要全面诊断结构性引用失败。

Method: 构建CITETRACE数据集（11,200查询，112,000响应，761,495引用对），设计三维评估框架（意图对齐、源适用性、答案-源忠实度），并大规模应用分析。

Result: 发现已验证的误导模式：30.6%引用扭曲源，27.1%源不适用，96%用户遇到误导性引用；提供商差异解释88-96%的引用质量方差。

Conclusion: CITETRACE和评估框架提供了首个资源，用于诊断部署的搜索增强系统中的结构性引用失败。

中文摘要：用户依赖搜索增强型LLM的引用作为证据，但很少验证被引页面本身。每天数百万查询通过这些系统，引用质量成为用户被信息告知或被误导的无声决定因素——然而现有基准各自孤立地处理一个方面，忽略了决定引用可信度的联合结构。我们构建了CITETRACE，一个大规模数据集，追踪从用户查询到检索源再到生成答案的完整引用链：来自28个社区的11,200个真实查询，与来自五个提供商的十个模型的112,000个响应配对，产生761,495个可评估的引用对。我们设计了一个三维评估框架，对每个引用进行意图-目的对齐、源适用性和答案-源忠实度评分，使用专家验证的预定义矩阵和五级忠实度准则；该框架适用于任何产生带引用响应的系统。大规模应用该框架，我们发现一个系统性的模式，称为“已验证的误导”（VM）：模型引用真实、可访问的源，但未能满足一个或多个维度，产生忠实度-适用性权衡，即忠实模型选择不合适的源，反之亦然。在我们的池中，30.6%的引用扭曲了其源，27.1%的引用来自领域不合适的源；在响应级别，高达96%的用户至少遇到一个结构上误导性的引用。提供商级别的差异解释了88-96%的引用质量方差，表明源选择更多受个体模型能力以外的因素控制，而非LLM本身。总之，CITETRACE及其评估框架提供了首个用于诊断部署的搜索增强系统中结构性引用失败的资源。

Original abstract: Users of search-augmented LLMs rely on citations as evidence that responses are grounded in real sources, and rarely verify the cited pages themselves. Millions of queries per day now pass through these systems, making citation quality a silent determinant of whether users are informed or misled-yet existing benchmarks each address one facet in isolation, leaving the joint structure that determines citation trustworthiness unmeasured. We construct CITETRACE, a large-scale dataset that traces the full citation chain from user query through retrieved source to generated answer: 11,200 real-world queries from 28 communities paired with 112,000 responses from ten models across five providers, yielding 761,495 evaluable citation pairs. We design a three-dimension evaluation framework that scores each citation on intent-purpose alignment, source suitability, and answer-source fidelity, using expert-validated predefined matrices and a five-level fidelity rubric; the framework applies to any system that produces citation-bearing responses. Applying this framework at scale, we identify a systematic pattern we call VERIFIED MISGUIDANCE (VM): models cite real, accessible sources yet fail along one or more dimensions, producing a fidelity-suitability trade-off in which faithful models select inappropriate sources and vice versa. Across our pool, 30.6% of citations distort their sources and 27.1% originate from domain-inappropriate sources; at the response level, up to 96% of users encounter at least one structurally misleading citation. Provider-level differences explain 88-96% of citation-quality variance, suggesting that source selection is governed more by factors beyond individual model capability than by the LLMs themselves. Together, CITETRACE and its evaluation framework provide the first resource for diagnosing structural citation failures in deployed search-augmented systems.

</details>

### [97] [SPAR: Support-Preserving Action Rectification](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27877v1)
*Jiaxin Zhao,Weihang Pan,Xun Liang,Binbin Lin*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 离线强化学习方法，可迁移至agent策略优化和技能学习。

TL;DR: 提出SPAR方法，通过局部残差纠正和潜在自模仿机制，解决离线策略改进中的过保守和梯度冲突问题，实现最先进性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 离线策略改进存在最大化价值与拟合数据分布的矛盾：样本内加权回归过保守，梯度方法有拟合-优化冲突。

Method: 将全局学习转为局部残差纠正（SPAR），结合潜在自模仿的加权回归机制，消除流形法向漂移。

Result: D4RL实验显示SPAR从次优基线提取显著收益，达到最先进性能。

Conclusion: SPAR有效解决了离线策略改进中的关键矛盾，理论证明消除梯度漂移，实验验证性能优越。

中文摘要：离线策略改进面临最大化价值与拟合数据分布之间的固有矛盾。虽然样本内加权回归是稳定的，但它存在过度保守的问题，抑制了分布尾部的高价值动作；相反，基于梯度的方法通常表现出梯度的拟合-优化冲突，这会将策略推向数据流形之外。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了支持保持动作纠正（SPAR），它将全局学习重新定义为锚定在冻结的纯行为克隆策略上的局部残差纠正。该框架在残差空间中进行细粒度拟合和局部策略改进，从而压缩搜索空间。我们进一步引入了潜在自模仿，利用潜在采样加权回归机制来解决残差空间中的拟合-改进梯度冲突。理论上，我们证明了该机制消除了标准值梯度的流形法向漂移，而广泛的D4RL实验表明，SPAR从次优基线中提取显著收益，实现了最先进的性能。

Original abstract: Offline policy improvement faces an inherent conflict between maximizing value and fitting the data distribution. While in-sample weighted regression is stable, it suffers from over-conservatism that suppresses high-value actions in the distribution tail; conversely, gradient-based approaches often exhibit a fitting-optimization conflict of gradients, which drives the policy off the data manifold. To address this, we propose Support-Preserving Action Rectification (SPAR), which reframes global learning as a local residual rectification anchored to a frozen pure behavior cloning policy. This framework performs fine-grained fitting and local policy improvement in the residual space, thereby contracting the search space. We further introduce Latent Self-Imitation, utilizing a latent-sampling weighted-regression mechanism to address fitting-improvement gradient conflict in the residual space. Theoretically, we prove this mechanism eliminates the manifold-normal drift of standard value gradients, while extensive D4RL experiments show SPAR extracts significant gains from suboptimal baselines to achieve state-of-the-art performance.

</details>


### [98] [Context Distillation as Latent Memory Management](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28889v1)
*Ziyang Zheng,Zeju Li,Xiangyu Wen,Jianyuan Zhong,Junhua Huang,Lei Chen,Mingxuan Yuan,Qiang Xu*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 将上下文蒸馏建模为潜在记忆管理，模块化LoRA适配器、检索与门控机制，是通用agent记忆方法，可迁移。

TL;DR: 将上下文蒸馏建模为潜在记忆管理问题，通过独立LoRA适配器构成模块化记忆库，结合检索、路由和自门控机制实现安全激活，并用缓存共享提升效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有上下文蒸馏方法忽略了多个蒸馏记忆在非oracle设置下的存储、检索和安全激活问题。

Method: 将每个上下文蒸馏为独立LoRA适配器形成模块化记忆库；查询时检索候选记忆并路由到最适配器，使用自门控机制决定是否激活；引入缓存共享降低推理开销。

Result: 在检索任务上显著优于基线，自门控通过停用无关记忆提升了鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 提出的框架有效解决了多个潜在记忆的管理和激活问题，提升了性能与鲁棒性。

中文摘要：上下文蒸馏将上下文信息压缩到模型参数中，然而现有方法常常忽略在非oracle设置下如何存储、检索和安全激活多个蒸馏后的潜在记忆。我们将上下文蒸馏表述为一个潜在记忆管理问题。我们将每个上下文蒸馏成一个独立的LoRA适配器，形成一个模块化记忆库，从而能够进行显式的记忆选择。给定一个查询，我们的框架检索候选记忆，将查询路由到最合适的适配器，并使用自门控机制来决定是否应激活潜在记忆。为了提高效率，我们进一步引入缓存共享以减少推理过程中的管理开销。实验表明，我们的方法在检索方面显著优于基线，而自门控通过停用不必要的潜在记忆提高了鲁棒性。

Original abstract: Context distillation compresses contextual information into model parameters, yet existing methods often ignore how multiple distilled latent memories should be stored, retrieved, and safely activated in non-oracle settings. We formulate context distillation as a latent memory management problem. We distill each context into an independent LoRA adapter, forming a modular memory bank that enables explicit memory selection. Given a query, our framework retrieves candidate memories, routes the query to the most suitable adapter, and uses a Self-Gating mechanism to decide whether latent memory should be activated. To improve efficiency, we further introduce cache sharing to reduce management overhead during inference. Experiments show that our method substantially outperforms baselines with retrieval, while Self-Gating improves robustness by deactivate unnecessary latent memories.

</details>


### [99] [How Far Can Disaggregation Go? A Design-Space Exploration of Attention-FFN Disaggregation for Efficient MoE LLM Serving](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28302v1)
*Hanjiang Wu,Abhimanyu Rajeshkumar Bambhaniya,Sarbartha Banerjee,Tuhin Khare,Sudarshan Srinivasan,Suvinay Subramanian,Souvik Kundu,Madhu Kumar,Midhilesh Elavazhagan,William Won,Amir Yazdanbakhsh,Tushar Krishna*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 探讨MoE模型推理的Attention-FFN分离架构，为agent部署中高效推理提供系统设计思路。

TL;DR: 系统分析了MoE模型中不同解耦级别的权衡，证明在严格延迟要求下注意力-FFN解耦（AFD）可实现4k tokens/s吞吐量，且非AFD方案不可行，并给出了资源划分设计原则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM推理解耦趋势日益深入，但不同解耦级别（分块预填充、P/D解耦、AFD）在MoE模型中的实际收益尚不明确，需要系统研究何时采用何种解耦级别。

Method: 通过融合设备上内核测量与高保真网络模拟的框架，以分块预填充和P/D解耦为基线，在实际工作负载（不同序列长度、前缀KV重用、延迟约束）下对比分析AFD的性能。

Result: 在严格TTFT/TPOT SLO下，AFD在DeepSeek-V3.2上针对聊天、编码等任务维持约4k tokens/s系统吞吐量，而非AFD部署不可行；同时给出注意力与FFN的GPU划分策略。

Conclusion: AFD对于满足严格的延迟SLO和大吞吐量需求是必要的；未来解耦AI基础设施应基于工作负载和模型架构动态调整注意力与FFN的GPU分配。

中文摘要：现代大语言模型（LLM）推理已逐步解耦，以跟上不断增长的模型规模和严格的TTFT和TPOT服务级别目标：从分块预填充聚合，到预填充-解码（P/D）解耦，再到最近的操作符级别的注意力-FFN解耦（AFD）。这一趋势对于混合专家（MoE）模型尤为重要，其中内存受限的注意力、计算密集的专家FFN以及MoE调度/组合通信产生了不同的资源需求。AFD通过将注意力和MoE-FFN执行置于单独的GPU组上，进一步暴露了这种异构性。每个解耦级别都加深了调度设计空间，涉及工作负载特征、资源分配和互连拓扑，引发了一个核心问题：每个级别在何时真正值得？我们系统地描述了MoE推理在跨输入/输出序列长度、前缀KV重用和每用户延迟约束的实际工作负载下的这种权衡。以分块预填充和P/D解耦为基线，我们通过一个融合设备上内核测量与高保真网络模拟的框架，研究了AFD在大规模下的优势和限制。在严格的TTFT/TPOT SLO下，AFD在DeepSeek-V3.2上针对聊天、编码和智能体编码工作负载维持了约4k tokens/s的系统吞吐量，而在非AFD部署中这是不可行的。我们提炼出具体要点，用于联合优化吞吐量和交互性，包括如何根据工作负载和模型架构在GPU之间划分注意力和FFN，为当前的机架级和集群级部署以及未来的解耦AI基础设施提供设计原则。

Original abstract: Modern large language model (LLM) inference has progressively disaggregated to keep pace with growing model sizes and tight TTFT and TPOT service-level objectives: from chunked-prefill aggregation, to prefill-decode (P/D) disaggregation, and most recently to operator-level Attention-FFN Disaggregation (AFD). This trend is especially important for mixture-of-experts (MoE) models, where memory-bound attention, compute-intensive expert FFNs, and MoE dispatch/combine communication create distinct resource demands. AFD further exposes this heterogeneity by placing attention and MoE-FFN execution on separate GPU groups. Each level of disaggregation deepens the scheduling design space across workload characteristics, resource allocation, and interconnect topology, raising the central question: when does each level actually pay off? We systematically characterize this trade-off for MoE inference across realistic workloads spanning input/output sequence lengths, prefix-KV reuse, and per-user latency constraints. Using chunked-prefill and P/D disaggregation as baselines, we study the benefits and limits of AFD at scale through a framework that fuses on-device kernel measurements with high-fidelity network simulation. Under strict TTFT/TPOT SLOs, AFD sustains around 4k tokens/s of system throughput on DeepSeek-V3.2 across chat, coding, and agentic-coding workloads, where non-AFD deployments are infeasible. We distill concrete takeaways for jointly optimizing throughput and interactivity, including how to partition attention and FFN across GPUs as a function of workload and model architecture, providing design principles for current rack- and cluster-scale deployments as well as future disaggregated AI infrastructure.

</details>


### [100] [Learning the Error Patterns of Language Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28328v1)
*Jinwoo Kim,Taylor Berg-KirkPatrick,Loris D'Antoni*

Main category: cs.LG

中文摘要：在为具有特定有效性约束的领域生成输出时（例如程序应能编译），LLM往往会在少数集中的方面失败：例如，在生成TypeScript时使用Python函数名。我们观察到这些错误模式可以用少量的约束来表示，这些约束在实践中可以学习。我们提出\emph{前缀过滤器}，它是每个领域和LLM的符号函数，作为捕获错误模式的对象；提出Palla算法，用于在实践中高效学习前缀过滤器，并实现了Palla。通过学习得到的Palla前缀过滤器能够：i）帮助我们定量分析LLM的错误模式；ii）可通过约束采样算法用于约束模型的输出。例如，Palla在TypeScript生成上将Qwen2.5-1.5B的编译率提高了超过60%，使得Qwen2.5-1.5B在无约束条件下达到与Llama3.1-8B相似的性能。

Original abstract: When generating outputs for domains with specific validity constraints (e.g., a program should compile), LLMs often fail in a small number of focused ways: for example, by using Python function names when generating TypeScript. We observe that these error patterns can be represented using a small number of constraints that can be learned in practice. We propose \emph{prefix filters}, which are per-domain-and-LLM symbolic functions, as objects to capture the error patterns, Palla as an algorithm to learn prefix filters efficiently in practice, and implement Palla. Prefix filters learned by Palla i) help us quantitatively analyze the error patterns of LLMs, and ii) can be used to constrain the outputs of a model via constrained sampling algorithms. For example, Palla boosts compile rates for Qwen2.5-1.5B on TypeScript generation, by over 60%, allowing Qwen2.5-1.5B to achieve similar performance to Llama3.1-8B unconstrained.

### [101] [ADWIN: Adaptive Windows for Horizon-Aware On-Policy Distillation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28396v1)
*Kun Liang,Chenming Tang,Clive Bai,Weijie Liu,Saiyong Yang,Yunfang Wu*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 提出自适应窗口的在线策略蒸馏方法，提升训练效率，可应用于代码生成模型的蒸馏训练。

TL;DR: 提出ADWIN框架，通过自适应调整训练展开长度，在在线策略蒸馏中大幅降低计算成本而不牺牲性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准全展开训练成本高，且过度关注后期低价值位置；需要更高效的训练方式。

Method: ADWIN自适应窗口框架，将展开长度作为在线决策，使用短教师锚定前缀训练并结合延迟全展开探测来调整视界。

Result: 在数学和代码推理任务中，相比全展开和前缀基线，训练成本降低4.1倍，准确率相当或更好。

Conclusion: ADWIN有效改善OPD的准确率-计算权衡，是一种高效实用的蒸馏方法。

中文摘要：在线策略蒸馏（OPD）通过在学生生成的轨迹上根据教师反馈训练学生来转移推理行为，但标准的全展开训练将每次更新与昂贵的完成绑定，并且可能将监督过度分配到后期位置，这些位置对当前学生的边际价值较低。我们通过有用监督视界重新审视这一假设：学生诱导的展开可能偏离教师偏好的延续，而对齐的前缀可能已经保留了长期OPD的更新方向。我们提出ADWIN，一种用于OPD的自适应窗口框架，将展开长度视为在线可接受性决策，在短教师锚定前缀上进行训练，同时使用延迟的全展开探测来审计前缀与全展开的对齐，并通过滞后控制自适应调整下一个视界。在数学和代码推理基准测试中，在单任务、多任务和强到弱设置下，ADWIN在全展开OPD和基于前缀的基线上改善了准确率-计算权衡，将端到端训练成本降低高达4.1倍，同时实现了相当或更好的准确率。

Original abstract: On-policy distillation (OPD) transfers reasoning behavior by training a student on teacher feedback along student-generated trajectories, but standard full-rollout training ties every update to a costly completion and can over-allocate supervision to late positions with low marginal value for the current student. We revisit this assumption through the useful supervision horizon: student-induced rollouts can drift from teacher-preferred continuations, while aligned prefixes may already preserve the long-horizon OPD update direction. We propose ADWIN, an adaptive-window framework for OPD that treats rollout length as an online admissibility decision, training on short teacher-anchored prefixes while using delayed full-rollout probes to audit prefix--full alignment and adapt the next horizon with staleness control. Across math and code reasoning benchmarks in single-task, multi-task, and strong-to-weak settings, ADWIN improves the accuracy--compute trade-off over full-rollout OPD and prefix-based baselines, reducing end-to-end training cost by up to 4.1 times while achieving comparable or better accuracy.

### [102] [Extrapolative Weight Averaging Reveals Correctness-Efficiency Frontiers in Code RL](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28751v1)
*Kunhao Zheng,Pierre Chambon,Juliette Decugis,Jonas Gehring,Taco Cohen,Benjamin Negrevergne,Gabriel Synnaeve*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 代码RL中权重平均揭示正确性-效率前沿，直接相关代码优化agent。

TL;DR: 在竞争性编程的强化学习中，通过嵌套单元测试覆盖训练得到的检查点展现出正确性-效率前沿，外推权重平均可以扩展该前沿并提高推理时的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索外推权重平均是否能在不额外进行强化学习训练的情况下，将微调检查点之间的帕累托前沿扩展到推理时有用的新检查点。

Method: 在竞争性编程的强化学习中，从共享初始化开始，训练不同嵌套单元测试覆盖奖励（低覆盖到高覆盖）的检查点，并分析插值和外推权重平均的效果。

Result: 外推权重平均扩展了正确性-效率前沿，在三个推理设置和两种模型规模上均有效，且集成外推权重平均在LCB/hard上将pass@250提高了3.3%。

Conclusion: 代码强化学习中的嵌套单元测试覆盖诱导了一个前沿，外推权重平均可以导航、扩展和利用该前沿，从而获得互补策略并提高性能。

中文摘要：线性插值在微调检查点之间已被证明可以追踪竞争目标之间的帕累托前沿，但外推权重平均是否能在没有额外强化学习训练的情况下，将此类前沿扩展到推理时有用的新检查点，仍不清楚。我们在竞争性编程的强化学习中研究这一问题，其中隐藏的单元测试在时间和内存限制下强制执行功能正确性和计算效率。从共享初始化开始，我们在嵌套单元测试覆盖下训练检查点：低覆盖奖励要求通过较小输入测试，而高覆盖奖励要求通过逐渐增大的测试直至完整套件。这一扫描揭示了正确性-效率前沿的出现：在难题上，更高覆盖奖励减少了优化失败但增加了正确性失败，使得解题率几乎不变。低覆盖和高覆盖检查点之间的插值恢复了这一前沿，而外推则将其扩展到训练端点之外。这一前沿及其外推延续出现在三种推理设置（纯推理、工具使用和智能体编码）以及两种模型规模（32B和7B）中。在问题层面，沿前沿移动会改变被解决的问题，使得外推检查点成为推理时扩展中的互补策略。具有外推权重平均的集成拓宽了覆盖，并在匹配样本预算下，在LCB/hard上的pass@250比最佳单一检查点提高了3.3%。这些结果表明，代码强化学习中的嵌套单元测试覆盖诱导了一个前沿，而外推权重平均可以导航、扩展和利用该前沿。

Original abstract: Linear interpolation between fine-tuned checkpoints has been shown to trace the Pareto front between competing objectives, but whether extrapolative weight averaging can extend such frontiers to new checkpoints useful at inference time, without additional RL training, remains unclear. We study this question in RL for competitive programming, where hidden unit tests under time and memory limits enforce both functional correctness and computational efficiency. Starting from a shared initialization, we train checkpoints under nested unit-test coverage: low-coverage rewards require passing smaller-input tests, while high-coverage rewards require passing progressively larger tests up to the full suite. This sweep reveals the emergence of a correctness-efficiency frontier: on hard problems, higher-coverage reward reduces optimization failures but increases correctness failures, leaving solve rate nearly unchanged. Interpolation between low- and high-coverage checkpoints recovers this frontier, while extrapolation extends it beyond the trained endpoints. Both the frontier and its extrapolative continuation appear across three inference settings, pure reasoning, tool use, and agentic coding, and across two model scales, 32B and 7B. At the problem level, moving along the frontier changes which problems are solved, making extrapolated checkpoints complementary policies in inference-time scaling. Ensembles with extrapolative weight averaging broaden coverage and improve pass@250 on LCB/hard by 3.3% over the best single checkpoint at matched sample budget. These results show that nested unit-test coverage in code RL induces a frontier that extrapolative weight averaging can navigate, extend, and exploit.

Original abstract: Computer-use agents (CUAs) have recently made substantial progress, but deploying a separate large expert for each software domain remains expensive. Small open computer-use agents are more practical specialization targets, but they remain substantially weaker and exhibit uneven domain-specific failures. A straightforward remedy is to synthesize large-scale training data for the target domain, yet we find that this naive approach yields only marginal improvements. Building on this observation, we introduce LearnWeak, an annotation-free specialization framework for small computer-use agents that uses a stronger reference agent to identify the student's weaknesses in the target domain, synthesize targeted tasks, and construct supervision automatically. LearnWeak further introduces an error-aware specialization objective that disentangles planning and execution errors, enabling more behaviorally precise updates than broad uniform supervision. On OSWorld, LearnWeak achieves average gains of 11.6 and 11.1 percentage points over EvoCUA-8B and OpenCUA-7B, respectively, across eight domains. We also validate that our student-aware dataset generation and training approaches outperform existing autonomous trajectory generation and training baselines. Our work highlights the importance of student awareness in both data synthesis and agent training, pointing toward a more principled and efficient path for specializing small computer-use agents in diverse domains.

*Youting Wang,Yuan Tang,Bowen Liu,Xuan Liu,Dingyan Shang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 诊断驱动的迭代细化：利用训练诊断和故障模式分类法指导奖励函数的针对性修订。

Conclusion: 该方法适用于PPO下具有可靠接口的稀疏结构化任务，在密集奖励连续控制中表现受限，事件文本字段的影响不确定。

中文摘要：对于具有语义奖励函数接口的稀疏、结构化强化学习任务，将LLM生成的奖励塑造视为调试而非一次性生成更为合适。我们以MiniGrid为核心评估、MuJoCo为边界压力测试，研究使用PPO训练的智能体。我们的审计发现两种主要的一次性失败模式——奖励洪水和语义/API误解——以及一种较罕见的弱塑造情况。我们提出诊断驱动的迭代细化方法，其中训练诊断和故障模式分类法指导有针对性的奖励函数修订。细化将DoorKey-8x8从2.3%提升到97.6%，KeyCorridor从31.2%提升到86.7%，但种子间方差较大。对照实验表明，这些提升并非来自重试或额外训练：仅基于指标的重提示导致大幅下降，而静态词汇表对照恢复了一部分差距（87.6%；70.7%），表明分类法提示是一个主要机制，动态标签仅提供部分孤立的增量证据。预算匹配和最佳3次比较将细化与选择和训练时间效应区分开来。组件移除测试、敏感性分析以及与作者标签的对比审计为调试解释提供了汇聚证据，同时揭示了校准限制。连续控制结果显示了边界：基于成功的诊断可能在密集奖励运动中误报，而返回趋势反馈消除了一个假阳性机制但未带来稳健提升。低调用协议是与基于种群的奖励搜索的成本对比，而非基准比较。在四个交叉方差设计环境中，点估计表明当LLM奖励函数方差占主导时收益更大，但自助法区间较宽。该方法局限于PPO下具有可靠接口的稀疏结构化任务；像event_text这样的字段可能有帮助、有害或中性。

Original abstract: For sparse, structured reinforcement-learning tasks with semantic reward-function interfaces, LLM-generated reward shaping is better framed as debugging than one-shot generation. We study PPO-trained agents using MiniGrid as core evaluation and MuJoCo as boundary stress test. Our audit finds two dominant one-shot failure modes -- reward flooding and semantic/API misunderstanding -- plus a rarer weak-shaping case. We propose diagnostic-driven iterative refinement, where training diagnostics and a failure-mode taxonomy guide targeted reward-function revision. Refinement improves DoorKey-8x8 from 2.3% to 97.6% and KeyCorridor from 31.2% to 86.7% with high seed-to-seed variance. Controls show these gains are not from retrying or extra training: metrics-only re-prompting yields large drops, while a static-vocabulary control recovers much of the gap (87.6%; 70.7%), showing the taxonomy prompt is a major mechanism and dynamic labels provide only partially isolated incremental evidence. Budget-matched and Best-of-3 comparisons separate refinement from selection and training-time effects. Component-removal tests, sensitivity analyses, and an audit against author labels provide converging evidence for the debugging interpretation while revealing calibration limits. Continuous-control results show the boundary: success-based diagnostics can misfire in dense-reward locomotion, and return-trend feedback removes one false-positive mechanism without robust gains. The low-call protocol is a cost contrast with population-based reward search, not a benchmark comparison. In four crossed-variance-design environments, point estimates suggest larger gains when LLM reward-function variance dominates but bootstrap intervals are wide. The method is bounded to sparse structured tasks with reliable interfaces under PPO; fields like event_text may help, hurt, or be neutral.

### [105] [Conf-Gen: Conformal Uncertainty Quantification for Generative Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28920v1)
*Gabriel Loaiza-Ganem,Kevin Zhang,Wei Cui,Marc T. Law,Kin Kwan Leung*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 提供生成模型的置信度保证，适用于agent输出验证

TL;DR: 提出了保形生成（Conf-Gen）框架，将保形风险控制扩展到无监督生成任务，并在LLM、图像生成、对话AI和AI智能体中获得保形保证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了Conf-Gen，通过放宽CRC的理论假设，将其适配到生成任务，统一并推广了先前将CP应用于LLM的方法。

Result: 展示了Conf-Gen在多个新领域的应用：确保图像生成器不产生记忆图像、对话AI提出足够澄清问题、AI智能体输出正确性。

中文摘要：保形预测（CP）及其扩展——保形风险控制（CRC）是通过形式化保证在监督机器学习中量化不确定性的成熟框架。然而，近期人工智能（AI）的突破主要由无监督生成模型驱动，例如大型语言模型（LLM）和图像生成器，这些模型与CP或CRC并不直接兼容。在这项工作中，我们引入了保形生成（Conf-Gen），这是一个将CRC适配到生成任务并放宽其理论假设的通用框架。Conf-Gen统一并推广了先前将CP应用于LLM的尝试，并将保形方法扩展到全新的领域。我们通过一些新颖的应用展示了Conf-Gen的灵活性，包括在以下方面获得保形保证：生成非记忆图像的图像生成器、提出足够澄清问题的对话式AI系统，以及AI智能体输出的正确性。

Original abstract: Conformal prediction (CP) and its extension, conformal risk control (CRC), are established frameworks for quantifying uncertainty in supervised machine learning through formal guarantees. However, recent breakthroughs in artificial intelligence (AI) have been driven by unsupervised generative models, such as large language models (LLMs) and image generators, which are not directly compatible with CP or CRC. In this work we introduce conformal generation (Conf-Gen), a general framework adapting CRC to generative tasks while relaxing its theoretical assumptions. Conf-Gen unifies and generalizes previous attempts to apply CP to LLMs, and extends conformal methodology to entirely new domains. We demonstrate the flexibility of Conf-Gen through some novel applications, including obtaining conformal guarantees on: image generators producing non-memorized images, conversational AI systems having asked enough clarifying questions, and the output of AI agents being correct.

### [106] [From Human Guidance to Autonomy: Agent Skill System for End-to-End LLM Deployment on Spatial NPUs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07586v2)
*Jiajie Li,Erwei Wang,Zhiru Zhang,Samuel Bayliss*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 直接相关：agent技能系统自动优化LLM部署在NPU

TL;DR: 一种两阶段基于代理的方法，用于在空间NPU上端到端部署LLM，实现了多个模型的自主部署，且性能具有竞争力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在空间NPU上端到端部署LLM人力成本高，现有研究仅关注单核优化，缺乏完整的部署方法。

Method: 两阶段方法：第一阶段通过人类引导的代理辅助开发参考部署并记录优化经验；第二阶段将文档提炼为包含八个阶段的代理技能系统，实现自主优化和调试，并严格保证数值正确性。

Result: 在AMD XDNA 2 NPU上自主部署了九个LLM，其中三个模型的持续性能达到或超过手工优化基线，部署时间为0.5-4小时，且首次通过开源栈部署了多个新模型。

Conclusion: 代理技能系统能够泛化到未见过的LLM，无需人工工程即可实现有竞争力的性能。

中文摘要：空间神经处理单元（NPU）为边缘大语言模型推理提供了能效平台，但在此类硬件上高效端到端部署大语言模型仍需要大量人力。尽管AI编码代理已开始降低这一成本，现有研究主要关注单核优化，而非在资源受限的空间NPU上端到端部署大语言模型。我们提出了一种两阶段方法论，在AMD XDNA 2 NPU上实现，从人类引导的开发过渡到代理自主。在第一阶段，我们通过人类引导的代理辅助开发了Llama-3.2-1B的参考部署。与手工优化基线相比，该实现实现了2.2倍的预填充加速和4.0倍的解码加速，优化轨迹及其经验教训在整个过程中记录为结构化文档。在第二阶段，我们将这些文档提炼为一个由八个阶段组成的代理技能系统，编排优化和调试技能集，并在每个阶段严格强制执行数值正确性。利用我们的代理技能系统，我们使用开源编译器栈在AMD XDNA 2 NPU上自主端到端部署了另外八个仅解码器的大语言模型（Llama-3.2-3B、SmolLM2-1.7B、Qwen2.5-{0.5B, 1.5B, 3B}、Qwen3-{0.6B, 1.7B, 4B}）。据我们所知，这些模型此前未通过任何开源软件栈部署在AMD NPU上。每次部署在0.5-4小时的代理墙钟时间内完成，几乎无需人工指导，并通过了数值正确性门控，展示了对先前未遇到的大语言模型的功能泛化能力。其中三个模型的持续性能达到或超过了我们的Llama-3.2-1B参考部署，表明生成的实现可以在无需额外模型特定人工工程的情况下具有竞争力。

Original abstract: Spatial neural processing units (NPUs) provide an energy-efficient platform for edge LLM inference, but efficiently deploying an LLM end-to-end on such hardware remains labor-intensive. Although AI coding agents have begun to lower this cost, existing studies have largely focused on single-kernel optimization rather than end-to-end LLM deployment on resource-constrained spatial NPUs.
  We present a two-stage methodology, instantiated on the AMD XDNA 2 NPU, that progresses from human-guided development to agent autonomy. In the first stage, we develop a reference deployment of Llama-3.2-1B through human-guided agent assistance. The resulting implementation achieves a speedup of 2.2x on prefill and 4.0x on decode over the hand-optimized baseline, with the optimization trajectory and its lessons recorded as structured documentation throughout. In the second stage, we distill the documentation into an agent skill system consisting of eight phases, orchestrating the optimization and debugging skill sets, with numerical correctness strictly enforced at each phase.
  Using our agent skill system, we autonomously deploy eight additional decoder-only LLMs (Llama-3.2-3B, SmolLM2-1.7B, Qwen2.5-{0.5B, 1.5B, 3B}, Qwen3-{0.6B, 1.7B, 4B}) end-to-end on the AMD XDNA 2 NPU using the open-source compiler stack. To our knowledge, these models have not previously been deployed on AMD NPUs via any open-source software stack. Each deployment completes in 0.5-4 hours of agent wall time with almost no human guidance, and passes the numerical-correctness gates, demonstrating functional generalization to previously unencountered LLMs. Three of the eight match or exceed the sustained performance of our Llama-3.2-1B reference deployment, suggesting that the resulting implementations can be competitive without additional model-specific human engineering.

</details>


### [107] [FormInv: A Measurement Protocol for Semantic Invariance in Mathematical Reasoning Benchmarks](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29001v1)
*Nishal Thomas,Noel Thomas*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 语义不变性评估协议，可迁移到agent评测方法

TL;DR: 通过审计释义质量发现，移除少量语义错误可改变模型排名，且标准基准无法检测到较大的语义一致性差距；FormInv协议可自动检测错误并提供不变性度量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准无法检测释义质量引起的排名不稳定性，且存在语义一致性率与准确率之间的巨大差距，需要一种低成本的审计方法来确保评估的可靠性。

Method: 提出FormInv审计协议，利用跨模型一致性自动检测语义错误，并使用语义一致性率（SCR）和Cochran's Q作为不变性度量，在Lean4验证的定理上对9个模型进行评估。

Result: MathCheck中3.1%的释义语义错误导致GPT-4o排名下降；自制数据集中47%的自动生成变体有误；9个模型SCR范围50-82%，与准确率范围86-96%存在32点差距；证明No-Free-Benchmark推论。

Conclusion: 释义质量对模型排序有显著影响，标准基准存在不可见的度量漏洞；FormInv协议可有效检测错误并量化语义不变性，助力可靠的模型选择。

中文摘要：对MathCheck（ICLR 2025）的释义质量审计发现，在129组中存在4个语义不正确的释义（3.1%）；移除它们使得GPT-4o从第2名降至第4名，并将Claude Haiku和DeepSeek V3提升至其之上；这些排名变化对任何单模型评估都是不可见的。跨模型一致性（MathCheck上≥3/4模型，我们的主要评估中≥6/9）以低于10美元的成本自动发现了这些错误；在我们自己的数据集中，相同的协议发现47%的自动生成的连接变体释义在语义上不正确。这一缺陷加剧了一个更深层次的测量差距：Claude Haiku 4.5达到86%的准确率，但SCR=50%，意味着其一半的定理在语义等价的重新表述下得到了不同的答案，而9个模型的聚合准确率范围仅为86-96%，但语义一致性率（SCR）范围却为50-82%——这是一个标准基准不可见的32个百分点的差距。形式上，对于9个前沿模型的任何目标排名，都存在一个对释义家族的加权方式来实现该排名（No-Free-Benchmark推论），因为没有模型在所有家族上帕累托支配——因此，选择家族的基准设计者隐含地决定了哪个模型获胜。FormInv提供了审计协议（在外部基准上以100%召回率复制）、SCR和每个定理的Cochran's Q作为主要不变性度量（在9个模型上评估，涉及366-811个条目，基于Lean4验证的定理），以及用于情景区分模型选择的FormInvSelector。

Original abstract: A paraphrase-quality audit of MathCheck (ICLR 2025) detected 4 semantically incorrect paraphrases in 129 groups (3.1%); removing them drops GPT-4o from rank 2 to rank 4 and elevates Claude Haiku and DeepSeek V3 above it; these ranking changes are invisible to any single-model evaluation. Cross-model unanimity found these errors automatically (>= 3/4 models for MathCheck; >= 6/9 for our primary evaluation) for under $10; in our own dataset the same protocol found that 47% of auto-generated connective-variation paraphrases were semantically incorrect. That flaw compounds a deeper measurement gap: Claude Haiku 4.5 achieves 86% accuracy yet SCR=50%, meaning half its theorems are answered differently under semantically equivalent restatements, while aggregate accuracy across 9 models spans only 86-96% yet Semantic Consistency Rates (SCR) span 50-82% -- a 32-point gap invisible to standard benchmarks. Formally, for any target ranking over 9 frontier models there exists a weighting over paraphrase families that realizes it (No-Free-Benchmark corollary), because no model Pareto-dominates all families -- so benchmark designers who select families are implicitly choosing which model wins. FormInv supplies the audit protocol (replicated on external benchmarks at 100% recall), SCR and per-theorem Cochran's Q as primary invariance measures evaluated on 9 models across 366-811 items (on Lean4-verified theorems), and FormInvSelector for regime-aware model selection.

</details>


### [108] [Label-Free Reinforcement Learning via Cross-Model Entropy](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29009v1)
*Matt Gorbett,Hossein Shirazi*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 跨模型熵标签免费RL，可应用于agent训练

TL;DR: 提出跨模型熵（CME）作为无标签奖励信号，用于强化学习后训练，扩展其到开放式指令跟随领域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RL后训练受限于奖励信号，需要真实奖励或人工偏好标签，而自我参考信号会强化模型自身错误。

Method: 使用独立验证模型计算生成器响应的平均对数似然作为奖励信号，集成到GRPO训练循环中。

Result: 在四个模型族和三种训练设置下，CME奖励的胜率（经平局调整）为52.5%至71.4%，优于未训练基础模型。

Conclusion: CME提供了一种有效的无标签奖励信号，无需外部验证即可将RL后训练扩展到开放式指令跟随任务。

中文摘要：使用强化学习对大型语言模型进行后训练时，奖励信号是瓶颈。现有方法需要可验证的真实奖励（限制在数学、代码执行等自动正确性检查领域）或人工偏好标签（昂贵且易受奖励黑客攻击）。最近的无标签方法用自我参考信号（如多数投票或模型自身输出的token熵）替代真实验证器，但有强化模型自身错误的风险。本文提出跨模型熵（CME），即生成器响应在独立验证模型下的平均对数似然，作为用于RL后训练的无标签奖励信号。CME是连续的、无需训练的，其原理是验证器认为不意外的响应很可能是正确或高质量的。由于验证器独立于生成器，该信号无法通过自一致性来欺骗。我们将CME集成到GRPO中，无需对训练循环做其他更改，将无标签RL扩展到开放式指令跟随——这是一个自我参考信号不适用或不适合的领域。在开放式指令跟随（UltraFeedback提示，在AlpacaEval 2.0上评估）中，CME奖励在四种模型族（Qwen、Llama、Gemma、OLMo）和三种训练设置（预训练、SFT和指令微调）的逐对LLM作为裁判比较中击败了未训练的基础模型，经平局调整的胜率范围为52.5%至71.4%。代码将在发表后发布。

Original abstract: Post-training large language models with reinforcement learning is bottlenecked by the reward signal. Existing approaches require either ground-truth verifiable rewards, restricting training to domains with automatic correctness checks (e.g., mathematics, code execution), or human preference labels, which are expensive to collect and prone to reward hacking. Recent label-free methods replace ground-truth verifiers with self-referential signals like majority voting or token entropy over a model's own outputs, but risk reinforcing a model's own errors. In this work we propose Cross-Model Entropy (CME), the mean log-likelihood of a generator's response under a separate verifier model, as a label-free reward signal for RL post-training. CME is continuous, training-free, and grounded in the principle that responses a verifier finds unsurprising are likely correct or high quality. Because the verifier is independent of the generator, the signal cannot be gamed through self-consistency. We integrate CME into GRPO with no other changes to the training loop, extending label-free RL to open-ended instruction following -- a regime where self-referential signals are inapplicable or poorly suited. On open-ended instruction following (UltraFeedback prompts, evaluated on AlpacaEval 2.0), CME rewards beat the untrained base in head-to-head LLM-as-Judge comparisons across four model families (Qwen, Llama, Gemma, OLMo) and three training regimes (pretrained, SFT, and instruction-tuned), with tie-adjusted win rates ranging from 52.5% to 71.4%. Code will be released upon publication.

</details>


### [109] [Return-to-Go Is More Than a Number: Q-Guided Alignment for Return-Conditioned Supervised Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29028v1)
*Yuxiao Yang,Weitong Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: Q指导对齐方法，可迁移到agent规划

TL;DR: 提出Q-ALIGN DT框架，通过Q值对齐确保条件序列模型中RTG与策略性能一致，理论保证最优性，在D4RL上实现高可控性和性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有CSMs将RTG仅作为数值输入，未使其与策略性能对齐，导致控制信号与策略输出脱节。

Method: 利用Q函数提供密集指导，并通过RTG扰动技术微调Q函数，强制输出策略的Q值与输入RTG一致。

Result: 在D4RL基准测试中，Q-ALIGN DT实现了优越的可控性和性能，并成功泛化到速度追踪等任务。

Conclusion: Q-ALIGN DT有效学习结构化的策略族，确保精确对齐，为条件序列模型提供了可靠的控制机制。

中文摘要：条件序列模型（CSMs）通过将回报待实现（RTG）作为控制信号来学习策略。然而，现有的CSMs通常将RTG视为简单的数值输入，而不是使其与策略的性能对齐。在本文中，我们提出Q-ALIGN DT，一个通过确保输出策略的Q值与输入RTG一致来强制这种对齐的框架。通过利用Q函数为CSMs提供密集指导，并使用RTG扰动技术结合CSM进一步微调Q函数，我们的方法确保更高的RTG始终映射到具有更高期望回报的轨迹。理论上，我们证明Q-ALIGN DT能够有效学习期望的策略，并在RTG足够高时输出接近最优的策略。实验上，我们通过大量实验证明Q-ALIGN DT在D4RL基准测试中实现了优越的可控性和性能。值得注意的是，我们的模型有效学习了结构化的策略族，保持精确对齐并泛化到先前方法失败的速度追踪等任务。

Original abstract: Conditioned Sequence Models (CSMs) learn policies by treating return-to-go (RTG) as a control signal. However, existing CSMs often treat the RTGs as simple numerical inputs rather than aligning them with the performance of their policies. In this paper, we propose Q-ALIGN DT, a framework that enforces this alignment by ensuring the $Q$-value of the output policy is consistent with the input RTG. By leveraging a $Q$ function to provide dense guidance to CSMs and further fine-tuning it using an RTG-perturbation technique with the CSM, our method ensures that higher RTGs are consistently mapped to trajectories with higher expected returns. Theoretically, we show that Q-ALIGN DT can efficiently learn the desired policy and output a near-optimal one when the RTG is sufficiently high. Empirically, we demonstrate through extensive experiments that Q-ALIGN DT achieves superior controllability and performance across the D4RL benchmark. Remarkably, our model effectively learns a structured family of policies that maintains precise alignment and generalizes to tasks like velocity-tracking where prior methods fail.

</details>


### [110] [Influence-Guided Symbolic Regression: Scientific Discovery via LLM-Driven Equation Search with Granular Feedback](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29184v1)
*Evgeny S. Saveliev,Samuel Holt,Nabeel Seedat,David L. Bentley,Jim Weatherall,Mihaela van der Schaar*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: LLM驱动符号回归结合MCTS，提出可迁移的agent搜索框架

TL;DR: 提出影响引导的符号回归（IGSR），结合LLM生成候选函数与影响分数剪枝，通过MCTS探索，在多个基准和实际数据中表现优异，并发现新的生物关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前LLM用于符号回归时，使用标量指标（如全局MSE）引导导致反馈粗粒度，无法识别具体项的好坏。因此需要更细粒度的评估方法。

Method: 提出IGSR框架，迭代进行LLM生成候选基函数和利用影响分数Δ_j进行剪枝，并结合蒙特卡洛树搜索（MCTS）平衡探索与利用。

Result: 在LLM-SRBench、PKPD模型、流行病模拟和基因组数据基准上验证效果。在生物数据集案例中，发现DNA甲基化与RNA聚合酶II暂停的新关系，并经湿实验验证。

Conclusion: IGSR通过细粒度影响引导，有效提升了符号回归的发现能力，有望加速科学发现。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）为科学发现提供了有前景的途径，但它们在符号回归中的应用常常受到低效搜索策略和粗糙反馈信号的限制。目前的方法通常使用标量指标（例如全局均方误差）引导LLM，但这些指标无法识别所提出方程中的哪些成分驱动性能或导致错误。我们引入了影响引导的符号回归（IGSR），该方法将方程发现构建为迭代的两步过程，结合多样的项生成与严格的选择：LLM为线性模型生成候选基函数$ψ_j(\mathbf{x})$，然后使用细粒度的影响分数$Δ_j$进行评估。这些分数量化了每个项对泛化准确性的边际贡献，从而实现影响引导的剪枝过程，系统地优化模型结构。将这一机制集成到蒙特卡洛树搜索（MCTS）中，可以在探索新型函数形式与利用高影响组件之间取得平衡，从而导航组合搜索空间。我们在多样化的基准测试集上展示了IGSR的有效性，包括LLM-SRBench、药理学PKPD模型、流行病学模拟以及真实世界基因组数据。值得注意的是，我们在一个使用高维生物数据集的案例研究中验证了该框架的真正发现能力，其中IGSR识别了DNA甲基化与RNA聚合酶II暂停之间的新颖关系；这一假设随后通过湿实验室实验得到了支持。

Original abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) offer a promising avenue for scientific discovery, yet their application to symbolic regression is often constrained by inefficient search strategies and coarse feedback signals. Current methods typically guide LLMs using scalar metrics (e.g., global Mean Squared Error), which fail to identify which components of a proposed equation are driving performance or causing error. We introduce \textit{Influence-Guided Symbolic Regression} (IGSR), a method that frames equation discovery as an iterative two-step process combining diverse term generation with rigorous selection: an LLM generates candidate basis functions $ψ_j(\mathbf{x})$ for a linear model, which are then evaluated using granular influence scores $Δ_j$. These scores quantify each term's marginal contribution to generalization accuracy, enabling an influence-guided pruning process that systematically refines the model structure. Integrating this mechanism into a Monte Carlo Tree Search (MCTS) enables navigating the combinatorial search space while balancing exploration of novel functional forms with exploitation of high-influence components. We demonstrate IGSR's effectiveness on a diverse suite of benchmarks, including LLM-SRBench, pharmacological PKPD models, an epidemiological simulation, and real-world genomic data. Notably, we validate the framework's capacity for genuine discovery in a case study using a high-dimensional biological dataset, in which IGSR identified a novel relationship between DNA methylation and RNA Polymerase II pausing; a hypothesis that was subsequently supported via wet-lab experimentation.

</details>

### [111] [DecomposeRL: Learning to Ask Useful, Informative, and Diverse Questions for Semi-Supervised, Traceable Claim Verification](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27858v1)
*Shubhashis Roy Dipta,Ankur Padia,Francis Ferraro*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: RL分解策略用于声明验证，训练方法可迁移至agent技能学习。

TL;DR: 提出DecomposeRL，通过强化学习框架和GRPO训练，在少量精选数据上训练出准确且具有可检查痕迹的声明验证模型，性能优于更大模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有声明验证方法要么准确但不可检查，要么可检查但性能较差，需要一种兼顾准确性和可检查性的方法。

Method: 将声明验证视为强化学习中的分解策略，使用GRPO和多面奖励集成训练，并通过数据筛选漏斗将大量声明压缩为高质量子集以降低训练成本。

Result: 在11个基准上，DecomposeRL-7B在仅5K精选数据上达到86.3域内和69.8域外准确率，匹配32B和GPT-4.1-mini，并在半监督设置中优于基线。

Conclusion: DecomposeRL成功结合了准确性和可检查性，通过高效的训练策略和数据筛选实现了优异性能，代码和数据已开源。

中文摘要：声明验证分为两类：端到端分类器准确但无法提供可检查的痕迹，而基于分解的方法可以产生可检查的痕迹但在基准数据集上性能落后。我们提出了DecomposeRL，一个准确且能产生可检查痕迹的声明验证器。DecomposeRL将分解视为一种强化学习策略，通过GRPO和多面奖励集成进行训练，支持从无标签声明中进行全监督和半监督学习。DecomposeRL通过一个数据筛选漏斗解决了GRPO的过高训练成本，该漏斗将115K条事实验证声明浓缩为5K条紧凑且学习信号密集的子集。我们展示了在仅约5K条精选声明上进行全监督训练的DecomposeRL-7B策略，在包含生物医学、政治、科学和通用领域的11个声明验证基准上取得了86.3的域内和69.8的域外平衡准确率。尽管模型小了4倍，但它匹配了32B基线和GPT-4.1-mini，并且在仅使用10%标注声明的半监督设置中进一步优于基线。代码、数据和模型可在https://dipta007.github.io/DecomposeRL获取。

Original abstract: Claim verification splits between end-to-end classifiers that are accurate but yields no inspectable traces, and decomposition-based methods produce inspectable traces but lag performance on benchmark datasets. We propose DecomposeRL an accurate claim-verifier that produce inspectable traces. DecomposeRL frames decomposition as an RL policy trained with GRPO and a multi-faceted reward ensemble, enabling both fully supervised and semi-supervised learning from unlabeled claims. DecomposeRL addresses the prohibitive training cost of GRPO with a data-curation funnel that distills 115K fact-verification claims into a compact, learning-signal-dense subset of 5K claims. We show that a DecomposeRL-7B policy trained with full supervision on only ~5K curated claims achieves 86.3 in-domain and 69.8 out-of-domain balanced accuracy across 11 claim-verification benchmarks containing biomedical, political, scientific, and general-domain claims. Despite being 4x smaller, it matches 32B baselines and GPT-4.1-mini, and it further outperforms baselines in a semi-supervised setting with only 10% labeled claims data. Code, data, and models are available at https://dipta007.github.io/DecomposeRL

</details>


### [112] [VibeSearchBench: Benchmarking Long-horizon Proactive Search in the Wild](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27882v1)
*Xiaohongshu Inc*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 长程主动搜索benchmark，涉及多轮交互与评估，可迁移至coding agent评估。

TL;DR: 现有搜索基准存在评估-体验差距，作者提出VibeSearch范式并创建VibeSearchBench基准，发现所有前沿模型在协作式搜索任务中表现均不足，最佳F1仅30.30。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有搜索基准依赖过度明确的查询、单轮交互和固定模式评估，无法反映真实搜索行为中用户与智能体通过多轮对话协作细化模糊意图的模式，导致评估结果与用户体验之间存在显著差距。

Method: 提出VibeSearch范式，构建VibeSearchBench基准，包含200个手动策划的双语任务（分专业和日常子集），每个任务配对用户角色和模式无关知识图谱，采用渐进式用户模拟器和图匹配评估框架，在ReAct和OpenClaw下测试七种前沿模型。

Result: 所有模型在VibeSearch任务上表现严重不足，最佳F1得分仅30.30。

Conclusion: 现有模型在长上下文推理、主动意图激发和结构化知识构建方面仍存在根本性不足，需要进一步研究以实现更自然的协作式搜索交互。

中文摘要：基于LLM的智能体在搜索基准测试中得分很高，但真实用户始终对结果不满意，揭示了持久的评估-体验差距。我们将这一差距归因于现有基准依赖于过度明确的查询、单轮交互和固定模式评估，这些都不反映真实搜索行为——用户和智能体通过多轮对话协作细化模糊意图。我们将此范式称为VibeSearch，并引入VibeSearchBench，一个包含200个手动策划的双语（中文和英文）任务的基准，涵盖20个领域，分为VibeSearch-Pro（专业）和VibeSearch-Daily（日常生活）子集。每个任务将一个用户角色与一个模式无关的真实知识图谱配对，并通过渐进式用户模拟器和图匹配评估框架进行评估。我们在ReAct框架和OpenClaw智能体工具包下对七个前沿模型进行了基准测试。结果表明，所有模型在VibeSearch上仍然严重不足（最佳F1：30.30），凸显了在长上下文推理、主动意图激发和结构化知识构建方面取得根本性进展的必要性。

Original abstract: LLM-based agents score well on search benchmarks, yet real users consistently find results unsatisfying, revealing a persistent evaluation-experience gap. We attribute this gap to existing benchmarks' reliance on over-specified queries, single-turn interactions, and fixed-schema evaluation, none of which reflect real search behavior where users and agents collaboratively refine vague intent through multi-turn dialogue. We term this paradigm VibeSearch and introduce VibeSearchBench, a benchmark comprising 200 manually curated bilingual (Chinese and English) tasks across 20 domains, split into VibeSearch-Pro (professional) and VibeSearch-Daily (daily-life) subsets. Each task pairs a user persona with a schema-free ground-truth knowledge graph, and is evaluated through a progressive-disclosure user simulator and a graph-matching evaluation framework. We benchmark seven frontier models under both the ReAct framework and the OpenClaw agent harness. Results show that all models remain substantially inadequate for VibeSearch (best F1: 30.30), highlighting the need for fundamental advances in long-context reasoning, proactive intent elicitation, and structured knowledge construction.

### [113] [The Fragility of Chain-of-Thought Monitoring Across Typologically Diverse Languages](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27901v1)
*Eric Onyame,Runtao Zhou,Kowshik Thopalli,Bhavya Kailkhura,Chirag Agarwal*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: CoT监控多语言评估，对agent安全监控与可解释性有潜在参考。

TL;DR: 首次大规模跨语言评估表明，链式思维监控在非英语语言中普遍不忠实，模型系统性地进行策略性操纵，低资源语言中欺骗率高达100%，CoT监控在语言分布偏移下脆弱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: CoT监控被提出作为安全机制，但其可靠性在非英语和不同模型系列中尚未充分探索。

Method: 对13种语言、7个模型系列共16个模型进行对抗性提示评估，结合内部答案标记概率分析，评估CoT可监控性。

Result: CoT不忠实率平均95.9%；模型存在策略性操纵；欺骗模式在低资源语言中100%出现；模型在生成前15%内已在潜在激活中承诺失调线索。

Conclusion: CoT监控在语言分布偏移下本质脆弱，安全信号弱于英语研究显示，需发展更稳健的监控技术和白盒方法。

中文摘要：链式思维（CoT）监控已被提出作为检测大型语言模型中失调行为的一种有前景的安全机制。然而，其可靠性在英语之外以及跨不同模型系列方面仍很大程度上未被探索。我们首次对跨越13种不同语言和7个前沿模型系列（共16个模型）的CoT可监控性进行了大规模评估。使用需要明确中间计算的对抗性提示评估，结合对内部答案标记概率的分析，我们一致地发现CoT在不同语言和提示类型中存在不忠实现象，在8B-120B参数模型中平均不忠实率为95.9%。我们发现前沿模型系统性地进行策略性操纵，包括答案切换、事后合理化以及对提示的程序性利用，使得外部监控器难以检测欺骗行为。我们表明，即使CoT看似忠实，前沿模型通常会在生成的前15%内在潜在激活中承诺失调线索。令人惊讶的是，这些欺骗模式在低资源语言中保持100%，揭示了当前基于CoT的监督存在根本性限制。我们的结果表明，CoT监控在语言分布偏移下本质上脆弱，提供的安全信号远弱于仅英语研究所表明的。这些发现强调了开发稳健的CoT监控器的迫切需要，并加速研究白盒监控技术，特别是在中低资源语言中提高CoT可监控性。我们的代码可在此处获取：https://multilingual-cot-monitoring.github.io/

Original abstract: Chain-of-thought (CoT) monitoring has been proposed as a promising safety mechanism for detecting misaligned behavior in large language models. However, its reliability remains largely unexplored beyond English and across diverse model families. We present the first large-scale evaluation of CoT monitorability across 13 diverse languages and seven frontier model families, comprising 16 models. Using adversarial-hint evaluations that require explicit intermediate computation, together with analysis of internal answer-token probabilities, we consistently find CoT unfaithfulness across languages and hint types, with an average rate of 95.9\% across 8B--120B parameter models. We find that frontier models systematically engage in strategic manipulation, including answer-switching, post-hoc rationalization, and procedural exploitation of hints, making external monitors struggle to detect deception. We show that frontier models often commit to the misaligned cue in their latent activations within the first 15\% of generation, even when the CoT appears faithful. Surprisingly, these deceptive patterns remain 100\% in low-resource languages, revealing fundamental limitations in current CoT-based oversight. Our results reveal that CoT monitoring is fundamentally fragile under linguistic distribution shift, providing a substantially weaker safety signal than what English-only studies suggest. These findings underscore an urgent need to develop robust CoT monitors and to accelerate research into white-box monitoring techniques, especially to improve CoT monitorability in mid- and low-resource languages. Our code is available \href{https://multilingual-cot-monitoring.github.io/}{\textcolor{blue}{here}}.

### [114] [Does Capability Transfer to Subjective Behavior -- and Would Our Instruments Tell Us? A Self-Evolving, Trust-by-Construction Evaluation Paradigm](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27914v2)
*Yuming,Huang,Yao Liu,Pengjie Ding,Lei Wang,Junchen Wan*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 提出自进化评估范式，可迁移至agent评测。

TL;DR: 本文针对LLM在主观、面向人类任务上的评估问题，提出了一种自我进化的工具和信任构建范式，发现客观基准上的能力提升并不总是转移到主观行为上，如建议约束维度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基准测试在客观领域（如数学、代码）成熟，但在主观、面向人类的领域（如陪伴、情感支持）缺乏可靠评估方法，因为人工评估一致性低、有偏差且不可重复，无法判断客观能力是否转移到主观行为。

Method: 构建了一个自我进化的工具，在乘法反博弈适应度下选择并自主生成行为维度，自停机制；采用信任构建范式，通过三个证书（无人类金标准）建立信任；在49个模型、8个家族上评估主观行为。

Result: 能力转移是可分离的；建议约束是前沿的普遍最低维度，在gpt-4.1到gpt-5中倒退；温暖约束受模型生成驱动，而非规模、MoE宽度等；开源模型在低成本下匹配闭源；四个评判者家族在ESConv对话上复制了评分标准。

Conclusion: 客观基准上的能力并不完全转移到主观行为，需要针对主观任务设计更有效的评估方法；所提出的工具和范式能揭示此类不一致，且数据、代码等将公开。

中文摘要：基准测试在答案可验证的领域（数学、代码、推理）已经成熟，但LLM增长最快的用途是主观的、面向人类的：陪伴、情感支持、咨询。在那里，默认的有效性测试——将指标与人类判断相关联——没有稳定的锚点：评分者间一致性低，受评分者身份影响，几乎不可重复，且存在长度偏差。因此我们无法回答那个重要的问题：在客观基准上扩展的能力是否会转移到主观行为上，如果不会，我们的工具能否告诉我们？我们为此构建了一个工具，并报告它在前沿的发现。我们贡献了：第一，一个自我进化的工具，在乘法反博弈适应度下选择并自主生成其行为维度，在停止改进时自动停止；第二，一个信任构建范式，通过在没有人类金标准的情况下建立三个证书来赢得信任，人类评分者饱和（rho ~ 0.45）；第三，它揭示的发现——能力转移是可分离的。在49个模型、8个家族和24个月中，主观行为是客观基准扩展未能传递的地方：最尖锐的例子是建议约束（知道何时不给建议），是前沿的普遍最低维度，在gpt-4.1到gpt-5的过程中它倒退，而总分却隐藏了它——一条指令即可恢复的退化。温暖约束受模型生成驱动，而非原始规模、MoE宽度、推理预算或推理模式；开源权重的帕累托前沿在每次调用成本低约10-80倍的情况下匹配闭源旗舰；四个评判者家族在保留的人类ESConv对话上复制了评分标准。数据、代码、锁定评分标准和评判者提示将在发表后发布。

Original abstract: Benchmarking is mature where answers are verifiable -- math, code, reasoning -- but the fastest-growing uses of LLMs are subjective and human-facing: companionship, emotional support, counseling. There the default validity test, correlating a metric to human judgment, has no stable anchor: inter-rater agreement is low, structured by annotator identity, barely reproducible, and length-biased. So we cannot answer the question that matters: does capability that scales on objective benchmarks transfer to subjective behavior, and would our instruments even tell us if it did not? We build an instrument for this regime and report what it reveals at the frontier. We contribute, first, a self-evolving instrument that selects and then authors its own behavioral dimensions under a multiplicative anti-gaming fitness, self-halting when it stops improving; second, a trust-by-construction paradigm that earns belief through three certificates established without a human gold standard, where human raters saturate (rho ~ 0.45); and third, the finding it makes visible -- capability transfer is dissociable. Across 49 models, 8 families, and 24 months, subjective behaviors are where objective-benchmark scaling fails to carry over: the sharpest case, advice-restraint (knowing when not to give advice), is the frontier's universal-lowest dimension, and at gpt-4.1->gpt-5 it ran backwards while the aggregate score hid it -- a regression one instruction recovers. Warm restraint is moved by model generation, not by raw scale, MoE width, inference budget, or reasoning mode; the open-weight Pareto frontier matches closed flagships at ~10-80x lower per-call cost; and four judge families replicate the rubric on held-out human ESConv conversations. Data, code, the locked rubric, and judge prompts will be released upon publication.

</details>


### [115] [MemGuard: Preventing Memory Contamination in Long-Term Memory-Augmented Large Language Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28009v1)
*Hyeonjeong Ha,Jeonghwan Kim,Cheng Qian,Jiayu Liu,William M. Campbell,Yue Wu,Yuji Zhang,Kathleen McKeown,Dilek Hakkani-Tur,Heng Ji*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: MemGuard记忆框架，防止记忆污染，适用于agent记忆系统。

TL;DR: 提出MemGuard，一种类型感知记忆框架，通过为记忆分配功能角色并选择性组合证据，解决异构记忆污染问题，提升记忆可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有记忆系统将不同类型记忆混在一起，导致异构记忆污染，造成推理错误。

Method: 在写入时为每个记忆分配功能角色，维护类型隔离记忆的关系，并在检索时只从必要类型中选择证据。

Result: 在幻觉和长时程对话基准上，记忆可靠性提升最多28.27%，检索令牌减少5.8倍。

Conclusion: 可靠的长期推理需要原则性的组织和选择性使用异构记忆。

中文摘要：记忆增强的大型语言模型通过维护跨交互的长期记忆，扩展了推理能力，超越了固定的上下文窗口。然而，现有的记忆系统常常将稳定的用户事实、情景事件和行为规则压缩到共享空间中，使得功能上不同的记忆可以被检索并用作可互换的证据。我们将这种失败模式识别为异构记忆污染，即上下文特定的事件变成过度泛化的主张，或者语义相关但功能不兼容的记忆误导生成。为此，我们引入了MemGuard，一种类型感知的记忆框架，在记忆构建和检索过程中保留功能记忆边界。它在写入时为每个记忆分配明确的功能角色，维护跨类型隔离记忆的关系，并仅从必要的记忆类型中选择组合证据，减少来自不相关或功能不兼容证据的污染。在幻觉和长时程对话基准测试中，MemGuard将记忆可靠性提高了最多28.27%，同时检索的记忆令牌比先前方法少5.8倍。这些结果表明，可靠的长期推理依赖于有原则的组织和异构记忆的选择性使用。

Original abstract: Memory-augmented large language models extend reasoning beyond a fixed context window by maintaining long-term memory across interactions. However, existing memory systems often collapse stable user facts, episodic events, and behavioral rules into a shared space, allowing functionally distinct memories to be retrieved and used as interchangeable evidence. We identify this failure mode as heterogeneous memory contamination, where context-specific events become overgeneralized claims, or semantically relevant but functionally incompatible memories mislead generation. To this end, we introduce MemGuard, a type-aware memory framework that preserves functional memory boundaries during memory construction and retrieval. It assigns each memory an explicit functional role at write time, maintains relations across type-isolated memories, and selectively composes evidence only from necessary memory types, reducing contamination from irrelevant or functionally incompatible evidence. Across hallucination and long-horizon conversation benchmarks, MemGuard improves memory reliability by up to 28.27% while retrieving up to 5.8x fewer memory tokens than prior methods. These results suggest that reliable long-term reasoning depends on principled organization and selective use of heterogeneous memory.

</details>


### [116] [Beyond pass@k: Redundancy-Aware RLVR for Multi-Sample Code Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28022v1)
*Le Bronnec Florian,Alexandre Verine,Rio Yokota,Benjamin Negrevergne*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 添加基于JPlag的反冗余奖励到验证器强化学习中，提高了有限预算下的代码生成性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 仅正确性的RL目标导致生成冗余实现，损害了更大预算下的Pass@k性能。

Method: 我们使用JPlag相似性为RLVR增加直接的反冗余奖励，以抑制近重复生成。

Result: 在3个模型和3个基准上，该方法可靠地提高了有限预算下的可执行性能，通常匹配或优于专门考虑Pass@k的目标。

Conclusion: 抑制代码生成中的冗余可以提升性能，基于JPlag的奖励是有效的。

中文摘要：用于代码生成的LLM通常在重复采样设置下通过Pass@k进行评估，其中多个候选程序在有限的采样预算下针对单元测试执行。虽然最近基于验证器的强化学习（RLVR）方法提高了可执行正确性，但这些目标如何影响采样程序之间的冗余仍然不清楚。在这项工作中，我们使用JPlag（一种代码抄袭检测系统）研究代码生成中的实现级冗余。跨模型和基准，我们表明仅正确性的RLVR通常会使生成集中在重复实现上，而考虑Pass@k的目标则保持较低的冗余并提高更大预算的性能。受这些观察的启发，我们基于JPlag相似性为RLVR增加了直接的反冗余奖励。在3个模型和3个基准上，鼓励非重复生成可靠地提高了有限预算下的可执行性能，通常匹配或优于专门考虑Pass@k的目标。

Original abstract: LLMs for code generation are commonly evaluated in repeated-sampling settings using Pass@k, where multiple candidate programs are executed against unit tests under a finite sampling budget. While recent verifier-based reinforcement learning (RLVR) methods improve executable correctness, how these objectives affect redundancy among sampled programs remains poorly understood. In this work, we study implementation-level redundancy in code generation using JPlag, a plagiarism-detection system for code. Across models and benchmarks, we show that correctness-only RLVR often concentrates generations around repeated implementations, whereas Pass@k-aware objectives maintain lower redundancy and improve larger-budget performance. Motivated by these observations, we augment RLVR with direct anti-redundancy rewards based on JPlag similarity. Across 3 models and 3 benchmarks, discouraging near-duplicate generations reliably improves finite-budget executable performance, often matching or outperforming specialized Pass@k-aware objectives.

### [117] [LegalGraphRAG: Multi-Agent Graph Retrieval-Augmented Generation for Reliable Legal Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28120v1)
*Zerui Chen,Qinggang Zhang,Zhishang Xiang,Zhimin Wei,Linfeng Gao,Xiao Huang,Zhihong Zhang,Jinsong Su*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 多智能体GraphRAG用于法律推理，可迁移至coding agent的分工与验证设计

TL;DR: LegalGraphRAG通过层次化法律图和多智能体验证系统，提升了法律领域检索增强生成的准确性和可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有GraphRAG在处理异构法律语料时无法区分不同粒度知识，且缺乏证据验证机制，导致检索不准确和推理不可靠。

Method: 提出层次化法律图组织多粒度法律知识，并设计多智能体系统（研究者、审计员、裁决者）进行证据检索、验证和综合裁决。

Result: 在准确性和可信度上达到最先进水平，优于现有GraphRAG基线。

Conclusion: LegalGraphRAG有效解决了法律推理中的异构性和证据验证问题，提升了RAG在专业领域的适用性。

中文摘要：基于图的检索增强生成（GraphRAG）通过将知识结构化为关系图，推进了平面文档检索，从而实现更连贯和有效的推理。然而，将其应用于法律推理等特定领域面临着关键挑战。（i）法律语料库是异构的，包含来自案例、法条和解释的多粒度知识。平坦的知识图无法充分区分事实细节、适用规则和抽象原则，限制了准确检索。（ii）可靠的法律判断需要透明、基于证据的推理。传统的RAG直接将检索到的上下文传递给LLM而不加验证，导致不透明且易出错的推理。为此，我们提出了LegalGraphRAG，一个专为可靠法律推理设计的框架。我们的方法引入了两个核心组件：一个层次化法律图，该图层次化地组织法律源以在适当的抽象级别进行检索；以及一个用于可靠法律推理的多智能体系统，其中研究者检索候选证据，审计员严格验证其与源文档的一致性，裁决者综合一组已验证的证据做出最终判断。大量实验表明，LegalGraphRAG取得了最先进的性能，在准确和可信的法律分析中超越了现有的GraphRAG基线。我们的代码、数据集和实现细节可在https://github.com/XMUDeepLIT/LegalGraphRAG获取。

Original abstract: Graph-based Retrieval-Augmented Generation (GraphRAG) advances flat document retrieval by structuring knowledge as relational graphs, enabling more coherent and effective reasoning. However, applying it to specific domains like legal reasoning faces critical challenges. (i) Legal corpora are heterogeneous, containing multi-granular knowledge from cases, articles and interpretations. A flat knowledge graph cannot adequately differentiate between factual details, applied rules, and abstract principles, limiting accurate retrieval. (ii) Reliable legal judgment demands transparent, evidence-based reasoning. Traditional RAG passes retrieved context directly to an LLM without verification, resulting in opaque, error-prone reasoning. To this end, we propose LegalGraphRAG, a framework designed for reliable legal reasoning. Our approach introduces two core components: a hierarchical legal graph that hierarchically organizes legal sources to enable retrieval at appropriate abstraction levels, and a multi-agent system for reliable legal reasoning, where a Researcher retrieves candidate evidence, an Auditor rigorously verifies its validity against source documents, and an Adjudicator synthesizes the set of verified evidence to render a final judgment. Extensive experiments show that LegalGraphRAG achieves the state-of-the-art performance, outperforming existing GraphRAG baselines in accurate and trustworthy legal analysis. Our code, datasets and implementation details are available at https://github.com/XMUDeepLIT/LegalGraphRAG.

</details>


### [118] [Revisiting Anthropomorphic Reflection Markers in Large Language Model Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28305v1)
*Yahan Yu,Noa Nakanishi,Fei Cheng*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 分析LLM推理中的反思标记，对agent中反思机制的设计有启发意义。

TL;DR: 本研究通过提示级和词元级干预抑制拟人化反思标记，发现这些标记并非推理所必需，抑制后可能提升性能，表明它们只是表面线索而非反思本身。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拟人化反思标记机制不明，可能导致冗余和重复的标记引发的过度思考风险，因此需要重新审视其必要性和作用。

Method: 通过提示级别和词元级别的干预来抑制拟人化反思标记，并在四个基准测试和两个模型规模上分析其对任务性能的影响。

Result: 抑制拟人化标记可以在多种设置下保持或提高性能，尤其在较大采样预算下；且标记抑制不必然消除反思行为，模型仍可进行无标记验证。

Conclusion: 拟人化标记倾向于表面线索而非可靠代理，激励未来研究超越显式标记模式的推理机制。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLMs）在复杂推理过程中经常产生显式的反思痕迹，并伴有拟人化标记，如“等等”、“嗯”和“或者”。尽管这些标记通常被用作反思的可见指标，但其机制仍不明确，这带来了与冗余和重复的反思标记相关的过度思考风险。在这项工作中，我们重新审视了拟人化反思标记，考察了它们对推理的必要性以及在反思中的作用。我们通过提示级别和词元级别的干预来抑制这些标记，并分析了它们在四个基准测试和两个模型规模上对任务性能的影响。我们的结果表明，拟人化标记并非对推理性能均匀必要：抑制它们可以在多种设置下保持或提高性能，尤其是在较大的采样预算下。同时，标记抑制并不一定消除反思行为，因为模型仍然可以进行无标记验证。这些表明，拟人化标记往往是表面线索，而不是反思本身的可靠代理，并激励未来研究超越显式标记模式的推理机制。

Original abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) often produce explicit reflective traces during complex reasoning, accompanied by anthropomorphic markers such as wait, hmm, and alternatively. Although these markers are commonly used as visible indicators of reflection, their mechanisms remain unclear, which leaves the risk of overthinking associated with redundant and repetitive reflection markers. In this work, we revisit anthropomorphic reflection markers, examining their necessity for reasoning and role in the reflection. We suppress these markers through prompt-level and token-level interventions, and analyze their effects on task performance across four benchmarks and two model scales. Our results show that anthropomorphic markers are not uniformly necessary for reasoning performance: suppressing them can preserve or improve performance in several settings, especially under larger sampling budgets. Meanwhile, marker suppression does not necessarily remove reflection behavior, as models can still perform marker-free verification. These suggest that anthropomorphic markers tend to be surface cues rather than reliable proxies for reflection itself, and motivate future research on reasoning mechanisms beyond explicit marker patterns.

### [119] [Evaluating the Realism of LLM-powered Social Agents: A Case Study of Reactions to Spanish Online News](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28598v1)
*Alejandro Buitrago López,Alberto Ortega Pastor,Javier Pastor-Galindo,José A. Ruipérez-Valiente*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 评估LLM社交agent真实性，可迁移至agent评测方法。

TL;DR: 评估LLM生成新闻评论的真实性，发现开箱模型表现差，微调改善有限，Qwen3最平衡，Mistral7B情感对齐好但高估仇恨。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究缺乏对短促、反应性话语（如新闻评论）的真实性评估，本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 使用Hatemedia数据集，配对新闻与真实评论，用五个LLM生成合成评论，从仇恨言论、情感、语义对齐三个维度比较真实与合成数据。

Result: 开箱模型明显低估仇恨言论、有情感偏差；微调改善不均，Qwen3最平衡，Mistral7B对齐最好但高估仇恨。

Conclusion: 看似合理的合成回复未必能复现真实话语的分布特性，当前LLM模拟受众反应仍有限。

中文摘要：基于大语言模型的社会化智能体越来越多地被用于模拟在线社交行为，但其真实感仍然难以验证。现有工作主要依赖于通用基准测试，而对短促、反应性的话语（例如受众对在线新闻的回复）关注较少。在本文中，我们评估了LLM生成的西班牙语在线新闻反应是否再现了真实受众话语的可测量属性。利用Hatemedia数据集，我们将5,631条新闻与58,555条真实受众反应配对，并在共享实验设置下使用五个LLM生成匹配的合成数据集。我们从仇恨言论、情感和语义对齐三个维度比较真实和合成反应，同时考虑开箱即用和微调生成。结果表明，开箱即用的模型是真实受众反应的不良代理：它们严重低估仇恨言论，引入特定模型的情感偏差，并且在分布上与人类回复相距甚远。微调改善了保真度但不均匀。Qwen3提供了最平衡的近似，而Mistral7B实现了最强的情感和语义对齐，但高估了仇恨普遍性。看似合理的合成回复不一定再现公共话语的分布特性。

Original abstract: LLM-powered social agents are increasingly used to simulate online social behavior, yet their realism remains difficult to validate. Existing work has largely relied on general-purpose benchmarks, while less attention has been paid to short, reactive discourse such as audience replies to online news.
  In this paper, we evaluate whether LLM-generated reactions to Spanish online news reproduce measurable properties of real audience discourse. Using the Hatemedia dataset, we pair 5,631 news items with 58,555 real audience reactions, and generate a matched synthetic dataset using five LLMs under a shared experimental setting. We compare real and synthetic reactions across three dimensions: hate speech, sentiment, and semantic alignment, considering both off-the-shelf and fine-tuned generation.
  Results show that off-the-shelf models are poor proxies for real audience reactions: they strongly underproduce hate speech, introduce model-specific sentiment biases, and remain distributionally distant from human replies. Fine-tuning improves fidelity unevenly. Qwen3 provides the most balanced approximation, while Mistral7B achieves the strongest sentiment and semantic alignment but overshoots hate prevalence. Plausible synthetic replies do not necessarily reproduce the distributional properties of public discourse.

### [120] [MemTrace: Tracing and Attributing Errors in Large Language Model Memory Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28732v3)
*Xinle Deng,Ruobin Zhong,Hujin Peng,Xiaoben Lu,Yanzhe Wu,Guang Li,Buqiang Xu,Yunzhi Yao,Jizhan Fang,Haoliang Cao,Junjie Guo,Yuan Yuan,Ziqing Ma,Yuanqiang Yu,Rui Hu,Baohua Dong,Hangcheng Zhu,Ningyu Zhang*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 提出LLM记忆系统错误追踪与归因方法，可迁移至agent记忆管理。

TL;DR: 提出MemTrace框架，通过将记忆流水线转化为记忆演化图，并构建MemTraceBench基准和自动归因方法，实现了对LLM记忆系统错误追踪与归因，最终通过归因信号指导提示优化，将端任务性能提升高达7.62%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有记忆系统不可靠且难以调试，而追踪记忆动态演变对于理解信息如何合成、传播或损坏至关重要，因此需要研究错误追踪和归因问题。

Method: 提出将记忆流水线转化为可执行记忆演化图的框架，构建包含多种代表性记忆系统的MemTraceBench基准，并引入自动归因方法通过迭代追踪操作子图定位失败根因。

Result: 分析发现记忆故障是系统性的，源于操作级问题（如信息丢失和检索错位）；利用归因信号指导下游提示优化，建立闭环系统，最终端任务性能提升高达7.62%。

Conclusion: 通过使用细粒度归因信号进行提示优化，实现了自动纠正记忆系统故障并显著提升下游任务性能的闭环系统。

中文摘要：记忆对于使大型语言模型能够支持长程推理至关重要，然而现有的记忆系统仍然不可靠且难以调试。追踪记忆的动态演变对于理解信息如何随时间合成、传播或损坏至关重要。在这项工作中，我们研究了大语言模型记忆系统中的错误追踪和归因这一新问题。我们提出了一种新颖的框架，将记忆流水线转化为可执行的记忆演化图，从而实现操作信息流的细粒度追踪。然后我们构建了MemTraceBench，这是一个从代表性记忆系统（如Long-Context、RAG、Mem0和EverMemOS）收集的基准，用于系统研究记忆故障模式。我们进一步引入了一种自动归因方法，通过迭代追踪操作子图来定位任何失败案例的根本原因。我们的分析表明，记忆故障是系统性的，源于操作级别的问题，如信息丢失和检索错位。关键的是，我们利用这些细粒度的归因信号来指导下游提示优化，建立了一个自动纠正故障并提升最终任务性能高达7.62%的闭环系统。代码将在https://github.com/zjunlp/MemTrace发布。

Original abstract: Memory is essential for enabling large language models to support long-horizon reasoning, yet existing memory systems remain unreliable and difficult to debug. Tracing memory's dynamic evolution is crucial to understand how information is synthesized, propagated, or corrupted over time. In this work, we study the new problem of error tracing and attribution in LLM memory systems. We propose a novel framework that transforms memory pipelines into executable memory evolution graphs, enabling fine-grained tracing of operational information flow. We then construct MemTraceBench, a benchmark collected from representative memory systems such as Long-Context, RAG, Mem0, and EverMemOS, to systematically study memory failure modes. We further introduce an automatic attribution method that iteratively traces operation subgraphs to pinpoint the root cause of any failed case. Our analysis reveals that memory failures are systematic, stemming from operation-level issues like information loss and retrieval misalignment. Crucially, we leverage these fine-grained attribution signals to guide downstream prompt optimization, establishing a closed-loop system that automatically corrects faults and boosts end-task performance by up to 7.62%. Code will be released at https://github.com/zjunlp/MemTrace.

### [121] [Hallucination Detection-Guided Preference Optimization for Clinical Summarization](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28910v3)
*Shamanth Kuthpadi Seethakantha,Dung Ngoc Thai,Vara Prasad Gudi,Simran Tiwari,Rami Matar,Avijit Mitra,Wenlong Zhao,Andrew McCallum,Wael Salloum*

TL;DR: 通过幻觉检测引导的细化和偏好学习，有效减少临床摘要中的幻觉，并保持摘要质量。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 检测引导的细化和偏好学习为改善临床摘要的事实忠实性提供了自动化解决方案。

中文摘要：大型语言模型在摘要任务中显示出潜力，但它们经常产生幻觉，即无根据或不正确的陈述，这限制了它们在专门医疗应用中的可靠性。我们引入幻觉检测引导的自我细化（HDSR），一种推理时方法，利用幻觉检测器引导迭代摘要修订以进行事实更正。在此基础上，我们提出用于偏好学习的HDSR（HDSR-PL），它将检测器引导的细化轨迹转换为偏好对，用于模型微调。大量实验表明，我们的方法在总结来自MIMIC-IV-Note v2.2的真实临床笔记时，显著减少了Llama和Gemma模型的幻觉。例如，HDSR减少了24%的幻觉，HDSR-PL在Llama-3.1-8B-Instruct中减少了48%的幻觉。重要的是，根据人类专家和LLM-Jury评估，这两种方法都保留了摘要的流畅性、连贯性和相关性。总之，这些结果表明，检测引导的细化和偏好学习为改善临床摘要中的事实忠实性提供了自动化解决方案。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have shown promise on summarization tasks, but they often produce hallucinations, which are unsupported or incorrect statements that limit their reliability in specialized healthcare applications. We introduce Hallucination Detection Guided Self-Refinement (HDSR), an inference-time method that leverages hallucination detectors to guide iterative summary revisions toward factual corrections. Building on this, we propose HDSR for Preference Learning (HDSR-PL), which converts detector-guided refinement trajectories into preference pairs for model finetuning. Extensive experiments show that our methods substantially reduce hallucinations for Llama and Gemma models in summarizing real-world clinical notes from MIMIC-IV-Note v2.2. For example, HDSR reduces 24% and HDSR-PL reduces 48% hallucinations in Llama-3.1-8B-Instruct. Importantly, both methods preserve summary fluency, coherence, and relevance according to human expert and LLM-Jury evaluations. Together, these results demonstrate that detection-informed refinement and preference learning offer an automated solution for improving factual faithfulness in clinical summarization.

### [122] [Rethinking Memory as Continuously Evolving Connectivity](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28773v1)
*Jizhan Fang,Buqiang Xu,Zhixian Wang,Haoliang Cao,Xinle Deng,Baohua Dong,Hangcheng Zhu,Ruohui Huang,Gang Yu,Ying Wei,Guozhou Zheng,Feiyu Xiong,Haofen Wang,Huajun Chen,Ningyu Zhang*

Selection reason: 演化连接性记忆框架，适用于agent动态记忆管理。

TL;DR: 提出FluxMem，一种连接演化的记忆框架，通过三阶段拓扑优化实现动态环境下的强适应性和泛化能力，在多个基准上取得SOTA。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有记忆增强型LLM代理的记忆存储静态且检索固定，在动态环境中脆弱，无法适应反馈、任务变化和异构信号。

Method: 将记忆建模为异构图，通过初始连接形成、反馈驱动细化和长期巩固三个阶段逐步优化拓扑，并利用记忆泛化性和演化成熟度指标指导修复、剪枝、对齐和提炼。

Result: 在LoCoMo、Mind2Web和GAIA三个多样基准上取得一致SOTA性能，展示强适应性和泛化能力。

Conclusion: FluxMem通过动态记忆拓扑演化有效提升LLM代理在复杂环境下的表现，是通用且稳健的记忆框架。

中文摘要：现有的记忆增强型LLM代理通常将记忆视为一个具有预定义表示和固定检索管道的静态存储库，这在动态代理环境中是脆弱的，其中反馈、任务变化和异构信号不断重塑应该记住什么以及如何连接。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了FluxMem，一个连接演化的记忆框架，它将记忆建模为异构图，并通过三个阶段逐步优化其拓扑结构：初始连接形成、反馈驱动的细化和长期巩固。在执行过程中，FluxMem修复缺失的连接、剪枝干扰、对齐抽象粒度，并将重复的成功轨迹提炼为可复用的程序化回路，由记忆泛化性和演化成熟度的一个指标指导。在包括LoCoMo、Mind2Web和GAIA在内的三个根本不同的基准测试中，FluxMem取得了一致的最先进性能，展示了在复杂代理环境中的强适应性和泛化能力。代码将开源在https://github.com/zjunlp/LightMem。

Original abstract: Existing memory-augmented LLM agents often treat memory as a static repository with pre-defined representations and fixed retrieval pipelines, which is brittle in dynamic agentic environments where feedback, task variation, and heterogeneous signals continuously reshape what should be remembered and how it should be connected. To address this, we propose FluxMem, a connectivity-evolving memory framework that models memory as a heterogeneous graph and progressively refines its topology through three stages: initial connection formation, feedback-driven refinement, and long-term consolidation. During execution, FluxMem repairs missing links, prunes interference, aligns abstraction granularity, and distills recurrent successful trajectories into reusable procedural circuits, guided by one metric for memory generalizability and evolutionary maturity. Across three fundamentally distinct benchmarks including LoCoMo, Mind2Web, and GAIA, FluxMem achieves consistent state-of-the-art performance, demonstrating strong adaptation and generalization in complex agentic environments. The code will be open-sourced in https://github.com/zjunlp/LightMem.

### [123] [Skill-Conditioned Gated Self-Distillation for LLM Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28791v1)

Result: 在数学推理基准上，SGSD持续优于GRPO，与答案条件OPSD竞争力相当；例如在Qwen3-1.7B上平均提升GRPO 6.2%、OPSD 1.7%。

Conclusion: SGSD在更弱的特权信息假设下有效提升了推理能力，为经验驱动的自蒸馏提供了新范式。

中文摘要：在策略自蒸馏（SD）通过使用教师端的特权信息（PI）将稀疏的验证器结果转化为密集的令牌级监督来提升LLM推理能力。现有方法通常假设可信的PI，例如参考答案或成功轨迹。我们提出疑问：PI是否可能来自经验衍生的技能库，其中检索到的技能紧凑且可重用，但也可能不相关或具有误导性。我们提出了技能条件门控自蒸馏（SGSD），它将基于技能的SD表述为教师假设验证而非无条件模仿。SGSD检索技能-错误对，构建多教师池，并让所有技能条件的教师对相同的纯提示学生轨迹进行评分。验证器验证每位教师的极性：支持成功或抑制失败提供正向监督，而相反立场则被反转。然后，一个鲁棒的门控目标蒸馏出信息丰富的教师-学生分歧，同时抑制不确定或极端的信号。在多个数学推理基准上的实验表明，SGSD在较弱的PI假设下持续优于GRPO，并与答案条件OPSD保持竞争力。例如，在Qwen3-1.7B上，SGSD在AIME24、AIME25和HMMT25上的平均表现比GRPO高出6.2%，比OPSD高出1.7%。我们的代码可在https://github.com/walawalagoose/SGSD获取。

Original abstract: On-policy self-distillation (SD) improves LLM reasoning by using teacher-side privileged information (PI) to turn sparse verifier outcomes into dense token-level supervision. Existing methods usually assume trusted PI, such as reference answers or successful traces. We ask whether PI can instead come from an experience-derived skill bank, where retrieved skills are compact and reusable but may also be irrelevant or misleading. We propose Skill-Conditioned Gated Self-Distillation (SGSD), which formulates skill-based SD as teacher hypothesis validation rather than unconditional imitation. SGSD retrieves skill-mistake pairs, constructs a multi-teacher pool, and lets all skill-conditioned teachers score the same plain-prompt student rollout. The verifier validates each teacher's polarity: supporting a success or suppressing a failure gives positive supervision, while the opposite stance is reversed. A robust gated objective then distills informative teacher-student disagreements while suppressing uncertain or extreme signals. Experiments on multiple mathematical reasoning benchmarks show that SGSD consistently improves over GRPO and remains competitive with answer-conditioned OPSD under a weaker PI assumption. For example, on Qwen3-1.7B, SGSD outperforms GRPO by 6.2% and OPSD by 1.7% on average on AIME24, AIME25, and HMMT25. Our code is available at https://github.com/walawalagoose/SGSD.

</details>


### [124] [OmniVerifier-M1: Multimodal Meta-Verifier with Explicit Structured Recalibration](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28805v1)
*Xinchen Zhang,Bowei Liu,Jiale Liu,Chufan Shi,Yizhen Zhang,Junhong Liu,Youliang Zhang,Zhiheng Li,Yujiu Yang,Ling Yang*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 多模态元验证器用于agent生成系统，提供可解释验证。

TL;DR: 探索多模态元验证，发现符号验证器输出优于文本解释，解耦强化学习目标优于联合优化，训练OmniVerifier-M1实现细粒度验证和自校正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 视觉结果在多模态大语言模型中日益重要，需要可靠且细粒度的验证来扩展通用基础模型。

Method: 研究多模态元验证，利用符号验证器输出作为推理过程，并采用解耦强化学习分别优化二元判断和元验证目标。

Result: 训练OmniVerifier-M1，提供稳健验证和细粒度错误定位，并支持M1-TTS系统实现动态区域级自校正。

Conclusion: 为更可靠、可解释、细粒度的多模态验证铺平道路，支持更安全可控的基础模型部署。

中文摘要：视觉结果在多模态大语言模型中日益重要，因此可靠且细粒度的验证对于扩展通用基础模型至关重要。在这项工作中，我们研究了多模态元验证，即利用验证器生成的推理过程而非仅决策信号，并探索如何有效地将元验证反馈融入多模态验证器训练。我们发现了两个关键结论。首先，符号验证器输出（例如边界框）作为元验证推理过程优于文本解释，能够实现高效的基于规则的强化学习奖励，同时避免依赖来自辅助判断模型的基于模型的奖励。其次，将二元判断和元验证的强化学习目标解耦，显著优于联合奖励优化，这是由于输出结构和学习动态的内在差异。基于这些见解，我们训练了OmniVerifier-M1，一个利用符号元验证和解耦强化学习的通用视觉验证器。OmniVerifier-M1提供稳健的验证和细粒度的错误定位，并进一步实现了M1-TTS，一个由验证器驱动的智能体生成系统，能够实现动态区域级自校正。该方法为更可靠、可解释和细粒度的多模态验证铺平了道路，支持更安全且更可控的基础模型部署。

Original abstract: Visual outcomes are increasingly central to multimodal large language models, making reliable and fine-grained verification essential for scaling generalist foundation models. In this work, we investigate multimodal meta-verification, which leverages verifier-generated rationales rather than decision-only signals, and explore how to effectively incorporate meta-verification feedback into multimodal verifier training. We identify two key findings. First, symbolic verifier outputs (e.g., bounding boxes) outperform textual explanations as meta-verification rationales, enabling efficient rule-based reinforcement learning rewards while avoiding reliance on model-based rewards from auxiliary judge models. Second, decoupling reinforcement learning objectives for binary judgment and meta-verification substantially outperforms joint reward optimization, due to intrinsic differences in output structure and learning dynamics. Based on these insights, we train OmniVerifier-M1, a generalist visual verifier leveraging symbolic meta-verification and decoupled reinforcement learning. OmniVerifier-M1 provides robust verification and fine-grained error localization, and further enables M1-TTS, a verifier-driven agentic generation system achieving dynamic region-level self-correction. This approach paves the way for more reliable, interpretable, and fine-grained multimodal verification, supporting safer and more controllable foundation model deployment.

</details>

### [125] [Turning Video Models into Generalist Robot Policies](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27817v1)
*Sizhe Lester Li,Evan Kim,Xingjian Bai,Tong Zhao,Tao Pang,Max Simchowitz,Vincent Sitzmann*

Main category: cs.RO

Selection reason: 将视频模型解耦为planner和IDM，生成机器人策略，思路可迁移至decoupled agent设计。

TL;DR: 本文提出VERA，通过解耦视频规划器和实体特定的逆动力学模型，实现零样本、跨实体的机器人控制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有机器人基础模型需要大量动作标签数据，且视频模型与动作模型耦合紧密，迁移性差。作者希望探索一种解耦方法，保持视频模型不变，仅训练轻量级的IDM，从而提升数据效率和跨实体泛化能力。

Method: 提出VERA框架，包括一个无动作视频世界模型（视频规划器）和一个基于机器人实体雅可比矩阵设计的逆动力学模型（IDM）。视频规划器生成未来观察序列，IDM将观察序列映射为具体动作。IDM可独立使用自对弈数据训练，且不同实体只需更换对应的IDM。

Result: 在零样本Panda手臂操作和16自由度Allegro手灵巧重定向任务上取得强劲性能，验证了解耦方法的有效性。相同的视频规划器可通过不同IDM用于多个实体。

Conclusion: 解耦的视频规划加忠实的视频到动作转换是实现零样本、跨实体、可泛化机器人控制的可行替代路线。

中文摘要：视频生成模型已成为一种有前途的机器人骨干网络，能够生成展示跨实体和环境的复杂任务完成的视频。最近的工作提出了机器人基础模型，通过使用带有动作标签的数据微调视频模型，共同预测未来的观测和动作。在本文中，我们测试了一种替代方法的局限性：保持视频规划器不变，同时训练一个特定于实体的逆动力学模型（IDM）。这种解耦带来了几个自然的好处：视频规划器保持实体无关，不同的视频模型可以轻松互换而无需重新训练IDM，并且IDM可以独立使用现成的自对弈数据进行训练。我们提出了一种闭环的视频到动作策略，该策略将无动作视频世界模型与基于机器人实体雅可比矩阵精心设计的IDM相结合。我们证明了我们的IDM设计既数据高效又可扩展到高维动作空间。我们的策略，我们称之为视频到实体机器人动作模型（VERA），在模拟和真实世界基准测试中取得了强劲的性能，包括零样本Panda手臂操作和16自由度Allegro手灵巧立方体重定向。通过将相同的视频规划器与不同的特定实体IDM配对，它可以用于多个实体。我们的结果表明，解耦的视频规划加上忠实的视频到动作转换是实现零样本、跨实体和可泛化机器人控制的可行替代途径。更多结果可在我们的项目网站上找到：https://vera.csail.mit.edu。

Original abstract: Video generative models have emerged as a promising robotics backbone, capable of generating videos that depict the completion of complex tasks across embodiments and environments. Recent work proposes robot foundation models that jointly predict future observations and actions by finetuning video models with action-labeled data. In this paper, we test the limits of an alternative approach: leave the video planner as-is while training an embodiment-specific inverse dynamics model (IDM). This decoupling offers several natural benefits: the video planner remains embodiment-agnostic, different video models can be interchanged easily without re-training the IDM, and the IDM can be independently trained with readily available self-play data. We present a closed-loop, video-to-action policy that combines an action-free video world model with a carefully-designed IDM based on the robot embodiment Jacobian. We demonstrate that our IDM design is both data-efficient and scalable to high-dimensional action spaces. Our policy, which we coin the Video-to-Embodied Robot Action Model (VERA), achieves strong performance across simulated and real-world benchmarks, including zero-shot Panda arm manipulation and 16-DoF Allegro-hand dexterous cube re-orientation. The same video planner can be used across multiple embodiments by pairing it with different embodiment-specific IDMs. Our results show that decoupled video planning plus faithful video-to-action translation is a viable alternative route towards zero-shot, cross-embodiment, and generalizable robot control. More results are available on our project website: https://vera.csail.mit.edu.

</details>
