### [126] [When Think-with-Image Meets Safety: What Determines Multimodal Jailbreak Robustness?](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27932v1)
*Yuan Tian,Bing Hu,Fang Wu,Xiaomin Li,Binghang Lu,Neil Zhenqiang Gong*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: 多模态jailbreak安全性分析，对agent安全控制有启发。

TL;DR: 显式图像工具交互能显著降低多模态越狱攻击成功率，其机制是引入安全相关的表示偏移。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究不同Think-with-image推理范式对多模态越狱鲁棒性的影响，并解释显式图像工具交互为何更安全。

Method: 通过实验比较多种视觉-语言模型下的不同推理范式，引入图像工具安全向量框架进行表征分析。

Result: 显式图像工具交互将越狱攻击成功率平均降低约30%，且该效果不受返回图像语义或文本痕迹影响。

Conclusion: 显式图像工具交互是提升越狱鲁棒性的有效设计模式，需针对特定管道进行安全评估。

中文摘要：带图像推理正在成为大型视觉-语言模型的一种新兴推理范式，但其安全性影响仍知之甚少。现有系统已经涵盖了多种过程设计，包括直接响应生成、仅文本的前一轮、视觉状态操作以及显式外部图像工具调用。在本文中，我们探讨这些评估范式中的哪一种提高了多模态越狱鲁棒性，以及原因。在多个视觉-语言模型中，显式图像工具交互在我们的实验中实现了最低的攻击成功率，在评估模型上平均相对降低了约30%的越狱成功率。这一发现最初令人惊讶：即使返回的图像工具输出被手动覆盖或本身看起来不安全，ASR仍然较低，但在仅文本前一轮控制下恢复到接近直接回答的水平。这些结果表明，较低的ASR不能用良性返回图像语义或仅文本图像工具痕迹来解释。为了解释这一模式，我们引入了一个图像工具安全向量框架，将图像工具调用建模为隐藏表示向安全相关方向的残差偏移。表示层面的分析和激活干预支持了这一解释。总体而言，我们的结果表明，显式图像工具交互是提高越狱鲁棒性的一种有前景的设计模式，同时也促使进行管道特定的安全评估。

Original abstract: Think-with-image reasoning is emerging as a new inference paradigm for large vision-language models, but its safety implications remain poorly understood. Existing systems already span multiple process designs, including direct response generation, text-only prior turn, visual-state manipulation, and explicit external image-tool invocation. In this paper, we ask which of these evaluated paradigms improves multimodal jailbreak robustness, and why. Across multiple vision-language models, explicit image-tool interaction yields the lowest attack success rates in our experiments, reducing jailbreak success by around 30% relative on average across the evaluated models. This finding is initially surprising: ASR remains low even when the returned image-tool output is manually overridden or itself unsafe-looking, but returns near direct-answering levels under text-only prior turn controls. These results indicate that the lower ASR is not explained by benign returned-image semantics or by the textual image-tool trace alone. To explain the pattern, we introduce an image-tool safety vector framework that models image-tool invocation as a residual shift in hidden representations toward a safety-relevant direction. Representation-level analyses and activation interventions support this account. Overall, our results suggest that explicit image-tool interaction is a promising design pattern for improving jailbreak robustness, while also motivating pipeline-specific safety evaluation.

</details>


### [127] [ROVER: Routing Object-Centric Visual Evidence for Grounded Multi-Image Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27959v2)
*Guannan Lv,Ren Nie,Hongjian Dou,Tingting Gao*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: 轻量级推理插件ROVER，可迁移至agent推理模块。

TL;DR: 提出ROVER插件，通过对象中心差分注意力和三步令牌机制实现高效全局视觉证据路由，在多图像接地推理中取得SOTA性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于接地的方法削弱整体场景理解且解码成本高，自适应特征选择需要细粒度监督或复杂启发式。

Method: ROVER是一个轻量可学习插件，在每次对象接地预测时注入步骤特定令牌三元组，分别聚合上下文、提取图像内线索到视觉工作空间、路由整合历史感知证据。集成到Qwen2.5-VL-7B并通过SFT-to-GRPO训练。

Result: 在MM-GCoT上答案准确率+4.8%、接地准确率+14.6%，VideoEspresso上答案准确率+8.6%，迁移性使平均性能提升4.7%。

Conclusion: ROVER有效弥补现有方法缺陷，实现高效全局证据路由，提升多图像推理性能并展现强迁移能力。

中文摘要：多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）越来越倾向于定位和交错视觉证据以进行深思熟虑的推理。基于接地的方法通常通过将裁剪的图像块或特定于RoI的特征注入推理上下文来关注感兴趣区域（RoIs）。然而，这种设计可能会削弱整体场景理解和对象间关系，同时产生与RoI数量和大小成比例的解码成本。或者，自适应视觉特征选择通常需要细粒度监督或复杂启发式方法。为了解决这些局限性，我们提出了ROVER（用于接地多图像推理的路由目标中心视觉证据），这是一种轻量级、可学习的插件，用于高效的全局视觉证据路由。在每次对象接地预测时，ROVER注入一个特定步骤的标记三元组，以协同地：(i)聚合正在进行的推理上下文，(ii)通过以对象为中心的差分注意力将图像内线索提取到视觉工作空间中，以及(iii)在此空间内跨对象和图像路由和整合历史感知的证据，以供后续推理。我们将ROVER集成到Qwen2.5-VL-7B中，并开发了一个交错的SFT到GRPO训练流程。严格遵守原始数据集和评估协议，我们的方法在MM-GCoT（答案准确率+4.8%，接地准确率+14.6%）和VideoEspresso（答案准确率+8.6%）上取得了最佳性能。在VideoEspresso上训练的模型表现出强大的迁移能力，在各种基准测试上平均超过基础模型4.7%。

Original abstract: Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) have increasingly localized and interleaved visual evidence for deliberative reasoning. Grounding-based approaches typically focus on regions of interest (RoIs) by injecting cropped image patches or RoI-specific features into the reasoning context. However, such designs can weaken holistic scene understanding and inter-object relations, while incurring decoding costs that scale with the number and size of RoIs. Alternatively, adaptive visual feature selection often requires fine-grained supervision or complex heuristics. To address these limitations, we propose ROVER (Routing Object-centric Visual Evidence for grounded multi-image Reasoning), a lightweight, learnable plugin for efficient global visual evidence routing. Upon each object grounding prediction, ROVER injects a step-specific token triplet to synergistically: (i) aggregate the ongoing reasoning context, (ii) distill intra-image cues into a visual working space via object-centric differential attention, and (iii) route and integrate history-aware evidence across objects and images within this space for subsequent reasoning. We integrate ROVER into Qwen2.5-VL-7B and develop an interleaved SFT-to-GRPO training pipeline. Strictly adhering to the original datasets and evaluation protocols, our method achieves the best performance on MM-GCoT (+4.8% answer accuracy, +14.6% grounding accuracy) and VideoEspresso (+8.6% answer accuracy). The VideoEspresso-trained model demonstrates strong transferability, outperforming the base model by +4.7% on average across diverse benchmarks.

</details>

# cs.CR [[Back]](#toc)

### [128] [Disentangling Adversarial Prompts: A Semantic-Graph Defense for Robust LLM Security](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27823v1)
*Xiang Fang,Wanlong Fang*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: LLM安全防御框架，对抗提示检测，对agent安全控制有启发。

TL;DR: 提出APD框架，通过语义分解、图意图分类和轻量级Transformer分类器，在LLM输入前检测并中和对抗性提示，减少85%以上有害输出，且对性能影响小。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLMs易受利用语义歧义的对抗性提示攻击（如越狱、提示注入），现有防御不足，需主动检测和中和恶意成分以保障安全。

Method: APD框架包含三个创新：基于互信息的语义分解隔离对抗与良性成分、基于图的频谱分析检测恶意模式、轻量级Transformer分类器高效识别对抗意图。

Result: 在多样数据集上，APD减少有害输出超过85%，对模型性能影响极小，计算效率支持实时部署。

Conclusion: APD提供可扩展、合乎道德的防御，有效应对基于提示的对抗性威胁，解决ML安全中的关键挑战。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLMs）越来越容易受到利用语义歧义绕过安全机制的对抗性提示的攻击，导致有害或不适当的输出。这些攻击，包括越狱和提示注入，对LLMs在安全关键型应用中的完整性和可用性构成了重大风险。本文提出了对抗性提示解缠（APD）框架，这是一种新颖的防御机制，能够在输入提示被LLM处理之前主动识别并中和其中的恶意成分。APD框架集成了三个关键创新：（1）基于互信息的语义分解方法，用于隔离对抗性和良性提示成分，确保统计独立性；（2）基于图的意图分类方法，利用频谱分析检测提示语义中的恶意模式；（3）轻量级基于Transformer的分类器，在真实的毒性和越狱提示数据集上训练，实现高效准确的对抗性意图检测。在包含对抗性提示的多样化数据集上评估，APD展示了卓越的鲁棒性，将有害输出生成减少了超过85%，同时保持对模型性能的影响微乎其微。该框架的计算效率支持实时部署，使其成为保护LLMs的实用解决方案。我们的工作解决了机器学习安全中关于新型攻击和ML系统完整性方法的关键挑战，并提供了一种可扩展、合乎道德的防御措施来应对基于提示的对抗性威胁。

Original abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly vulnerable to adversarial prompts that exploit semantic ambiguities to bypass safety mechanisms, resulting in harmful or inappropriate outputs. Such attacks, including jailbreaking and prompt injection, pose significant risks to the integrity and availability of LLMs in security-critical applications. This paper proposes the Adversarial Prompt Disentanglement (APD) framework, a novel defense mechanism that proactively identifies and neutralizes malicious components in input prompts before they are processed by the LLM. The APD framework integrates three key innovations: (1) a mutual information-based semantic decomposition method to isolate adversarial and benign prompt components, ensuring statistical independence; (2) a graph-based intent classification approach that leverages spectral analysis to detect malicious patterns in prompt semantics; and (3) a lightweight transformer-based classifier trained on real-world datasets of toxic and jailbreaking prompts, enabling efficient and accurate adversarial intent detection. Evaluated on diverse datasets containing adversarial prompts, APD demonstrates superior robustness, reducing harmful output generation by over 85\% while maintaining negligible impact on model performance. The framework's computational efficiency supports real-time deployment, making it a practical solution for securing LLMs. Our work addresses critical challenges in machine learning security on novel attacks and integrity methods for ML systems, and offers a scalable, ethically grounded defense against prompt-based adversarial threats.

</details>


### [129] [MIRAGE: Context-Aware Prompt Injection against Mobile GUI Agents via User-Generated Content](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28116v1)
*Ruoqi Guo,Yi Liu,Gelei Deng,Yiheng Xiong,Yuekang Li,Ying Zhang,Leo Yu Zhang,Lida Zhao,Ji Jie,Yuxiao Lu*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 针对移动GUI agent的提示注入攻击，对agent安全性评估有参考价值

TL;DR: MIRAGE是一种将移动截图转为提示注入样本的流水线，通过注入用户内容区域中攻击者控制的文本，成功攻击多个VLM代理，且与先前攻击相比具有更高真实性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有VLM驱动的GUI代理无法区分可信界面与用户生成内容，易受提示注入攻击，但缺乏真实且分布平衡的注入样本生成方法。

Method: MIRAGE分为三个阶段：Localizer定位用户可控区域，Generator生成并渲染上下文相关有效载荷，Curator审查真实性和平衡样本分布。

Result: 在1111样本基准上，五个VLM代理攻击成功率为23%-30%，MIRAGE真实性评分（3.02/5）优于先前攻击（2.52/5），且真实性与攻击成功率不相关。

Conclusion: MIRAGE揭示了移动GUI代理的提示注入脆弱性，并表明视觉质量过滤不足以防御，需更全面的安全措施。

中文摘要：由视觉语言模型驱动的移动图形用户界面（GUI）代理通过感知屏幕上的渲染像素并根据所见选择动作，因此无法可靠地区分可信界面元素与用户生成的内容。我们提出了MIRAGE（移动真实对抗性GUI示例注入），这是一个流水线，通过将攻击者控制的文本放入普通的用户生成内容区域，将良性移动截图转化为提示注入样本，且无需修改代理、应用程序或操作系统。MIRAGE分三个阶段运行：定位器识别截图上的用户可控区域，生成器合成上下文相关的有效载荷并以应用程序的原生样式渲染，策展人调节真实性并平衡跨应用程序、区域类型和攻击意图的样本。一个关键挑战是，注入的截图必须在视觉上与真实用户内容无法区分，同时仍能转移代理；我们通过分离控制覆盖范围、真实性和分布平衡的阶段来解决这一问题。在涵盖十个应用程序和十一种攻击意图的1,111个样本基准上，所有五个被评估的VLM代理均易受攻击，攻击成功率为23%-30%，并且MIRAGE在人类真实性评分上高于先前最强的攻击（3.02对2.52，满分5分）。我们进一步发现，每个样本的真实性和攻击成功率不相关，因此仅凭视觉质量过滤无法可靠防御这一威胁。

Original abstract: Mobile graphical user interface (GUI) agents driven by vision-language models (VLMs) perceive the screen as rendered pixels and choose actions from what they see, so they cannot reliably separate trusted interface elements from user-generated content. We present MIRAGE (Mobile Injection of Realistic Adversarial GUI Examples), a pipeline that turns benign mobile screenshots into prompt-injection samples by placing attacker-controlled text into ordinary user-generated content regions, without modifying the agent, the application, or the operating system. MIRAGE operates in three stages: a Localizer identifies user-controllable regions on the screenshot, a Generator synthesises context-aware payloads and renders them in the application's native style, and a Curator moderates realism and balances the samples across applications, region types, and attack intents. A key challenge is that an injected screenshot must stay visually indistinguishable from genuine user content while still diverting the agent; we address this by separating the stages that control reach, realism, and distributional balance. On a 1,111-sample benchmark spanning ten applications and eleven attack intents, all five evaluated VLM agents are vulnerable, with attack success rates of 23%-30%, and MIRAGE scores higher on human realism ratings than the strongest prior attack (3.02 versus 2.52 out of 5). We further find that per-sample realism and attack success are uncorrelated, so visual-quality filtering alone cannot reliably defend against this threat.

</details>


### [130] [SNARE: Adaptive Scenario Synthesis for Eliciting Overeager Behavior in Coding Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28122v1)
*Yubin Qu,Yi Liu,Gelei Deng,Yanjun Zhang,Yuekang Li,Ying Zhang,Leo Yu Zhang*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 直接针对coding agent的过度行为测试与基准生成，对SemOpt可靠性验证重要

TL;DR: 编码代理在执行良性任务时存在过度热心行为，SNARE管道检测到19.51%的运行会触发，且主要受代理框架影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准无法检测编码代理在执行良性任务时的越权行为（过度热心），需要新方法。

Method: 提出SNARE管道，从可重用范围和陷阱片段组合良性场景，用无评判oracle评分，并利用汤普森采样优化测试预算分配。

Result: 在10,000次良性运行中19.51%触发过度热心，代理框架解释56%的变化（模型仅21%），每对比率差异达11.9倍。

Conclusion: 过度热心行为普遍且与代理框架强相关，单框架或单模型评估会显著低估风险。

中文摘要：一个编码代理将良性任务执行为一系列shell、文件和网络操作，其中任何操作都可能悄然超出授权范围，而任务仍然完成。我们将此称为过度热心行为：提示并非对抗性且运行成功，但超出范围的一步可能泄露凭证或删除文件。现有基准无法检测到：任务完成套件认可任何完成的运行，越狱套件探测对抗性提示，而先前唯一的一个过度热心基准对每个代理-模型对应用单一的固定提示集，使得其最易和最难的配对测量不足。我们提出SNARE（为非对抗性场景合成适应奖励引导的诱导），这是一个从可重用范围和陷阱片段组合良性场景的管道，使用无评判的oracle通过标记陷阱模式匹配和非请求的文件添加或删除来评分每次运行，并使用汤普森采样将每对运行的预算引导到最常触发它的场景。在24个过度热心原型上实例化它得出了OverEager，我们在四个编码代理和五个基础模型的4x5矩阵上运行。在10,000次良性运行中，19.51%触发了过度热心行为，每对比率变化达11.9倍。这种变化由代理框架驱动，而非模型：框架占56%，而模型占21%，因此任何单框架或单模型评估都会低估矩阵约五分之一。

Original abstract: A coding agent executes a benign task as a sequence of shell, file, and network actions, any of which can quietly exceed the authorized scope while the task still completes. We call this overeager behavior: the prompt is not adversarial and the run succeeds, yet an out-of-scope step can leak credentials or delete files. Existing benchmarks miss it: task-completion suites credit any finished run, jailbreak suites probe adversarial prompts, and the one prior overeager benchmark applies a single fixed prompt set to every agent-model pair, leaving its easiest and most resistant pairs under-measured. We present SNARE (Synthesizing Non-adversarial scenarios for Adaptive Reward-guided Elicitation), a pipeline that composes benign scenarios from reusable scope and trap fragments, scores each run with a judge-free oracle flagging trap-pattern matches and unsolicited file additions or deletions, and uses Thompson sampling to steer each pair's run budget toward the scenarios that most often trigger it. Instantiating it over 24 overeager archetypes yields OverEager, which we run across a 4x5 matrix of four coding agents and five base models. Across 10,000 benign runs, 19.51% trigger overeager behavior, with per-pair rates spanning 11.9x. This variation is driven by the agent framework, not the model: the framework accounts for 56% of it against the model's 21%, so any single-framework or single-model evaluation undercounts the matrix by about a fifth.

</details>


### [131] [Technical Report: Exploring the Emerging Threats of the Agent Skill Ecosystem](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28588v1)
*Luca Beurer-Kellner,Aleksei Kudrinskii,Marco Milanta,Kristian Bonde Nielsen,Hemang Sarkar,Liran Tal*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 发现76个恶意负载，13.4%有严重问题，8个仍公开可用。

Conclusion: 自动化安全分析是必要的，市场需要加强安全审查。

Original abstract: We analyzed 3,984 AI agent skills from major marketplaces and found 76 confirmed malicious payloads, including credential theft, backdoor installation, and data exfiltration. 13.4% of all skills contain at least one critical-level security issue and at least 8 manually confirmed malicious skills remain publicly available on clawhub.ai as of the date of publication. This report documents our methodology, presents a threat taxonomy based on real-world samples, and details the attack patterns we observed. As skill marketplaces grow rapidly and AI agents gain access to sensitive credentials and systems, automated security analysis is no longer optional.

### [132] [AIRGuard: Guarding Agent Actions with Runtime Authority Control](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28914v1)
*Suliu Qin,Haomin Zhuang,Yujun Zhou,Yufei Han,Xiangliang Zhang*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 运行时权限控制保护agent动作，agent安全通用方法。

TL;DR: AIRGuard是一种运行时防护机制，通过动作时授权实现最小权限原则，有效防御针对工具使用语言智能体的权威混淆攻击，在降低攻击成功率的同时保持较高良性效用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 工具使用语言智能体的攻击模式不同于传统越狱攻击，其危害来自攻击者控制上下文将授权访问导向有害外部动作，现有防御不足。

Method: 提出AIRGuard运行时防护，包括标准化工具调用、步骤级权限派生、信任追踪、副作用模拟、跨步骤风险审计和动作前强制执行。

Result: AgentTrap上攻击成功率从36.3%降至5.5%；DTAP-150上良性效用76.0%（Haiku 4.5），优于ARGUS（52.0%）和MELON（42.0%）。

Conclusion: 专用运行时权威控制层比仅提示策略更有效，为智能体系统提供直接的工具副作用控制能力。

中文摘要：使用工具的语言智能体将模型决策转化为外部副作用：它们读取文件、运行脚本、调用API、发送消息以及调用模型上下文协议工具。这使得针对智能体的攻击与越狱攻击不同。有害步骤通常不是明显被禁止的输出，而是一个普通的可执行动作，之所以变得不安全是因为攻击者控制的上下文将授权访问导向了违背用户利益的方向。我们将这种失败模式识别为权威混淆：不可信的资源可以参与推理，但不能授权副作用。我们提出了AIRGuard，一个运行时防护机制，将最小权限原则操作为动作时授权。AIRGuard标准化异构工具调用，将任务权限分解为步骤级权限，追踪源和目标信任，模拟敏感副作用，审计跨步骤风险，并在动作执行前执行决策。在AgentTrap上，AIRGuard将Sonnet 4.6的攻击成功率从无防御时的36.3%降低到5.5%。在DTAP-150上，AIRGuard在Haiku 4.5上保持了76.0%的良性效用，而ARGUS为52.0%，MELON为42.0%。消融实验进一步表明，仅靠提示策略的帮助有限，而专用的运行时权威控制层使智能体系统能够直接控制工具介导的副作用。代码和数据可在https://github.com/Sophie508/AIRGuard获取。

Original abstract: Tool-using language agents turn model decisions into external side effects: they read files, run scripts, call APIs, send messages, and invoke Model Context Protocol tools. This makes agent attacks different from jailbreaks. The harmful step is often not an obviously forbidden output, but an ordinary executable action that becomes unsafe because attacker-controlled context steers authorized access against the user's interest. We identify this failure mode as authority confusion: untrusted resources may inform reasoning, but they must not authorize side effects. We present AIRGuard, a runtime guard that operationalizes least privilege as action-time authorization. AIRGuard normalizes heterogeneous tool calls, derives task authority into step-level authority, tracks source and target trust, simulates sensitive side effects, audits cross-step risk, and enforces decisions before actions execute. On AgentTrap, AIRGuard reduces Sonnet 4.6 attack success from 36.3% without defense to 5.5%. On DTAP-150, AIRGuard preserves 76.0% benign utility with Haiku 4.5, compared with 52.0% for ARGUS and 42.0% for MELON. An ablation further shows that prompt-only policy helps only modestly, whereas a dedicated runtime authority-control layer gives the agent system direct control over tool-mediated side effects. Code and data are available at https://github.com/Sophie508/AIRGuard.

</details>


### [133] [Measuring Real-World Prompt Injection Attacks in LLM-based Resume Screening](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28999v1)
*Mohan Zhang,Yuqi Jia,Zhen Tan,Steven Jiang,Neil Zhenqiang Gong,Tianlong Chen,Dawn Song*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 真实世界提示注入攻击测量，对agent安全有启发

TL;DR: 首次系统研究LLM在简历筛选中面临的提示注入攻击，基于20万份真实简历发现约1%存在注入，且近年显著增加，多数注入不显式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM的提示注入漏洞在学术和案例中已被展示，但在真实LLM应用中的影响和普遍性未知，需大规模实证研究。

Method: 设计针对简历的提示注入检测方法，通过手动验证小规模数据集确保高精度，然后应用于20万份真实简历进行测量。

Result: 约1%简历含隐藏提示注入，过去一两年比例显著上升，超过90%的注入不使用显式指令。

Conclusion: 首次提供真实LLM应用中大规模提示注入的证据，为后续理解和防御此类攻击奠定基础。

中文摘要：LLM容易受到提示注入攻击。然而，这种漏洞主要是在学术研究中概念性地展示，或通过少数案例研究进行说明。其在现实世界中基于LLM的应用中的普遍性和影响尚未得到充分探索。在这项工作中，我们首次针对一个广泛使用的应用——基于LLM的简历筛选——进行了提示注入攻击的系统研究。我们的分析基于hireEZ收集的多年约20万份真实简历。我们首先设计了针对性的方法来检测简历中的提示注入。在小规模数据集上的手动验证表明，我们的检测器实现了高精度，并优于最先进的通用检测器。随后，我们将检测器应用于完整简历数据集，并对真实世界的提示注入攻击进行了全面的测量研究。我们的分析揭示了几个有趣的发现：约1%的简历包含隐藏的提示注入；此类注入简历的普遍性在过去一两年中显著增加；超过90%的注入提示不使用明确的指令。这些结果为现实世界中基于LLM的应用中存在大规模提示注入提供了首个证据，并为未来理解和缓解此类攻击的研究奠定了基础。

Original abstract: LLMs are vulnerable to prompt injection attacks. However, this vulnerability has been primarily demonstrated conceptually in academic studies or through a few anecdotal case studies. Its prevalence and impact in real-world LLM-based applications are largely unexplored. In this work, we present the first systematic study of prompt-injection attacks in a widely used application: LLM-based resume screening. Our analysis is based on approximately 200K real-world resumes collected over multiple years by hireEZ. We first design tailored methods to detect prompt injection in resumes. Manual validation on a small-scale dataset demonstrates that our detectors achieve high precision and outperform state-of-the-art general-purpose detectors. We then apply our detector to the full resume dataset and conduct a comprehensive measurement study of real-world prompt injection attacks. Our analysis reveals several intriguing findings: approximately 1% of resumes contain hidden prompt injections; the prevalence of such injected resumes has increased noticeably over the past one to two years; and more than 90% of injected prompts do not use explicit instructions. These results provide the first evidence of large-scale prompt injection in real-world LLM-based applications and lay the groundwork for future studies to understand and mitigate such attacks.

</details>


### [134] [unix-ctf: Procedural Environments for Unix-Competence Reinforcement Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29115v1)
*Geoffrey Bradway,Roger Creus Castanyer,Lorenz Wolf,Maxwill Lin,Matthew James Sargent,Augustine N. Mavor-Parker*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: Unix shell agent训练环境，直接涉及coding agent与工具使用。

TL;DR: 本文提出 unix-ctf，一个通过 LLM 辅助合成生成 Unix 旗标收割任务的框架，用于训练和评估 shell 智能体的 Unix 能力，实验表明该能力可分离且可训练，微调效果显著。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有终端基准测试未能区分 Unix 能力和编程能力，导致 Unix 能力提升被忽视；需要专门的训练与评估方法。

Method: 设计 unix-ctf 过程生成器，通过 LLM 辅助流水线合成隐藏-寻找脚本对，经双向契约过滤，生成大量可移植的 Unix 旗标任务。

Result: 流水线成功率 87.5%（656/750），含 155 种独特技术；微调 Qwen3-8B 后解决率从 11.6% 升至 43.6%，取证领域提升 33 个百分点。

Conclusion: Unix 能力是可分离、可训练的，直接评估优于将之纳入编程能力评估。

中文摘要：Unix能力是指将 shell 和操作系统原语作为一等工具使用的能力，而不仅仅是能通过终端编写程序。当前的终端基准测试往往模糊了这一区别：一个精通 Python 但 Unix 能力弱的求解器可以通过 Terminal-Bench 2.0 的相当一部分测试，而相反的能力分布却很少得到锻炼。我们将这一区别操作化，并为 Unix 组件构建了一个训练面。unix-ctf 是一个为 shell 智能体生成夺旗式任务的过程生成器。每个任务在一个全新的 Linux 容器中使用单个 Unix 特性隐藏一个短令牌（形式为 flag(a3b1c9...) 的旗标），智能体必须恢复它。任务由一个 LLM 辅助的合成流水线生成，该流水线产生候选隐藏技术，将它们重写为参数化的隐藏-寻找脚本对，并通过双向契约进行过滤：隐藏脚本不得在磁盘上留下旗标的明文痕迹，寻找脚本必须在一个全新目录中恢复旗标。由于 LLM 只编写植入和恢复步骤（容器、布局和评分框架是固定的），该流水线将 750 次原始尝试中的 656 次转化为可移植、可复用的变体（87.5%）。我们复现的 Endless Terminals 全容器生成方法在相同检查下只达到 17.4%。656 个变体规范化为 155 种不同技术。使用 GRPO 通过 LoRA 对 Qwen3-8B 进行微调后，在包含 15 种技能的多种族留出集（n=225）上，解决率从 11.6% 提升到 43.6%；重新分配了模型解决的 InterCode-CTF 任务；在取证领域实现了 +33 个百分点的提升，并在 InterCode-CTF 上达到 32/100。这些结果表明，Unix 能力是可分离、可训练的，并且最好直接评估，而不是归入编程通过终端的范畴。

Original abstract: Unix competence is the ability to use shell and operating-system primitives as first-class tools, not merely to write programs through a terminal. Current terminal benchmarks tend to blur this distinction: a solver fluent in Python but weak in Unix can pass a substantial fraction of Terminal-Bench 2.0, while the reverse skill profile is rarely exercised. We make the distinction operational and build a training surface for the Unix component. unix-ctf is a procedural generator of capture-the-flag tasks for shell agents. Each task hides a short token (a flag of the form flag(a3b1c9...)) inside a fresh Linux container using a single Unix feature, and the agent must recover it. Tasks are produced by an LLM-assisted synthesis pipeline that generates candidate hiding techniques, rewrites them into parameterized hide-and-find script pairs, and filters them with a bidirectional contract: the hide script must leave no plaintext trace of the flag on disk, and the find script must recover the flag in a fresh directory. Because the LLM only writes the planting and recovery steps (the container, layout, and grading harness are fixed), the pipeline lands 656 of 750 raw attempts as portable, reusable variants (87.5\%). Our reproduction of Endless Terminals' full-container-generation approach lands only 17.4\% under the same checks. The 656 variants canonicalize to 155 distinct techniques. Fine-tuning Qwen3-8B with LoRA using GRPO on this surface lifts solve rate from 11.6\% to 43.6\% on a 15-skill multi-family holdout (n=225), redistributes which InterCode-CTF tasks the model solves, and produces a +33 pp gain in Forensics while reaching 32/100 on InterCode-CTF. These results suggest that Unix competence is separable, trainable, and best evaluated directly rather than folded into programming-through-a-shell.

</details>


<div id='cs.CE'></div>

# cs.CE [[Back]](#toc)

### [135] [Closed-Loop Molecular Design with Calibrated Deference](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02618v1)
*Newman Cheng,Gordon Broadbent,Jason Dong,Syed Mohammed Ali Hussaini,Farman Ullah,Morris Sharp,Gabrielle Barnes,Nanlin Guo,Deyu Zou,Karin Strauss,William Chappell,David G. Kwabi,Bichlien H. Nguyen,Jake A. Smith*

Main category: cs.CE

Selection reason: 闭环分子设计agent，包含计划-行动-自纠正循环，通用agent架构可迁移

TL;DR: CLIO结合持续更新的置信状态图与递归规划-执行循环，在AORFB负极液设计中实现校准的服从，成功识别并解决预测未捕捉的电化学可逆性问题，通过机制假设与实验闭环优化候选物。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI智能体缺乏在自身工具或假设失败时自适应调整的能力，无法生成机制性假设指导实验修订，限制了其在复杂科学发现中的效用。

Method: 提出CLIO框架，包含不断更新的置信状态图和递归的规划-执行循环，通过原位优化实现校准的服从，在闭环人机实验中指导AORFB负极液设计与改进。

Result: 在17个候选物中收敛到膦酸酯候选物，氧化还原电位提升130 mV；发现意外可逆性差后，CLIO生成机制假设、诊断出离子配对问题，并建议磺酸酯替代，最终化合物可逆性显著改善，电位提升90 mV。

Conclusion: CLIO实现了智能体在科学发现中自适应识别工具失败、生成机制假设并指导实验迭代的能力，有效闭环设计-制造-测试-重新设计循环，展示了人机协作的潜力。

中文摘要：我们提出了通过原位优化的认知循环（CLIO），一种将持续更新的置信状态图与递归的计划-执行循环相结合的智能体。结果是一个推理智能体，能够贡献某种定性不同的能力，我们称之为校准的服从：识别自身工具或假设何时失败、相应调整策略、以及生成指导实验修订的机制性假设的能力。我们在一个闭环人机活动中测试了CLIO，旨在设计一种水性有机氧化还原液流电池（AORFB）负极液，CLIO与化学家紧密合作进行提案和解释，化学家们则负责合成、表征并在设计选择上权衡。在三轮共17个候选物中，CLIO收敛到一个顶级膦酸酯候选物；表征确认其氧化还原电位比文献基线提高了130毫伏。然而，表征随后揭示了出乎意料的差电化学可逆性——这是任何性质预测器都未标记的回归。CLIO生成了竞争性的机制性假设，优先考虑了区分性诊断，将失败追溯至膦酸酯-钾离子配对，并提出了磺酸酯替代物。所得化合物显示出显著改善的电化学可逆性，并保持了90毫伏的氧化还原电位提升，从而闭环了设计-制造-测试-重新设计循环。

Original abstract: We present Cognitive Loop via In-Situ Optimization (CLIO), an agent that couples a continuously-updated belief-state graph with a recursive plan-then-act loop. The result is a reasoning agent that can contribute something qualitatively different, which we term \emph{calibrated deference}: the capacity to recognize when its own tools or assumptions are failing, to adapt its strategy in response, and to generate mechanistic hypotheses that guide experimental revision. We tested CLIO in a closed-loop human-AI campaign to design an aqueous organic redox flow battery (AORFB) negolyte, with CLIO leading proposal and interpretation in close partnership with chemists who synthesized, characterized, and weighed in on design choices. Across 17 candidates over three rounds, CLIO converged on a top phosphonate candidate; characterization confirmed a 130~mV improvement in redox potential over the literature baseline. Characterization then revealed unexpectedly poor electrochemical reversibility -- a regression no property predictor had flagged. CLIO generated competing mechanistic hypotheses, prioritized discriminating diagnostics, traced the failure to phosphonate-potassium ion pairing, and prescribed a sulfonate replacement. The resulting compound showed substantially improved electrochemical reversibility and maintained a 90~mV improvement in redox potential, closing the design-make-test-redesign loop.

</details>

# cs.IR [[Back]](#toc)

### [136] [Do Agents Need Semantic Metadata? A Comparative Study in Agentic Data Retrieval](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28787v1)
*Shiyu Chen,Tarfah Alrashed,Alon Halevy,Natasha Noy*

Main category: cs.IR

Selection reason: agent检索中语义元数据对比研究，指导agent数据发现设计。

TL;DR: 语义元数据对智能体数据发现至关重要：语义智能体在检索可操作数据方面精确率显著高于基础智能体（整体精确率高65.7%），尽管基础智能体覆盖率更高。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究在LLM时代，语义元数据（如schema.org）对于智能体数据发现是否仍然必要，还是智能体可以直接从非结构化网络中检索可操作数据。

Method: 对比分析两种智能体：基础智能体搜索开放网络文档，语义智能体利用schema.org标注的9000万数据集。使用LLM-as-a-judge评估流水线，基于FAIR原则评估语义相关性、数据可访问性和计算实用性。

Result: 语义智能体在数据集检索精确率上显著优势：元数据注册表精确率高44.9%，机器可读下载精确率高46.6%，整体FAIR合规数据精确率高65.7%。基础智能体覆盖率更高（多回答40%问题），但常返回散文页面（20.1%）和门户页面（8.5%）。

Conclusion: 非结构化检索适合广泛探索，但结构化语义生态系统是可靠、执行导向的自主工作流不可或缺的基础。

中文摘要：在自主智能体时代，机器可操作数据对于数据驱动的工作流至关重要。十多年来，像schema.org这样的语义元数据锚定了FAIR原则（可发现、可访问、可互操作、可重用），支持机器可操作数据，并实现了诸如Google Dataset Search之类的发现工具。然而，能够导航非结构化网络的大型语言模型（LLM）的兴起引发了一个基本问题：语义元数据对于智能体数据发现是否仍然必要，还是智能体可以直接从网络中可靠地检索可操作数据？我们提出了一个跨两个不同环境的智能体数据检索对比分析：一个基础智能体搜索数十亿个开放网络文档，以及一个语义智能体利用基于schema.org的9000万数据集的语料库。我们部署了一个“LLM作为评判者”评估流水线，直接映射到FAIR原则，以评估检索数据的语义相关性、数据可访问性和计算实用性。我们的结果显示了一个明显的分歧。语义智能体在检索可操作数据方面表现出色，在其返回结果中，对于元数据丰富的注册表，精确率提高了44.9%；对于具有机器可读下载的页面，精确率提高了46.6%。相反，基础智能体经常遭受“最后一英里效用”失败，检索到散文密集型页面（占结果的20.1%）和门户登录页面（8.5%），而不是实际的数据页面。虽然基础智能体通过回答多40%的问题实现了更高的覆盖率，但语义智能体提供了更高的准确性，在检索符合FAIR原则的数据集方面，整体精确率提高了65.7%。我们得出结论，尽管非结构化检索支持广泛的探索性任务，但结构化生态系统仍然是可靠的、面向执行的自主工作流不可或缺的基础。

Original abstract: In the era of autonomous agents, machine-actionable data is critical for data-driven workflows. For more than a decade, semantic metadata like schema.org has anchored the FAIR principles (Findable, Accessible, Interoperable, and Reusable) for machine-actionable data and enabled discovery tools like Google Dataset Search. However, the rise of Large Language Models (LLMs) capable of navigating the unstructured web raises a fundamental question: Is semantic metadata still necessary for agentic data discovery, or can agents reliably retrieve actionable data directly from the web? We present a comparative analysis of agentic data retrieval across two distinct environments: a Baseline Agent searching billions of open-web documents, and a Semantic Agent leveraging a corpus of 90 million datasets using schema.org. We deploy an "LLM-as-a-judge" evaluation pipeline, mapped directly to the FAIR principles, to assess the semantic relevance, data accessibility, and computational utility of the retrieved data. Our results reveal a clear divergence. The Semantic Agent excels at retrieving actionable data, achieving a 44.9% higher precision for metadata-rich registries and a 46.6% higher precision for pages with machine-readable downloads among its returned results. Conversely, the Baseline Agent frequently suffers "Last-Mile Utility" failures, retrieving prose-heavy pages (20.1% of results) and portal landing pages (8.5%) rather than actual data pages. While the Baseline Agent achieves higher coverage by answering 40% more questions, the Semantic Agent delivers greater accuracy, achieving 65.7% higher overall precision in retrieving FAIR-compliant datasets. We conclude that while unstructured retrieval supports broad exploratory tasks, structured ecosystems remain the indispensable foundation for reliable, execution-oriented autonomous workflows.

</details>

# cs.PL [[Back]](#toc)

### [137] [FPMoE: A Sparse Mixture-of-Experts Approach to Functional Code Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27849v1)
*Loc Pham,Lang Hong Nguyet Anh,Thanh Le-Cong*

Main category: cs.PL

Selection reason: functional代码生成模型，虽偏模型架构，但属于coding agent范畴，可迁移至代码优化agent。

TL;DR: 提出FPMoE，基于稀疏MoE架构，通过语言专用专家和共享专家解决函数式编程语言代码生成中的干扰与抽象问题，仅3B激活参数即可匹配大模型性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM在函数式编程语言上表现不佳，且单一语言微调无法共享抽象，多语言微调存在干扰。

Method: 构建轻量级稀疏MoE代码生成模型FPMoE，包含Haskell、OCaml、Scala三个语言专用专家和一个共享专家，分别处理干扰和跨语言抽象。

Result: 在FPEval上显著优于微调基线，仅3B活跃参数即匹配DeepSeek-Coder-6.7B、Qwen2.5-Coder-14B-Instruct、Qwen3-Coder-30B-A3B等大模型性能。

Conclusion: 专用专家与共享专家结合的设计有效解决了干扰和抽象缺失问题，实现了轻量高效的高质量函数式代码生成。

中文摘要：尽管基于LLM的代码生成取得了快速进展，但现有模型主要针对命令式语言进行训练，导致函数式编程语言（FPLs）如Haskell、OCaml和Scala长期未被充分探索，即使是前沿模型在FPLs上的表现也明显较差。微调是一种自然的补救措施，但我们的实验表明，针对单一语言的微调无法捕捉共享的函数式抽象，而合并的多语言微调则引入了跨语言干扰。为了解决这一问题，我们提出了FPMoE，一个轻量级、开源的代码生成模型，基于稀疏混合专家（MoE）架构，包含三个特定于语言的专家（分别针对Haskell、OCaml和Scala）和一个共享专家，用于捕捉跨语言的函数式模式，如单子推理和类型导向编程。这种设计同时解决了两种失败模式：专用专家消除了干扰，而共享专家保留了单语言模型遗漏的抽象。在FPEval上，FPMoE显著优于微调基线，并且仅用3B激活参数就匹配了更大模型（包括DeepSeek-Coder-6.7B、Qwen2.5-Coder-14B-Instruct和Qwen3-Coder-30B-A3B）的性能。

Original abstract: Despite rapid progress in LLM-based code generation, existing models are predominantly trained on imperative languages, leaving functional programming languages (FPLs) such as Haskell, OCaml, and Scala chronically underexplored, with even frontier models performing substantially worse on FPLs. Fine-tuning is a natural remedy, but our experiments show that per-language fine-tuning fails to capture shared functional abstractions, while merged multi-language fine-tuning introduces cross-language interference. To address this, we introduce FPMoE, a lightweight, open-source code generation model built on a sparse Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) architecture with three language-specific routed experts (one each for Haskell, OCaml, and Scala) and a shared expert that captures cross-language functional patterns such as monadic reasoning and type-directed programming. This design resolves both failure modes simultaneously: dedicated experts eliminate interference, while the shared expert preserves abstractions that per-language models miss. On FPEval, FPMoE substantially outperforms fine-tuned baselines and, with only 3B active parameters, matches the performance of much larger models including DeepSeek-Coder-6.7B, Qwen2.5-Coder-14B-Instruct, and Qwen3-Coder-30B-A3B.

</details>
